### [32] [HPR-SAM: Hierarchical Probabilistic Representation Learning for Prompt-free SAM-based Medical Image Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06972)
*Yingzhen Hu,Yiheng Zhong,Keying Zhu,Zimu Zhang,Zihan Ye,Sifan Song,Jionglong Su,Xiaofeng Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出分层概率表示（HPR）框架，通过分布解剖表示、多组件解剖表示和局部可靠性表示学习互补解剖表征，并利用分层预测融合进行无提示医学图像分割，在Synapse、LA和PROMISE12数据集上取得最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SAM无提示适应方法主要关注提示生成，忽略了提示质量受限于解剖表示的表达能力，而确定性原型或语义标记难以同时捕捉全局解剖先验、结构内多样性和局部结构可靠性。

Method: 提出HPR框架，包含三个互补模块：分布解剖表示（DAR）建模全局解剖先验、多组件解剖表示（MAR）捕捉结构内多样性、局部可靠性表示（LRR）衡量局部结构可靠性；通过分层预测融合（HPF）集成各模块预测，保持与原始SAM解码器兼容。

Result: 在Synapse数据集上达到SOTA性能，在LA和PROMISE12数据集上取得少样本设置下的最佳性能。

Conclusion: 验证了分层概率表示学习框架在无提示医学图像分割中的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像分割同样存在地物类别多样性、边界模糊性和类内异质性等问题，可将HPR框架中的DAR用于建模地物全局分布先验，MAR用于处理同种地物（如不同季节的农田、不同朝向的建筑）的表征多样性，LRR用于评估分割结果的局部可靠性。HPF可用于融合多尺度遥感特征。此外，可引入遥感特有的地理空间先验信息增强DAR，并适配SAM的遥感预训练权重以提升分割精度。

Abstract (英文): Prompt-free adaptation of the Segment Anything Model (SAM) has emerged as a promising paradigm for automatic medical image segmentation. Existing methods mainly focus on prompt generation, while overlooking that prompt quality is fundamentally constrained by the expressiveness of anatomical representations. However, deterministic prototypes or semantic tokens are insufficient to jointly capture global anatomical priors, intra-structure diversity, and local structural reliability. To address this limitation, we propose the Hierarchical Probabilistic Representation (HPR) framework, which learns complementary anatomical representations through Distributional Anatomical Representation (DAR), Multi-component Anatomical Representation (MAR), and Local Reliability Representation (LRR), and integrates their predictions via Hierarchical Prediction Fusion (HPF) while remaining compatible with the original SAM decoder. Experiments on the Synapse, LA, and PROMISE12 datasets demonstrate that HPR-SAM achieves state-of-the-art performance on Synapse and the best performance under few-shot settings on LA and PROMISE12, validating the effectiveness of the proposed hierarchical probabilistic representation learning framework for prompt-free medical image segmentation. Code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/HPR-SAM-E4AF.

### [33] [EdgeCompress: Coupling Multidimensional Model Compression and Dynamic Inference for EdgeAI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06982)
*Hao Kong,Di Liu,Shuo Huai,Xiangzhong Luo,Ravi Subramaniam,Christian Makaya,Qian Lin,Weichen Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: EdgeCompress是一个面向资源受限嵌入式设备的CNN压缩框架，通过动态图像裁剪(DIC)和复合收缩(CS)从输入图像和网络架构两个维度减少计算冗余，并进一步引入动态推理机制处理不同难度的输入图像。在ImageNet-1K上，该方法使ResNet-50计算量减少48.8%的同时准确率提升0.8%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CNN在图像分类任务中表现优异，但其高昂的计算成本阻碍了在资源受限的嵌入式设备上的部署。

Method: 提出EdgeCompress框架，包含三个关键组件：(1) 动态图像裁剪(DIC)：设计轻量级前景预测器，精准裁剪输入图像中最具信息量的前景目标进行推理，避免背景区域冗余计算；(2) 复合收缩(CS)：根据对精度和模型计算量的贡献，协同压缩CNN的三个维度（深度、宽度和分辨率）；(3) 动态推理框架：级联多个不同复杂度的模型，针对不同识别难度的输入图像动态选择相应模型。

Result: 在ImageNet-1K上，EdgeCompress使ResNet-50计算量减少48.8%，同时top-1准确率提升0.8%；与最先进的压缩框架HRank相比，在相近计算量下准确率提升4.1%。

Conclusion: EdgeCompress通过图像级和架构级的双重冗余压缩策略，有效提升了CNN的推理效率，促进了先进CNN在嵌入式硬件上的部署。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：(1) 遥感图像往往包含大量背景区域（如海洋、沙漠），DIC的前景预测器可针对遥感目标（如舰船、飞机、建筑物）进行微调，减少背景冗余计算；(2) CS可针对遥感CNN模型（如遥感目标检测网络）的三维结构进行联合优化，尤其在高分辨率遥感影像处理中效果显著；(3) 遥感图像的识别难度差异大（如不同地物类型的区分难度不同），动态推理框架可根据图像复杂度自适应选择模型，平衡精度与效率；(4) 可进一步将DIC与遥感中的感兴趣区域(ROI)提取技术结合，提升前景预测的准确性。

Abstract (英文): Convolutional neural networks (CNNs) have demonstrated encouraging results in image classification tasks. However, the prohibitive computational cost of CNNs hinders the deployment of CNNs onto resource-constrained embedded devices. To address this issue, we propose EdgeCompress, a comprehensive compression framework to reduce the computational overhead of CNNs. In EdgeCompress, we first introduce dynamic image cropping (DIC), where we design a lightweight foreground predictor to accurately crop the most informative foreground object of input images for inference, which avoids redundant computation on background regions. Subsequently, we present compound shrinking (CS) to collaboratively compress the three dimensions (depth, width, and resolution) of CNNs according to their contribution to accuracy and model computation. DIC and CS together constitute a multidimensional CNN compression framework, which is able to comprehensively reduce the computational redundancy in both input images and neural network architectures, thereby improving the inference efficiency of CNNs. Further, we present a dynamic inference framework to efficiently process input images with different recognition difficulties, where we cascade multiple models with different complexities from our compression framework and dynamically adopt different models for different input images, which further compresses the computational redundancy and improves the inference efficiency of CNNs, facilitating the deployment of advanced CNNs onto embedded hardware. Experiments on ImageNet-1K demonstrate that EdgeCompress reduces the computation of ResNet-50 by 48.8% while improving the top-1 accuracy by 0.8%. Meanwhile, we improve the accuracy by 4.1% with similar computation compared to HRank, the state-of-the-art compression framework. The source code and models are available at https://github.com/ntuliuteam/edge-compress

### [34] [Ego-Human Motion Prediction with 3D-Aware LLM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07001)
*Yujin Bae,Jaewoo Jeong,Hyeonseong Kim,Kuk-Jin Yoon*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Ego3DLM提出了一种基于3D场景感知和跨模态联合预测的自我中心视角人体运动预测方法，通过三阶段训练（场景预训练、统一指令微调、强化学习微调）同时预测过去/未来的姿态与描述，在Nymeria基准上达到SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自我中心运动预测方法忽略了3D空间和语义上下文，且将姿态预测与语言描述作为分离的推理流处理，导致预测结果缺乏物理合理性和语义一致性。

Method: (1) 以3D场景特征、自我中心视频和三点点跟踪为输入；(2) 使用单自回归解码器同时输出过去姿态、未来姿态、过去描述和未来描述；(3) 三阶段训练：空间-语义场景感知预训练→全输出统一指令微调→GRPO强化学习微调（含模态内和跨模态奖励）。

Result: 在Nymeria基准上，在未来运动预测、过去运动跟踪和运动描述任务中均取得最先进性能。

Conclusion: 3D场景感知和跨模态联合预测能够生成物理合理且语义一致的运动预测，验证了姿态与语言统一预测的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。遥感中的目标运动预测（如车辆轨迹、舰船航迹）可借鉴Ego3DLM的三个核心思路：(1) 引入3D地理空间特征（DSM、点云）替代原文的3D场景特征，增强运动预测的几何约束；(2) 将遥感目标的位置/速度序列（姿态）与其语义标签（如"转弯""减速"等描述）进行跨模态联合预测，而非分开处理；(3) 采用三阶段训练策略，特别是引入GRPO强化学习优化轨迹预测的物理合理性（如避免撞岛、遵循航道）。不足之处在于遥感缺乏自我中心视频输入，需调整为卫星/无人机视角下的全局观测。

Abstract (英文): Anticipating human motion from an egocentric perspective is fundamental for proactive assistance in AR/VR, human-robot collaboration, and embodied AI. While recent works incorporate language as a semantic prior to reduce the ill-posed nature of egocentric forecasting, they largely neglect the 3D spatial and semantic context that governs how motion unfolds, and treat pose and language prediction as separate inference streams. We introduce Ego3DLM, built on two core principles: accurate motion forecasting requires explicit spatial and semantic understanding of the 3D environment, and pose and language must be predicted holistically in a single pass, since motion is inherently tied to the semantic interpretation of actions being performed. Given three-point tracking, 3D scene features, and egocentric video, Ego3DLM simultaneously decodes past pose, future pose, past narration, and future narration in a single autoregressive pass, grounding predicted poses and descriptions in one another to enforce cross-modal and temporal consistency. We adopt a three-stage training scheme: (1) spatial-semantic scene awareness pretraining; (2) holistic instruction tuning over all four outputs in a single pass; and (3) GRPO-based reinforcement finetuning with intra- and inter-modal rewards that directly optimize pose-language fidelity. Experiments on the Nymeria benchmark demonstrate that Ego3DLM achieves state-of-the-art performance across future motion prediction, past motion tracking, and motion description, showing that 3D scene grounding and holistic cross-modal prediction yield physically plausible and semantically coherent motion forecasts. The project page is available at https://jaewoo97.github.io/Ego3DLM/.

### [35] [SHTA: Semantic Hard Token Correction and Center Alignment for Semi-Supervised Medical Image Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07019)
*Zhuoru Zhang,Yiheng Zhong,Zimu Zhang,Xiaofeng Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SHTA（语义硬令牌修正与中心对齐），一种轻量级训练时语义表示分支，通过语义分配、硬令牌精炼和语义中心对齐来改进困难区域的语义一致性，无需额外推理成本，在多个半监督医学图像分割框架上取得一致提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有半监督医学图像分割方法主要优化预测层面的监督质量（如一致性正则化、伪标签监督），但未能显式强制困难区域学习到的表示在语义上保持一致，导致不稳定语义分配的困难区域在训练中无法建立语义一致的表示，限制了分割性能的进一步提升。

Method: 提出SHTA，包含三个核心模块：1) 语义分配（Semantic Assignment）：将特征token映射到语义空间；2) 硬令牌精炼（Hard Token Refinement）：识别并修正语义不稳定的硬令牌；3) 语义中心对齐（Semantic Center Alignment）：对齐不同视图/增强下同一语义类别的中心表示。该方法作为轻量级训练时分支，不改变原始预测路径，无额外推理开销。

Result: 在Synapse和AMOS数据集上，将SHTA集成到GA-CPS、CPS、URPC和MagicNet四种代表性半监督分割框架中，均取得一致的性能提升，尤其在分割精度、弱器官恢复和语义模糊减少方面增益明显。

Conclusion: SHTA通过训练时显式优化困难区域的语义表示一致性，有效弥补了现有方法在表示层面监督的不足，是一种轻量级、即插即用的通用改进方案，且仅增加训练开销、不增加推理负担。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：1) 遥感图像中地物边界模糊、阴影遮挡等困难区域同样存在语义分配不稳定问题，SHTA可直接迁移至半监督遥感图像分割框架（如半监督语义分割中的跨视图一致性方法）；2) 遥感多时相/多模态数据中同一地物在不同成像条件下的语义漂移问题，可通过SHTA的语义中心对齐机制进行修正；3) 将硬令牌精炼模块适配到遥感目标检测任务中，用于改进边界框附近的前景-背景模糊区域的特征表示。

Abstract (英文): Recent advances in semi-supervised medical image segmentation have achieved remarkable performance through prediction consistency, pseudo-label supervision, and hard-region supervision. However, these methods primarily improve supervision quality rather than explicitly enforcing semantic consistency in the learned representations of hard regions. Consequently, even under increasingly stronger prediction-level supervision, difficult regions exhibiting unstable semantic assignment often fail to establish semantically consistent representations during training, thereby limiting further segmentation improvement. To address this issue, we propose SHTA (Semantic Hard Token Correction and Center Alignment), a lightweight training-time semantic representation branch. Instead of introducing additional prediction supervision, SHTA refines intermediate semantic representations through Semantic Assignment, Hard Token Refinement, and Semantic Center Alignment, thereby improving semantic consistency in hard regions while preserving the original prediction pathway and introducing no additional inference cost. We integrate SHTA into representative semi-supervised segmentation frameworks, including GA-CPS, CPS, URPC, and MagicNet, and conduct evaluations on the Synapse and AMOS datasets. Experimental results demonstrate that SHTA delivers consistent paired improvements across frameworks, with especially clear gains in segmentation accuracy, weak-organ recovery, and semantic ambiguity reduction, while incurring only training-time overhead. The code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/release_SHTA-42D5/.

</details>


### [36] [AnchorPrune: Relevance-Anchored Contextual Expansion for Visual Token Pruning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07033)
*Kyuan Oh,Bumsoo Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AnchorPrune是一种无需训练的视觉token剪枝框架，通过构建受保护的相关性锚点并扩展互补视觉上下文，在保持查询关键证据的同时恢复信息性非冗余上下文，有效提升了视觉语言模型的推理效率与精度的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大视觉语言模型因高分辨率输入产生大量视觉token，其中许多对给定查询是冗余的，导致高昂推理成本。现有剪枝方法中，相关性驱动与多样性驱动目标在激进压缩下存在冲突：相关性选择导致预算过度集中于相关局部证据，而多样性选择可能抑制不可或缺的token或保留无信息区域。

Method: 提出AnchorPrune，一个无训练框架。首先构建受保护的相关性锚点（relevance anchor），通过相关性排序token的新颖性轮廓自适应确定锚点大小，保留查询关键证据；然后将剩余预算通过重要性加权新颖性（importance-weighted novelty）分配，扩展互补视觉上下文，防止上下文扩展取代关键查询线索，同时改善视觉覆盖。

Result: 在图像和视频视觉语言模型及基准测试中，AnchorPrune持续优于无训练基线方法，尤其在高度压缩下表现突出。在LLaVA-NeXT-7B上，仅用160个（共2,880个）视觉token即保留了97.6%的全token性能。

Conclusion: 相关性锚定的上下文扩展是实现高效多模态推理的有效原则。AnchorPrune轻量级、架构感知，无需重训练或模型修改。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感影像通常具有高分辨率、大尺度、多通道的特点，视觉token数量庞大。可将AnchorPrune应用于遥感视觉问答（RSVQA）和遥感图像描述等任务中，以剪枝冗余的遥感图像块token。具体方案：1) 将遥感影像分割为局部图块作为视觉token，利用AnchorPrune保留与地理查询（如"该区域建筑密度如何"）相关的关键图块；2) 针对遥感中多尺度特征，可将锚点构建与尺度感知策略结合，优先保留包含地物变化或目标区域的token；3) 在遥感多模态检索任务中，利用重要性加权新颖性扩展覆盖不同地物类别，提升检索覆盖率。

Abstract (英文): Large vision-language models incur substantial inference costs because high-resolution inputs introduce thousands of visual tokens, many of which are redundant for a given query. Existing pruning methods often combine query relevance and token diversity, yet these objectives can conflict under aggressive compression: relevance-driven selection may overconcentrate the budget on correlated local evidence, while diversity-driven selection may suppress indispensable tokens or retain distinct but uninformative regions. We introduce AnchorPrune, a training-free framework that first constructs a protected relevance anchor and then expands it with complementary visual context. AnchorPrune adaptively determines the anchor size from the novelty profile of relevance-ranked tokens, preserving a compact set of query-critical evidence, and allocates the remaining budget through importance-weighted novelty to recover informative, non-redundant context relative to the anchor. This ordered design prevents contextual expansion from displacing indispensable query cues while improving overall visual coverage. AnchorPrune is lightweight, architecture-aware, and requires neither retraining nor model modification. Across image and video vision-language models and benchmarks, it consistently improves the accuracy-efficiency trade-off over training-free baselines, particularly under severe compression. On LLaVA-NeXT-7B, AnchorPrune preserves 97.6% of full-token performance using only 160 of 2,880 visual tokens. These results establish relevance-anchored contextual expansion as an effective principle for efficient multimodal inference. Code is available at https://github.com/MULTI-cau/AnchorPrune.

</details>


### [37] [TRACE-Seg3D: Counterfactual Context Auditing For Robust 3D Glioma Segmentation Under Institutional Shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07038)
*Nguyen Linh Dan Le,Nguyen Pham Hoang Le,Tran Dang Khoi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: TRACE-Seg3D是一个反事实上下文审计框架，用于鲁棒的3D医学图像分割。该框架通过保留病灶相关证据并系统性地改变成像上下文，量化模型在可控上下文偏移下的预测稳定性，提供逐案例的敏感性评估。在BraTS和UTSW胶质瘤分割基准上展示了竞争性的分布内和跨域性能，揭示了传统指标无法发现的上下文敏感失败模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有医学图像分割模型在基准测试中表现良好，但对扫描仪、协议和研究机构等上下文偏移敏感，而Dice和HD95等传统指标无法暴露这些由 nuisance 线索引起的不稳定性。

Method: 提出TRACE-Seg3D反事实上下文审计框架：保留病灶相关证据，系统性地变化成像上下文，量化可控上下文偏移下的预测稳定性；为每个分割结果配对审计证据，评估上下文敏感性和解剖学合理性。

Result: 在BraTS和UTSW胶质瘤分割基准上实现了竞争性的分布内和跨域性能，并成功暴露了传统指标无法检测的上下文敏感失败模式。

Conclusion: 反事实上下文审计是实现分布偏移下透明可靠3D医学图像分割的实用途径。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。1）遥感图像存在传感器、季节、光照等域偏移问题，可将反事实上下文审计框架直接迁移至遥感图像分割任务，量化模型对传感器类型、分辨率、云覆盖等上下文变化的鲁棒性。2）可借鉴其逐案例可靠性评估思路，为遥感分割结果提供可信度指标，辅助决策。3）需注意遥感图像空间尺度更大、地物类别更丰富，反事实生成策略需适配遥感场景中的语义上下文（如植被、水体、建筑等）变化。

Abstract (英文): Medical image segmentation models can achieve strong benchmark performance while remaining sensitive to scanner, protocol, and institutional variation. These context shifts alter image appearance without changing the underlying lesion, allowing models to exploit nuisance cues that Dice and HD95 fail to expose. We present TRACE-Seg3D, a counterfactual context auditing framework for robust 3D medical image segmentation. TRACE-Seg3D preserves lesion-relevant evidence and systematically varies imaging context to quantify prediction stability under controlled context shifts. The framework pairs each segmentation with audit evidence for context sensitivity and anatomical plausibility, enabling case-level reliability assessment beyond overlap-based evaluation. Experiments on BraTS and UTSW glioma segmentation benchmarks demonstrate competitive in-distribution and cross-domain performance. TRACE-Seg3D also exposes context-sensitive failure modes missed by conventional metrics. These results establish counterfactual context auditing as a practical route toward transparent and reliable 3D medical image segmentation under distribution shift. Our code is available at https://github.com/danleneurocom/Counterfactual-Representation-Network.

</details>


### [38] [Making Implicit Preservation Intent Explicit in Conversational Image Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07051)
*Soomin Han,Jihyung Ahn,Bumsoo Kim,Buru Chang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出OCCUR-Bench基准和ReSpec框架，用于评估和提升对话式图像编辑中跨轮次的时序内容保持，解决被遮挡但未改变内容无法恢复的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对话式图像编辑系统在跨轮次编辑中，当新增内容遮挡先前可见区域时，无法恢复这些被遮挡但语义未改变的内容，导致结果不一致或出现幻觉。作者旨在填补这一评估空白并提出解决方案。

Method: 1）OCCUR-Bench：构建包含遮挡-揭示场景的诊断基准，提供历史恢复参考用于评估忠实恢复而非合理生成。2）ReSpec：无训练框架，通过三个步骤实现隐式保持显式化——识别应持久化的内容、选择提供缺失视觉证据的历史图像状态、将生成的恢复感知指令与历史视觉参考输入上下文编辑器。

Result: 在OCCUR-Bench上的实验表明，ReSpec相比现有方法在恢复保真度和时序一致性上有显著提升。

Conclusion: 对话式图像编辑中的内容保持应基于编辑历史进行显式引导，而非仅依赖当前图像状态。OCCUR-Bench可作为该任务的标准评估工具。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。本工作的时序内容保持机制可直接迁移到遥感时序图像编辑场景。例如，多时相遥感影像中新增建筑/云层遮挡了历史地物，可利用ReSpec框架：1）识别需保持的历史地物（如植被、道路）；2）从历史时相中提取被遮挡区域的视觉证据；3）生成恢复感知指令指导编辑。此外，OCCUR-Bench的评估范式可改造为遥感时序一致性评测基准，评估模型在时序遥感图像编辑中是否忠实恢复被遮挡但未变化的地物信息。

Abstract (英文): Conversational image editing requires preserving not only visible content, but also content that temporarily disappears across turns. When newly added or modified content occludes a previously visible region, that region should reappear if it was never semantically changed. However, existing systems often fail to recover such occluded-but-unchanged content, producing inconsistent or hallucinated results. We introduce OCCUR-Bench, a diagnostic benchmark for temporal preservation in conversational image editing. OCCUR-Bench provides diverse occlusion-and-revelation scenarios with historical restoration references, enabling evaluation of faithful restoration rather than plausible regeneration. We also propose ReSpec, a training-free framework that makes implicit preservation explicit by pairing restoration-aware instructions with historical visual references. Given an editing history, ReSpec identifies what should persist, selects the historical image state that provides missing visual evidence, and conditions an in-context editor on the resulting instruction and reference image. Experiments show that ReSpec improves restoration fidelity and temporal consistency on OCCUR-Bench, highlighting the need to ground preservation in editing history rather than only the current image.

### [39] [Navigating Hierarchy: Hyperbolic Learning on Brain Graphs for Disorder Diagnosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07077)
*Yapeng Li,Bo Jiang,Ziyan Zhang,Dongdong Chen,Zhengzheng Tu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出HLBG框架，利用双曲几何建模脑网络中ROI、功能社区和全脑网络的层级结构，并引入GaMamba模型捕获长程依赖，在ABIDE-I和REST-MDD数据集上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有脑图建模方法难以建模ROI-社区间的交互，未能充分挖掘ROI、社区和全脑网络三个层级的层次结构信息。

Method: 1) 将ROI、社区和全脑网络的表征投影到洛伦兹双曲空间；2) 通过两种几何蕴含约束施加多层级层次结构；3) 提出Graph-aware Mamba模型，引入拓扑结构提示以捕获长程依赖同时保留图拓扑信息。

Result: 在ABIDE-I和REST-MDD数据集上，HLBG优于现有最先进方法，并能识别与疾病相关的功能性生物标志物。

Conclusion: 双曲空间能有效建模脑网络的固有层次几何结构，GaMamba可同时捕获长程依赖和拓扑信息，为脑网络分析提供了层次感知且判别性强的表征学习方法。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感中的地物（像素-地块-区域）天然具有层级结构，HLBG的双曲层级建模可直接迁移至遥感场景理解。具体方案：1) 将像素、地物斑块和遥感大场景分别映射为ROI、社区和全脑网络的角色，利用洛伦兹双曲空间建模三者层次关系；2) 将GaMamba中的拓扑结构提示替换为遥感空间邻接图（如超像素邻接图），用于捕获遥感图像中的长程空间依赖性；3) 双曲蕴含约束可施加不同尺度地物之间的包含关系（如建筑属于城市区域），提升多尺度遥感分类与分割性能。

Abstract (英文): Functional brain networks exhibit a hierarchical organization across ROI, community, and whole-brain levels, supporting local processing, inter-community coordination, and global integration. Recent studies have demonstrated that brain community-aware modeling is beneficial for both diagnosis and biomarker identification of brain networks. However, existing brain graph modeling methods often struggle to model ROI-community interactions, thereby failing to fully exploit the hierarchy across ROI, community, and whole-brain network levels. To address this issue, inspired by deep hyperbolic learning in modeling hierarchical structures, we propose a novel framework, termed Hyperbolic Learning on Brain Graphs (HLBG), for brain network analysis. The core idea of HLBG is to exploit the inherent hierarchical geometry of hyperbolic space to model the hierarchical relationships among ROIs, functional communities, and the whole-brain network, thereby learning hierarchy-aware and highly discriminative representations for brain network data. Specifically, HLBG first projects representations from ROIs, communities, and the whole-brain network into Lorentzian hyperbolic space. Then, the multi-level hierarchy is imposed via two geometric entailment constraints. In addition, we introduce a new Graph-aware Mamba (GaMamba) model, which incorporates topology-derived structural prompts into Mamba to capture long-range dependencies while preserving graph topological information. Experiments on ABIDE-I and REST-MDD demonstrate that HLBG outperforms state-of-the-art methods and identifies disorder-relevant functional biomarkers.

### [40] [AT-Attn: Temporal-Aware Cross-Attention for Longitudinal Multimodal Alzheimer's Disease Diagnosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07091)
*Xinyue Du,Yibo Liu,Zhenglei Zhou,Xuancheng Yao,Weimin Zhong,Qiuhui Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出AT-Attn，一种时序感知的多模态框架，通过变化-时间编码、时间偏置非对称交叉注意力和门控融合，在不规则随访中整合MRI与纵向临床信息，在ADNI队列中优于单模态和朴素融合基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纵向阿尔茨海默病诊断中，临床和影像数据常在不规则时间点采集，朴素融合在MRI存在噪声或间歇缺失时性能下降，需要时序感知的约束融合策略。

Method: AT-Attn框架包含三个核心组件：Change-and-Time编码（捕捉纵向变化和时间信息）、时间偏置非对称交叉注意力（处理模态间不规则时间对齐）、门控融合（控制MRI对最终决策的贡献）。

Result: 在1,520名患者的ADNI队列上，AT-Attn达到Accuracy 0.719±0.024、Macro F1 0.721±0.023、ROC-AUC 0.873±0.013、PR-AUC 0.783±0.018，优于单模态和朴素多模态融合基线。

Conclusion: 时序感知且受约束的融合策略有助于结构性MRI为患者层面的AD诊断提供临床相关的互补信息。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域同样存在时序多模态数据（如光学-SAR时序影像、地面观测数据）不规则采集的问题。具体方案：(1)将Change-and-Time编码迁移至遥感时序变化检测任务，编码不规则时间间隔的光学/SAR影像对；(2)时间偏置非对称交叉注意力可用于融合稀疏地面实测数据与密集遥感影像；(3)门控融合机制可自适应调节不同质量遥感模态（如有云遮蔽的光学影像）的贡献权重，提升时序分类和变化检测的鲁棒性。

Abstract (英文): In longitudinal Alzheimer's disease (AD) diagnosis support, clinical and imaging information is often collected at irregular visits. Integrating these multimodal observations may improve diagnostic assessment, but naive fusion can degrade performance when MRI is noisy or intermittently unavailable. We propose AT-Attn, a temporal-aware multimodal framework that combines Change-and-Time encoding, time-biased asymmetric cross-attention, and gated fusion to integrate MRI with longitudinal clinical information. We evaluate AT-Attn on an MRI-retained ADNI cohort of 1,520 patients using structural MRI, six cognitive-scale trajectories, and seven static clinical variables under patient-level five-fold cross-validation. The main asymmetric AT-Attn model achieves accuracy 0.719+/-0.024, macro F1 0.721+/-0.023, ROC-AUC 0.873+/-0.013, and PR-AUC 0.783+/-0.018, outperforming unimodal and naive multimodal fusion baselines while remaining competitive with strong tabular baselines. These results suggest that a temporal-aware and constrained fusion strategy can help structural MRI contribute clinically relevant complementary information for patient-level AD diagnosis support.

### [41] [Tree-of-Thoughts Reasoning for Text-to-Image In-Context Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07117)
*Stepanida Alekseeva,Jenifer Kalafatovich,Seong-Whan Lee*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种树状思维（ToT）推理框架用于文本到图像的情景学习（T2I-ICL），通过多阶段推理与选择层生成、评估并筛选多个候选解释，从而缓解提示歧义和组合错误，无需额外训练即可在CoBSAT基准上实现更一致、语义对齐的图像生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有最先进的多模态大语言模型在T2I-ICL任务中表现不佳，主要受限于组合推理能力不足以及对提示构建方式敏感，导致生成的图像与期望语义不一致。

Method: 提出树状思维（ToT）推理框架，包含多阶段推理与选择层：首先生成多个候选推理分支（假设），然后对每个分支进行评估，最后选择最连贯的解释用于构建最终图像合成提示，从而在推理阶段实现结构化多分支探索与择优。

Result: 在CoBSAT基准上的定性和定量结果表明，相比基线方法和思维链（Chain-of-Thought）提示策略，所提方法生成的图像更一致、语义对齐度更高，且无需任何额外训练或微调。

Conclusion: 结构化多分支推理能够有效缓解提示歧义和组合错误，提升T2I-ICL中图像生成的语义一致性，证明了无需训练即可通过推理优化改善多模态生成任务性能的可行性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：（1）遥感图斑生成：可应用ToT框架从少量遥感样本（如不同地物类型的纹理、形状组合）中推理出隐含的空间布局模式，生成更符合地理语义的遥感图像；（2）多源遥感提示融合：针对遥感中多模态数据（光谱、SAR、DEM）的少样本组合推理，利用ToT多分支探索最优模态组合与融合策略；（3）遥感变化检测中的情景生成：从少量变化示例中推理出变化模式，辅助生成变化后场景；（4）缓解遥感标注歧义：遥感图像中同类地物外观差异大，ToT可通过多假设推理与选择消除类别边界模糊性。

Abstract (英文): In text-to-image in-context learning (T2I-ICL), a model has to infer a latent compositional pattern from fewshot demonstrations for generating a query image. Recent studies show that state-of-the-art multimodal large language models struggle with this setting, particularly due to limited compositional reasoning and sensitivity to prompt construction. In this work, we propose a Tree-of-Thoughts (ToT) reasoning framework for T2I-ICL that introduces a multi-stage reasoning and selection layer that generates, evaluates, and selects among multiple candidate hypotheses before constructing the final prompt for image synthesis. By exploring alternative reasoning branches and selecting a coherent interpretation, the proposed approach mitigates prompt ambiguity and compositional errors. We implement the proposed approach in a complete ToT-T2IICL inference pipeline and evaluate it on the CoBSAT benchmark. Both qualitative and quantitative results show that structured multi-branch reasoning leads to more consistent and semantically aligned image generation compared to baseline and Chain-of-Thought prompting strategies, without any additional training or fine-tuning.

### [42] [Video-Based Detection of squint and cataract for accessibility-aware adaptive web interface rendering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07099)
*Amar Ranjan Dash,Manas Ranjan Patra*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于计算机视觉和实时视频的自动检测系统，利用MediaPipe面部网格（478点 landmarks）提取几何眼部特征进行斜视多分类，并通过灰度强度和直方图分析评估白内障的存在与严重程度。系统使用普通笔记本或手机摄像头即可部署，斜视检测准确率达98.39%，白内障分类准确率达96.90%。未来将集成到自适应用户界面和Web无障碍系统中，辅助视觉障碍人群。

Method: 采用MediaPipe Face Mesh（478点面部地标检测模型）提取眼部几何特征，实现多类斜视分类；同时通过灰度强度和基于直方图的晶状体不透明度分析来估计白内障的存在和严重程度。系统通过标准笔记本或手机摄像头录制短视频序列进行分析。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：65%。该文的核心技术（MediaPipe面部网格特征提取、灰度强度与直方图分析）属于通用计算机视觉方法，可迁移至遥感领域中的人脸/眼部区域分析任务。具体方案：(1) 将面部地标检测模型迁移至遥感影像中的人脸检测与眼部区域定位，用于灾后或特殊场景下的视觉状态监测；(2) 灰度强度与直方图分析方法可用于遥感影像中目标区域的纹理与不透明度分析，如云层遮挡检测、水体浑浊度评估等。但遥感影像通常空间分辨率较低、视角非正面，需额外进行视角校正和数据增强处理。

Abstract (英文): Squint and cataract are major ocular disorders that majorly affect visual perception and interaction capability. This paper proposes a real-time video-based automated detection system for squint and cataract detection based on computer vision and image processing methods. The proposed system uses a media-pipe face-mesh (a 478-point facial landmark detection model) to extract geometric ocular features for multi-class squint classification. Simultaneously, The presence and severity cataract is estimated through grayscale intensity and histogram-based lens opacity analysis. The system records short video sequences with standard laptop or mobile cameras, which can be deployed at low costs and on a large scale. The experimental performance has shown great accuracy in the detection of squint (98.39%) and classification of cataract (96.90%). Besides automatic ocular analysis, the proposed framework is also made accessible for visual impairment inference which will be integrated with future adaptive user interface and Web accessibility systems for people with visual impairment.

### [43] [Vision Foundation Models in Radiology: A Scoping Review of Data, Methodology, Evaluation and Clinical Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07219)

Abstract (英文): Vision foundation models (VFMs) are increasingly being developed for radiological imaging, yet their definition, development and evaluation remain heterogeneous. We conducted a PRISMAScR scoping review of peer-reviewed studies published between January 2017 and March 2026 describing foundation models trained exclusively on radiological imaging data. Sixty-seven studies were included and mapped across three pillars: data scale and heterogeneity, architectural and pretraining scalability, and downstream transferability and generalization. Datasets primarily covered brain MRI, thoracoabdominal CT, and chest X-ray, ranging from fewer than 100,000 samples to multi-million-image cohorts. Transformer-based architectures and self-supervised pretraining predominated, particularly masked image modeling, contrastive learning and multi-stage approaches. Evaluation focused mainly on segmentation and classification, whereas cross-center, cross-scanner, anatomical and modality-shift validation was inconsistently reported. Alignment with FUTURE-AI principles was uneven. Overall, radiology-specific VFMs show promising transferability, but clinical translation remains constrained by limited data representativeness, heterogeneous benchmarks, incomplete reporting and insufficient deployment-oriented evaluation.

### [44] [CarbonCLIP: Enhance Carbon Prediction from Satellite Imagery via Integrated Street-View Semantics and Temporal Context Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07292)
*Zeru Yang,Fang-Ying Gong,Steve H. L. Yim,Chau Yuen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CarbonCLIP提出了一种面向任务的多模态知识蒸馏框架，通过双分支对比学习将街景图像中提取的语义先验（空间分支）和月份时序先验（时间分支）融入卫星影像表征，从而在不依赖地面数据推理的情况下提升城市碳排放预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用双分支对比学习框架：空间分支利用大语言模型（LMMs）从街景图像自动生成细粒度文本描述，提供建筑功能、基础设施和城市活动等语义先验；时间分支通过月份编码器编码与月度排放变化相关的时序先验。多模态数据仅用于预训练，推理时仅需卫星图像。

Abstract (英文): Accurately estimating urban carbon emissions is critical for sustainable urban planning, yet many existing approaches remain difficult to apply consistently across cities due to data-source heterogeneity and the lack of fine-grained semantic-temporal context in remote sensing data. We propose CarbonCLIP, a task-oriented multimodal distillation framework that improves satellite-based carbon emission prediction by transferring contextual knowledge into a unified satellite representation through dual-branch contrastive learning. Unlike conventional methods that rely on static visual features, CarbonCLIP explicitly bridges the gap between top-down satellite views and ground-level human activities. Specifically, the spatial branch uses fine-grained textual descriptions automatically generated from street-view images by Large Multimodal Models (LMMs) to provide semantic priors reflecting building functions, infrastructure, and urban activities, while the temporal branch employs a month encoder to encode temporal priors associated with monthly emission variation. CarbonCLIP requires multimodal data only during the pretraining phase; during inference, it relies solely on satellite imagery, thereby supporting scalable deployment when ground-level data are unavailable at inference. Experiments on Beijing and Singapore demonstrate that CarbonCLIP outperforms baselines in both study cities. The results validate that our method effectively transfers multimodal knowledge into satellite representations, offering a robust solution for satellite-based urban carbon modeling.

### [45] [ColorFM: An Optimization-to-Learning Framework for Color Transfer via Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07119)
*Yuhang He,Kai Zhang,Xiaoming Li,Du Chen,Jian Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出ColorFM框架，将颜色迁移问题重构为沿速度场的像素分布传输（Flow Matching），通过优化（ColorFM-O）生成伪监督数据训练前馈模型（ColorFM-L），在保持语义一致性的同时实现高质量、高效的颜色迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有颜色迁移方法存在全局映射不准确、语义错位和视觉伪影等问题，需要一种既能保证精度又具备高效推理能力的解决方案。

Method: 将颜色迁移视为基于Flow Matching的像素分布传输问题；提出ColorFM-O通过语义先验引导的分层颜色耦合拟合速度场，数值积分生成高质量伪监督数据；ColorFM-L通过隐式状态建模提取深层语义特征，预测双向线性化传输的流参数进行前馈推理。

Result: ColorFM-L在视觉质量、结构保真度和语义一致性上均优于现有最先进方法，成功兼顾了优化的精度与前馈推理的速度。

Conclusion: ColorFM框架通过连接离线优化与在线推理，为颜色迁移任务提供了一种精度高、速度快且语义一致的有效解决方案。

Abstract (英文): Color transfer aims to align the color distribution of a source image with that of a reference image while preserving structural and semantic consistency. However, existing methods often suffer from inaccurate global mapping, semantic misalignment, and visual artifacts. To address these issues, we propose ColorFM, an optimization-to-learning framework. ColorFM connects online optimization to offline inference by reformulating color transfer as the transport of pixel distributions along velocity fields via Flow Matching. Specifically, we introduce ColorFM-O, an instance-specific optimization scheme that fits the velocity field through hierarchical color coupling guided by semantic priors. By numerically integrating the induced flow trajectories, ColorFM-O produces precise and semantically consistent color transfer results, while generating high-quality paired data as pseudo-supervision. Building upon this, we design ColorFM-L, an efficient feed-forward model trained on the generated pairs. Through implicit state modeling, ColorFM-L extracts deep semantic features to predict flow parameters for bidirectional linearized transport, ensuring accurate color transfer. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ColorFM-L outperforms state-of-the-art methods in visual quality, structural fidelity, and semantic consistency, successfully combining the accuracy of optimization with the speed of feed-forward inference.

### [46] [HAJJv2-CrowdCount: Zero-Shot Benchmark for Dense Crowd Counting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07322)
*Reem AlYabis,Fares AlTuwaim,AlJawharh AlOtaibi,Mohamed Eltahir*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 构建HAJJv2-CrowdCount逐秒人工标注数据集；2) 基准测试三种零样本范式：开放词汇检测器（YOLO-World）、基于点的计数器（APGCC）、可提示分割计数器（SAM3Count）；3) 按帧密度分层分析性能差异。

Result: SAM3Count整体MAE最低（70.4），YOLO-World次之（92.0），APGCC最差（152.9）。但在最密集帧中，检测和分割方法MAE超300，而APGCC仅114.9，表现更优。

Conclusion: 密集场景下不同计数范式的性能顺序发生反转，基于点的方法在高密度高遮挡环境下更具鲁棒性，这对实际Hajj人群管理决策至关重要。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感影像中的人群计数（如朝觐、大型集会监测）同样面临陡峭视角、严重遮挡和极高密度问题。可直接借鉴本文方法：1) 采用逐秒精细标注策略构建遥感人群计数基准数据集；2) 基准测试零样本范式，特别是点基计数方法在密集遥感场景中的优势；3) 针对遥感影像中更复杂的尺度变化和视角多样性，可进一步改进点基计数器的密度图生成机制。

Abstract (英文): Automated crowd counting in Hajj video is difficult not because current models lack capacity, but because the footage violates the assumptions those models were built on: cameras observe the crowd from steep, near-vertical angles, individuals occlude one another extensively, and a single frame can contain well over a thousand people. Benchmarks that test crowd counting in such an environment are either private or not detailed per second. We revisit the HAJJv2 dataset and contribute HAJJv2-CrowdCount: per-second human-annotated crowd counts for its testing videos. Using these annotations, we benchmark three recent zero-shot counting paradigms: an open-vocabulary detector (YOLO-World), a point-based counter (APGCC), and a promptable segmentation-based counter (SAM3Count). SAM3Count attains the lowest overall mean absolute error (MAE 70.4, 95% CI 56.0-86.1), ahead of YOLO-World (92.0) and APGCC (152.9). This ordering reverses, however, in the regime most relevant to deployment: on the densest frames, the detection- and segmentation-based counters both degrade sharply (MAE exceeding 300), while the point-based counter degrades far more gracefully (MAE 114.9). This inversion is decision-relevant for Hajj crowd management, where reliable counts are needed most precisely in the densest and most occluded scenes. The annotations are released to support reproduction and extension of these results.

### [47] [Widest-Path Reachability Fields for Connectivity-Preserving Slender Structure Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07123)
*Youcheng Zong,Runda Jia,Minxuan Hu,Weilan Su,Dakuo He*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 针对细长曲线结构分割中拓扑连接性断裂的问题，本文揭示了拓扑梯度饥饿(TGS)现象，即像素级损失函数均匀分配梯度导致瓶颈像素梯度贡献被淹没。提出可微最大-最小可达性场(WPRF)，通过动态规划实现瓶颈感知梯度重路由，在无推理开销下显著提升拓扑完整性，并在九种架构和六个数据集上验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准二值掩码监督下，基于像素级重叠优化的模型频繁产生拓扑断裂预测。根本原因在于像素级损失均匀分配梯度，而连接性依赖于稀疏的瓶颈像素，这些像素被厚结构和背景大量淹没，导致聚合梯度贡献可忽略不计。作者将这种现象命名为拓扑梯度饥饿(TGS)。

Method: 提出Widest-Path Reachability Fields (WPRF)，一种可微的最大-最小(Max-Min)可达性目标函数。核心机制包括：(1) 在域限制图上通过动态规划实现可微Max-Min优化；(2) 瓶颈感知的观测项平衡不同结构间的梯度贡献；(3) 即插即用、与骨干网络无关、无推理开销。与依赖后验骨架化或同调计算的拓扑感知损失不同，WPRF通过可微Max-Min代数直接端到端优化可达性。

Result: 在九种架构和六个数据集上验证，WPRF在固定超参数下改进了87%的实验，在结构脆弱的数据集上clDice提升7.2个百分点。同时发布了口腔微血管分割数据集OMVIS。

Conclusion: WPRF通过瓶颈聚焦梯度路由机制有效解决了拓扑梯度饥饿问题，显著提升了细长曲线结构分割的拓扑正确性，是一种通用且高效的拓扑感知优化方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。遥感图像中道路、河流、海岸线等细长结构的拓扑完整性对后续分析至关重要。具体方案：(1) 将WPRF直接应用于遥感道路/河流分割任务，替换或联合标准Dice/交叉熵损失；(2) 针对遥感大尺度场景，可在图构建阶段引入地理空间先验（如DEM引导的水系连通性）约束动态规划搜索域；(3) 结合遥感多尺度特征，在解码器不同层级分别施加WPRF损失以增强多尺度拓扑感知；(4) 将WPRF与遥感专用的骨架化后处理（如形态细化）对比，验证端到端优化的优势。

Abstract (英文): Segmenting slender curvilinear structures such as retinal vessels, cracks, and roads demands topological correctness, as even a single-pixel discontinuity can fragment a continuous network and invalidate downstream analysis. Under standard binary-mask supervision, models optimized for pixel-level overlap frequently produce topologically broken predictions. We trace this to a fundamental mismatch: pixel-wise losses distribute gradients uniformly, yet connectivity hinges on a sparse set of bottleneck pixels. These pixels are vastly outnumbered by thick structures and background, rendering their aggregate gradient contribution negligible. We term this phenomenon topological gradient starvation (TGS). To address it, we propose Widest-Path Reachability Fields (WPRF), a differentiable Max-Min reachability objective that redirects gradient flow to connectivity bottlenecks. The module is plug-and-play, backbone-agnostic, and incurs no inference overhead. WPRF implements a differentiable Max-Min objective via dynamic programming on a domain-restricted graph, coupled with a bottleneck-aware observation term that balances gradient contributions across varying structures. Compared to prior topology-aware losses that rely on post-hoc skeletonization or homology computation, WPRF directly optimizes end-to-end reachability via differentiable Max-Min algebra, enabling gradient flow to concentrate on connectivity bottlenecks without auxiliary structures. We introduce OMVIS, a new oral microvessel segmentation dataset. Experiments across nine architectures and six datasets validate the bottleneck-focused gradient routing mechanism. WPRF improves 87\% of experiments with fixed hyperparameters and achieves clDice gains of 7.2 percentage points on structurally fragile datasets.

</details>


### [48] [When Prompts Ignore Structure: Graph-Based Attribute Reasoning for Calibrated VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07395)
*Tanay Sodha,Aditya Sharma,Ramya Hebbalaguppe,Vinti Agarwal,Pranav Murthy Yeluripaty*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出ARGTCA方法，通过符号属性图（Symbolic Attribute Graph）和图注意力网络（GAT）对（类别，属性）对的依赖关系进行结构化建模，并设计了两种属性选择策略（ARGTCA-DIV和ARGTCA-DISC），在视觉语言模型的测试时适应中显著降低期望校准误差（ECE），分别平均降低约37%和17%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视觉语言模型在测试时适应中，提示调优提高了零样本准确率，但由于熵驱动过度自信导致校准性能退化。现有方法使用LLM派生的类属性和对比正则化，但将属性视为独立实体，忽略了它们之间的关系结构。

Method: 将(类别, 属性)对作为节点构建符号属性图，使用对比目标训练图注意力网络（GAT）生成结构信息嵌入以捕捉属性间依赖关系；提出两种属性选择策略：ARGTCA-DIV（类内多样性）和ARGTCA-DISC（类间判别性）。

Result: 在9个基准数据集上，ARGTCA-DIV平均ECE降低约37%，ARGTCA-DISC平均ECE降低约17%，且ARGTCA-DISC始终为次优变体。

Conclusion: 对符号属性交互进行建模为视觉语言模型的可靠测试时适应提供了一种原则性方法。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像中地物类别（如建筑物、水体、植被）具有丰富的语义属性（如屋顶材质、水深、植被类型），属性间存在明确的结构化依赖关系。可将该方法应用于：(1) 遥感场景分类的测试时适应，利用属性图建模地物类别间的空间共现关系（如道路与停车场常共现）以提升校准性能；(2) 遥感变化检测中，将变化类型及其视觉属性构建为属性图，增强模型对变化类别的置信度可靠性；(3) 引入遥感领域知识（如光谱指数、纹理特征）作为属性节点，通过GAT学习域内属性交互模式，提升跨传感器/跨区域泛化能力。需注意遥感数据中类别不平衡问题可能影响图结构的学习效果。

Abstract (英文): Reliable confidence estimation remains a key limitation of test-time adaptation in vision-language models (VLMs), where prompt tuning improves zero-shot accuracy but often degrades calibration due to entropy-driven overconfidence. Prior approaches mitigate this using LLM-derived class attributes and contrastive regularization, yet treat attributes independently, ignoring their relational structure. We propose ARGTCA, which represents (class, attribute) pairs as nodes in a Symbolic Attribute Graph and trains a Graph Attention Network (GAT) using contrastive objectives to produce structurally informed embeddings that capture inter-attribute dependencies. We introduce two attribute selection strategies: ARGTCA-DIV for intra-class diversity and ARGTCA-DISC for inter-class discrimination. Experiments across nine benchmarks show that ARGTCA-DIV reduces average Expected Calibration Error (ECE) by approximately ~37% over baselines, while ARGTCA-DISC consistently performs as the second-best variant, reducing average ECE by approximately ~17% over baselines. These results suggest that modeling symbolic attribute interactions provides a principled approach for reliable test-time adaptation in VLMs.

</details>


### [49] [Sparse Attention for Dense Open-Vocabulary Prediction in CLIP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07135)
*Fatimah Zohra,Chen Zhao,Shuming Liu,Bernard Ghanem*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出在CLIP推理阶段，将最后视觉自注意力层中的逐行softmax替换为α-entmax变换，通过注意力稀疏化减少低显著性token的噪声，从而提升开放词汇密集预测任务（如语义分割和细粒度检索）的性能。实验表明，注意力稀疏化的收益与基线注意力在目标类别上的分散程度成正比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CLIP依赖的softmax自注意力机制将概率质量分配给每一对token（包括语义无关的），产生噪声，掩盖了密集开放词汇预测所需的细粒度、空间定位线索。

Method: 在推理阶段，将CLIP最后视觉自注意力层中的逐行softmax替换为α-entmax变换，该变换通过数据相关阈值将低得分映射为零，作为隐式去噪器，同时应用于标准query-key注意力及其自相关变体。

Result: 在开放词汇密集语义分割（Pascal VOC、Pascal Context、ADE20K）和细粒度检索（FG-OVD）任务上，注意力稀疏化带来性能提升，且收益与基线注意力在目标类别上的分散程度成正比。

Conclusion: 用α-entmax替换softmax实现注意力稀疏化，可以有效去除CLIP中的噪声注意力，提升开放词汇密集预测任务的性能。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像中的地物目标往往尺度变化大、边界模糊，且存在大量背景噪声（如植被、水体等），与本文关注的注意力噪声问题高度契合。具体方案：（1）将α-entmax替换应用于遥感基础模型（如RemoteCLIP、GeoRSCLIP）的最后一层视觉自注意力，提升遥感场景下的开放词汇语义分割性能；（2）针对遥感图像中目标类内差异大、类间相似性高的问题，可调节α参数实现不同程度的稀疏化，自适应地聚焦于目标区域；（3）可进一步将稀疏注意力机制引入遥感目标检测的多尺度特征融合中，抑制背景干扰。

Abstract (英文): Contrastive Language-Image Pre-training (CLIP) relies on softmax-based self-attention, a strictly positive distribution that assigns probability mass to every pair of tokens-even semantically irrelevant ones. While these dense softmax weights are effective for gathering broad context during pre-training, they spread attention across many low-salience tokens, producing noise that obscures the fine-grained, spatially localized cues required for dense, open-vocabulary prediction. We study an inference-time substitution of the row-wise softmax in the final visual self-attention layers with the $α$-entmax transform, applied across both the standard query-key attention and self-correlation variants. Because entmax applies a data-dependent threshold that maps low scores exactly to zero, it acts as an implicit denoiser, zeroing contextually irrelevant dependencies while redistributing mass onto the most relevant tokens. We evaluate on open-vocabulary tasks-dense semantic segmentation (Pascal VOC, Pascal Context, ADE20K) and fine-grained retrieval (FG-OVD)-and find the gain from attention sparsification is proportional to how much the baseline attention spreads off the target class.

### [50] [Heterogeneity-Adaptive Diffusion Schrodinger Bridge for PET-Guided Whole-Body MRI Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07401)
*Chengbo Wang,Jiacheng Yu,Linjie Bian,Ming Qi,Xiaosheng Liu,Tongtong Che,Jichang Zhang,Shuyu Li,Shaoli Song,Xiuying Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出HA-DSB框架，利用扩散薛定谔桥和视觉-语言模型实现全身PET-MR扫描中的MRI翻译，通过PET引导的双阶段机制提升病变区域翻译质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全身PET-MR扫描时间过长是临床效率的主要障碍，现有深度学习方法多针对特定解剖区域，难以处理全身扫描中因不同解剖区域和病变组织导致的异质性特征分布。

Method: 提出HA-DSB框架：(1) 将翻译任务建模为源目标分布间的随机传输；(2) 利用VLM提取区域上下文嵌入实现区域特定建模；(3) 双阶段PET引导机制：前向过程中PET引导噪声调制模块自适应缩放空间扩散扰动，反向过程中通过注意力机制选择性增强病变相关结构。

Result: 在全身MRI翻译任务中，该方法在不同身体区域均优于现有方法，且在PET引导下病变区域的翻译质量显著提升。

Conclusion: HA-DSB通过异质性自适应设计和PET先验知识融合，有效解决了全身MRI翻译中的区域异质性和病变保真度难题，为加速PET-MR扫描提供了可行方案。

Abstract (英文): While whole-body multimodal medical imaging scanners have been increasingly recognized for more effective medical applications, the excessive long acquisition time in PET-MR scanning is a major obstacle in more efficient clinical practice. Deep learning-based MRI translation provides a potential solution to reduce scan duration. However, current models often focus on specific anatomical regions and face challenges for whole-body scans that consists of highly heterogeneous feature distributions mainly due to (1) different anatomical regions across whole-body, and (2) lesions or pathological tissues. This paper tackles the challenges through a novel Heterogeneity-Adaptive Diffusion Schrodinger Bridge (HA-DSB) framework. By explicitly modeling translation as stochastic transport between source and target distributions, HA-DSB incorporates region context embeddings derived from a vision-language model (VLM) to enable region-specific modeling. To enhance fidelity of the pathological tissue, lesion-aware metabolic prior from PET is integrated directly into the bridge dynamics through a dual-stage guidance mechanism. Specifically, a PET-guided noise modulation module adaptively scales spatial diffusion perturbations during the forward process, while PET features are leveraged during the reverse process to selectively amplify lesion-relevant structures via an attention mechanism. Experiments demonstrate the superiority of our method across different body regions in whole-body MRI translation and show improved translation quality in lesion areas under PET guidance. Our code is available at Github.

### [51] [ASFR-Net: Adversarial Alignment and Spatio-Frequency Refinement Network for Heterogeneous Remote Sensing Image Change Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07161)
*Xin-Jie Wu,Zhi-Hui You,Si-Bao Chen,Qing-Ling Shu,Xiao Wang,Jin Tang,Bin Luo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种端到端的对抗性时空频域精化网络（ASFR-Net），用于解决遥感影像异源变化检测中因模态差异导致的伪变化问题。该方法通过模态不变表示学习器（MIR-Learner）提取跨模态不变特征，再通过时空频域协同增强模块（SFEM）抑制传感器特有噪声，最后利用级联层次引导融合模块（HGFM）生成精确变化图。同时发布了针对建筑变化的可见光-近红外异源变化检测基准数据集（VisNIR-HCD）。实验结果表明该方法达到了SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 异源变化检测的核心挑战在于如何有效解耦真实地物变化与因不同成像机制导致的显著模态差异，这些固有差异容易引入伪变化，从而限制检测精度。

Method: 1) 模态不变表示学习器（MIR-Learner）引导骨干网络提取模态不变特征，初步弥合域差距；2) 时空频域协同增强模块（SFEM）通过频域处理识别并抑制空间域难以分辨的传感器特有噪声和伪影；3) 多级差异特征输入带有级联层次引导融合模块（HGFM）的解码器生成变化图。

Result: 在VisNIR-HCD数据集和公开数据集上的大量实验表明，ASFR-Net达到了SOTA性能，显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: ASFR-Net通过对抗性时空频域精化策略有效解决了异源变化检测中的模态差异问题，所构建的VisNIR-HCD数据集为模型泛化评估提供了具有欺骗性视觉相似性和非线性光谱反转挑战的鲁棒平台。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感异源变化检测论文，改进方案：1) 当前MIR-Learner采用对抗性学习，可进一步引入对比学习或自监督预训练策略增强模态不变性；2) SFEM的频域处理可扩展为可学习的自适应频域滤波器，结合注意力机制动态调整不同频率分量的抑制权重；3) 可尝试将HGFM替换为Transformer架构以捕获更长距离的差异特征依赖；4) VisNIR-HCD数据集可扩展至更多异源模态对（如SAR-光学、热红外-可见光等），增加场景多样性。

Abstract (英文): The core challenge of heterogeneous change detection in remote sensing imagery lies in effectively decoupling genuine land-cover changes from significant modal disparities caused by distinct imaging mechanisms. These intrinsic inconsistencies are prone to introducing pseudo-changes, thereby constraining detection accuracy. To address this, we propose a novel, end-to-end adversarial spatio-frequency refinement network (ASFR-Net). Initially, a modality-invariant representation learner (MIR-Learner) guides the backbone to extract modality-invariant features, effectively bridging the primary domain gap. Subsequently, to address persistent residual modal differences, we design an innovative spatio-frequency synergistic enhancement module (SFEM), which identifies and suppresses sensor-specific noise and artifacts that are difficult to discern in the spatial domain by leveraging frequency-domain processing. Multi-level difference features are then computed from these refined representations and fed into a decoder equipped with cascaded hierarchical guided fusion module (HGFM) blocks to generate precise change maps. To alleviate the data scarcity in heterogeneous tasks, we construct and release a new high-resolution benchmark specifically focused on building changes: the visible-near-infrared heterogeneous change detection (VisNIR-HCD) dataset. It presents unique scientific challenges arising from deceptive visual similarity and non-linear spectral inversions, providing a robust platform for evaluating model generalization. Extensive experiments on VisNIR-HCD and public datasets demonstrate that ASFR-Net achieves state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance, significantly outperforming existing methods. The source code and the VisNIR-HCD dataset are publicly available at https://github.com/LuoYang2024/ASFR-Net.

### [52] [HIVE: Understanding Post-Hallucination Reasoning in Vision Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07507)
*Feng He,Zhenting Wang,Qifan Wang,Qiang Guan,Dongfang Liu,Ruixiang Tang,Qiankun Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出HIVE框架研究视觉语言模型中的幻觉后推理（PHR）阶段，发现在9个任务和9个模型上，幻觉描述虽为语义错误，却能在视觉-语言任务中提升准确率，因其扩展了语义覆盖并重塑推理动态，揭示了幻觉语义一旦进入推理上下文会显著影响下游预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作主要关注在生成阶段检测或抑制VLM的幻觉，但忽略了幻觉语义进入模型推理上下文后如何影响下游预测这一问题，即幻觉后推理（PHR）阶段尚未被系统研究。

Method: 引入HIVE（幻觉推理与验证引擎）评估基础设施，在忠实描述与幻觉描述之间进行受控对比，覆盖9个任务和9个模型，系统分析幻觉语义进入推理上下文后的影响。

Result: 幻觉描述在视觉-语言任务上往往提升准确率，而在纯文本任务中效果有限或不稳定；幻觉线索扩大了语义覆盖范围，重塑了推理动态，同时保持了稳定的推理过程。

Conclusion: 幻觉语义一旦进入模型的推理上下文会显著影响下游推理，理解这一后幻觉阶段对提高多模态推理系统的可靠性和可解释性至关重要。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域多模态任务（如遥感图像描述生成、视觉问答、目标检测）同样面临VLM幻觉问题。可将HIVE框架迁移至遥感场景：1）构建遥感专用的忠实/幻觉描述对比数据集；2）评估遥感VLM中幻觉对地物分类、变化检测等下游任务的影响；3）针对遥感中特有的地理空间歧义（如相似地物、遮挡）设计专门的幻觉后推理矫正策略。

Abstract (英文): Hallucinations in vision language models (VLMs) are commonly treated as semantic errors, yet they often arise from partial or ambiguous visual evidence. Prior work mainly focuses on detecting or suppressing hallucinations at generation time, leaving the subsequent reasoning stage largely unexplored. In this work, we study Post Hallucination Reasoning (PHR), the stage in which hallucinated semantics enter the model's inference context and influence downstream predictions. To systematically investigate PHR, we introduce HIVE, Hallucination Inference and Verification Engine, an evaluation infrastructure that enables controlled comparisons between faithful and hallucinated captions. Across nine tasks and nine models, we observe structured modality dependent patterns: hallucinated captions often improve accuracy on vision language tasks, while text only tasks exhibit limited or unstable effects. Further analyses show that hallucinated cues broaden semantic coverage and reshape reasoning dynamics while preserving stable inference. These findings highlight that hallucinated semantics may influence downstream reasoning once they enter the model's inference context. Understanding this post hallucination stage is important for improving the reliability and interpretability of multimodal reasoning systems. Code is publicly available at https://github.com/hefengcs/HIVE.

### [53] [NoDrift3R: Raymap-Guided Coupling for Drift-Robust Unposed Feed-Forward 3D Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07168)
*Xiangyu Sun,Liu Liu,Seungkwon Yang,Jingbing Han,Seungtae Nam,Zhizhong Su,Eunbyung Park*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 针对无位姿前馈式3D高斯泼溅在长序列中因相机位姿漂移导致性能退化的问题，提出Raymap引导的耦合模块（RGC），将高斯中心锚定到光线映射几何上，联合优化RGB重建、光线映射一致性和相机正则化，并引入双频视角调度策略，实现几何与外观的协同优化，显著提升长序列重建鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无位姿前馈式3DGS在长图像序列中因累积相机位姿估计漂移导致误差传播，严重限制渲染质量；纯渲染监督的位姿-几何联合优化易陷入局部最优。亟需一种显式耦合几何与外观、且对位姿漂移鲁棒的框架。

Method: 1) Raymap引导耦合模块（RGC）：将高斯中心锚定到光线映射（raymap）诱导的几何上，统一优化RGB重建损失、光线映射一致性损失和相机正则化损失，形成几何-外观双向反馈回路；2) 双频视角调度策略（Dual-Frequency Viewpoint Scheduling）：结合易到难的间隔扩展与短间隔对回放，稳定长时序学习。

Result: 在域内和跨域数据集上，渲染质量和位姿估计均一致提升，长序列鲁棒性显著改善。消融实验验证了显式几何-外观协同设计对可扩展且抗漂移的无位姿前馈3D重建的关键作用。

Conclusion: 显式设计的几何-外观协同机制是解决无位姿前馈3DGS长序列位姿漂移问题的关键，所提RGC模块和双频调度策略有效提升了重建可扩展性和鲁棒性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。遥感领域的大范围多视角影像序列同样面临严重的位姿估计漂移问题。具体方案：1) 将RGC模块迁移至遥感三维重建管道，用卫星/无人机影像的光线映射约束高斯泼溅几何，缓解长航带拼接的累积误差；2) 双频视角调度策略可适配遥感中"短基线密集匹配+长基线全局对齐"的混合采集模式；3) 引入遥感特有的高程先验（如DEM）作为几何正则项，进一步增强光线映射一致性约束的抗噪能力。

Abstract (英文): Pose-Free Feed-forward 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) has recently emerged as a powerful paradigm for fast scene reconstruction. However, its performance degrades significantly in long image sequences due to cumulative camera pose estimation drift, which propagates errors into geometric modeling and severely limits rendering fidelity. In this work, we revisit the long-sequence bottleneck and identify pose drift as the primary factor restricting reconstruction quality. Furthermore, while SfM-based pseudo ground-truth poses introduce sensor noise, purely rendering-based supervision often leads to optimization instability and local minima due to the entangled optimization of geometry and pose. To address the challenges, we propose a synergistic pose-free framework that explicitly couples geometry and appearance via a Raymap-Guided Coupling Module (RGC). Concretely, we anchor Gaussian centers to raymap-induced geometry and jointly optimize RGB reconstruction, raymap consistency, and camera regularization under a unified objective, yielding a bidirectional feedback loop: stronger geometry improves rendering, and appearance supervision in turn refines geometry and pose. To further stabilize learning across wide temporal ranges, we introduce a Dual-Frequency Viewpoint Scheduling strategy that combines easy-to-hard interval expansion with replay of short-interval pairs. Extensive experiments across in-domain and cross-domain datasets show consistent gains in both rendering and pose estimation, with notably improved robustness on long sequences. Ablation studies validate our central insight: explicitly designed geometry-appearance synergy is the key to scalable and drift-robust pose-free feed-forward 3D reconstruction.

### [54] [TACoS: Weakly Supervised Learning of Two-Dimensional Materials from Scribble Annotations to Precise Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07169)
*Jiabei Chen,Liping Zhang,Jiang-Bin Wu,Zhongming Wei,Enhao Ning,Su Yan,Weijun Li,Ping-Heng Tan,Xin Ning*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出TACoS框架，利用半监督一致性学习与树能量约束，仅需不到0.6%标注数据即可实现超过96%的全监督性能，用于二维材料薄片的精准像素级分割。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统全监督方法依赖密集标注，成本高且耗时，严重限制了分割模型在二维材料高通量筛选中的实际部署。

Method: 设计统一框架TACoS，包含两个核心模块：(1) 未标记弱-强分布对齐模块，利用余弦一致性约束增强视图间预测对齐；(2) 树能量正则化模块，利用最小生成树建立像素亲和关系并生成结构感知软伪标签。此外引入非对称区域对比学习，融合高置信预测与涂鸦形成增强标签，构建类别原型，并对边界未标记区域的困难像素施加对比约束。

Result: 在构建的石墨烯和MoS2数据集上，TACoS使用不到0.6%标注数据达到全监督性能的96%以上，在弱对比边缘和复杂背景下展现出优异的结构一致性和边界稳定性。

Conclusion: TACoS为二维材料薄片自动化高通量筛选提供了一种高效、可扩展的涂鸦分割解决方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像中存在大量弱对比边缘（如建筑物阴影边界、植被过渡带）和复杂背景（如城郊混合区域），TACoS的树能量正则化模块通过最小生成树建立像素亲和关系，可有效改善遥感语义分割中的边缘模糊问题。其非对称区域对比学习对边界未标记区域困难像素的约束机制，可直接迁移至遥感场景中地物边界精细化分割。建议将涂鸦标注替换为遥感常用的点/块标注，并调整最小生成树的图结构以适应大尺寸遥感影像。

Abstract (英文): The precise pixel-level localization of 2D material flakes is crucial for high-throughput screening. However, traditional fully supervised methods rely on dense annotations, which are costly and time-consuming, severely limiting the practical deployment of segmentation models. This paper proposes TACoS, a specialized scribble segmentation framework tailored for 2D materials. First, we design a unified framework that integrates semi-supervised consistency learning with structured tree energy constraints. This framework comprises two core components: an unlabeled weak-strong distribution alignment module and a tree energy regularization module. The former employs cosine consistency constraints to enhance prediction alignment across views. Meanwhile, the latter utilizes minimum spanning trees to establish pixel affinity relationships and generate structure-aware soft pseudo labels for online semantic guidance. Next, we introduce asymmetric regional contrast learning. This approach fuses high-confidence predictions from the weak augmentation branch with scribbles to form augmented labels, and construct category prototypes in the representation space. Simultaneously, we prioritize contrastive constraints on challenging pixels in boundary-unlabeled regions. This strategy enhances intra-class cohesion and inter-class separation at the representation level, effectively reducing category confusion in low-contrast edges and complex backgrounds. Experiments conducted on the constructed graphene and MoS2 datasets demonstrate that our method TACoS achieves over 96% of fully supervised performance using less than 0.6% annotated data. Furthermore, it exhibits superior structural coherence and boundary stability in scenarios with weakly contrasting edges and complex backgrounds, providing an efficient and scalable solution for automated high-throughput screening of 2D material flakes.

### [55] [PUF: Plug-and-Play Uncertainty-Aware Fusion for Online 3D Scene Graph Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07170)
*Yi Yang,Myrna Castillo,Bodo Rosenhahn,Michael Ying Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出PUF，一种即插即用、不确定性感知、无需训练的融合框架，通过将场景图节点关联重构为概率似然、使用狄利克雷证据累积以及引入类条件先验，有效处理在线3D场景图生成中的观测、2D模型和3D表示三种不确定性来源，在3DSSG和ReplicaSSG基准上显著优于现有方法且保持实时性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线3D场景图生成方法将融合视为完全确定性的流水线，忽略了三种不确定性来源：观测不确定性、2D模型不确定性和3D表示不确定性。作者旨在提出一种不确定性感知的融合框架来解决这一问题。

Method: 1) 将场景图节点关联重构为基于语义和空间因子的概率似然，取代二元接受/拒绝门控；2) 使用狄利克雷证据累积，按关联似然比例将类别和关系证据分布到候选节点上；3) 引入可选的类条件先验，为稀疏或从未共同观测的对象对补全边。该方法即插即用、无需训练，并在3D高斯和3D体素两种后端上验证。

Result: 在3DSSG和ReplicaSSG基准上，PUF显著优于现有方法，同时保持实时延迟。在3D高斯和3D体素两种后端上均取得一致性改进，证明其跨表示泛化能力。

Conclusion: 不确定性感知融合是在线3D场景理解中一种有原则且有效的范式，PUF为后续研究提供了开源代码基础。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感三维场景理解（如城市场景重建、多视角遥感图像融合）面临类似的确定性融合问题。具体方案：1) 将PUF的狄利克雷证据累积应用于遥感多视角目标检测与分类中的类别不确定性建模；2) 遥感场景中物体（建筑物、树木、车辆）的稀疏共现问题可通过类条件先验进行边补全；3) 可结合3D高斯泼溅表示处理遥感点云数据中的观测噪声和空间不确定性，提升场景图构建的鲁棒性。

Abstract (英文): Online 3D scene graph generation builds a persistent, structured representation of a scene by incrementally fusing 2D observations into a global 3D graph. Existing online methods treat this fusion as a fully deterministic pipeline, where we identify three sources of uncertainty that are overlooked: observation, 2D model, and 3D representation. We propose PUF: a Plug-and-play, Uncertainty-aware, and training-free Fusion framework. Scene graph node association is reformulated as a probabilistic likelihood over semantic and spatial factors, replacing binary accept/reject gates. Dirichlet evidence accumulation distributes class and relationship evidence across plausible candidates proportional to association likelihood. An optional class-conditional prior completes edges for sparsely or never co-observed object pairs. We instantiate PUF with both a 3D Gaussian and a 3D voxel backend and observe consistent improvements, demonstrating its ability to generalize across different representations. Experiments on the 3DSSG and ReplicaSSG benchmarks show that our method substantially outperforms existing approaches while maintaining real-time latency. These results establish uncertainty-aware fusion as a principled and effective paradigm for online 3D scene understanding. The source code is publicly available at https://github.com/yyyyangyi/PUF.

### [56] [Stage-Aware Adaptation and Distribution Calibration for Subject-Driven Personalized Text-to-Image Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07173)
*Wenyan Xu,Alizer Wong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出SPaRa-DCAL框架，通过训练阶段的时步感知低秩适配（SPaRa）和推理阶段的分布校准候选选择（DCAL），解决个性化文本到图像生成中不同去噪阶段容量需求差异及候选选择偏向身份相似性导致表示多样性不足的问题。理论分析表明时步依赖缩放控制低秩适配器的扰动幅度，身份偏置候选选择限制特征半径。实验表明DCAL在固定LoRA候选池上提升身份一致性和文本对齐，但牺牲了多样性，说明评估应兼顾身份一致性、文本对齐和表示多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法（如PaRa）采用统一低秩约束或统一适配器强度，无法区分不同去噪阶段对模型容量的差异化需求；此外，推理阶段的候选选择主要基于身份相似度，导致所选样本在视觉表示空间中被压缩，缺乏多样性。

Method: 将问题分解为两个互补组件：（1）SPaRa——训练阶段时步感知的低秩适配，根据去噪时间步动态调整低秩适配器的缩放因子；（2）DCAL——推理阶段分布校准的候选选择，缓解身份相似度主导的样本压缩问题。两个组件组合为SPaRa-DCAL框架。

Result: 在SDXL和DreamBooth 30主体协议下，DCAL在固定LoRA候选池上提升了1-LPIPS、CLIP-I、DINO-I和CLIP-T指标，但同时揭示了与CLIP/DINO成对多样性和成对LPIPS之间的明确权衡关系。

Conclusion: 个性化生成不应仅以身份一致性指标评估，而应综合身份一致性、文本对齐和表示多样性三个维度进行评价。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该方法的时步感知低秩适配策略可迁移至遥感图像生成任务，如针对遥感场景中不同地物类别（建筑物、水体、植被）在不同生成阶段对细节保真度要求不同的问题，SPaRa可动态调整适配强度；DCAL的分布校准候选选择可用于遥感数据增强中保持地物类别多样性与身份一致性（如特定卫星传感器风格）的平衡。此外，遥感领域常面临样本稀缺问题，该框架的低秩适配策略可有效缓解过拟合。

Abstract (英文): Subject-driven personalized text-to-image generation requires a pretrained diffusion model to acquire a specific subject from a few reference images while preserving subject identity, following novel text prompts, and maintaining sample diversity. Existing optimization-based methods instantiate subject adaptation through full fine-tuning, textual embedding optimization, or low-rank parameter updates; PaRa further constrains personalization from the perspective of parameter rank reduction. However, a uniform low-rank constraint or a uniform adapter strength cannot explicitly distinguish the capacity requirements of different denoising stages. Moreover, inference-time candidate selection driven mainly by identity similarity may compress the selected samples in the visual representation space. We decompose the problem into two complementary components: SPaRa denotes training-side stage-aware low-rank adaptation, DCAL denotes inference-side distribution-calibrated candidate selection, and SPaRa-DCAL denotes the combined framework. Theoretical analysis shows that timestep-dependent scaling controls the effective perturbation magnitude of a low-rank adapter, while identity-biased candidate selection restricts the radius of selected features around the reference center under explicit conditions. Auditable experiments under the SDXL and DreamBooth 30-subject protocol show that DCAL improves 1-LPIPS, CLIP-I, DINO-I, and CLIP-T on a fixed LoRA candidate pool, while revealing a clear trade-off with CLIP/DINO pairwise diversity and pairwise LPIPS. These results indicate that personalized generation should be evaluated through identity consistency, text alignment, and representation diversity rather than identity metrics alone.

### [57] [Comparative Study of Domain-adapted VLMs for General Document Visual Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07179)
*Miguel Lopez-Duran,Elena Marrero,Julian Fierrez,Marta Robledo-Moreno,Ruben Vera-Rodriguez,Daniel DeAlcala,Aythami Morales,Ruben Tolosana,Oscar Delgado,Alvaro Ortigosa,Javier Ortega-Garcia*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了8种开源预训练VLM在DocVQA任务上的性能，涵盖零样本、全监督微调和少样本学习三种设置，涉及工业文档、信息图和幻灯片三种文档领域。研究发现：视觉理解是DocVQA的主要瓶颈，参数规模主导性能但小模型通过微调获益更大，仅需50个目标域样本即可快速适应新领域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管VLM在文本-视觉任务上表现优异，但其在DocVQA任务上的鲁棒性和跨文档领域的迁移能力尚未得到充分探索，缺乏系统性评估。

Method: 选取8种开源预训练VLM，在三种文档领域（工业文档、信息图、幻灯片）上进行零样本评估、全监督微调（域内和跨域评估）以及少样本学习评估，系统分析模型性能与参数规模、训练策略、领域差异之间的关系。

Result: 大型预训练VLM在结构化布局上零样本基线强，但在信息图和幻灯片等视觉复杂布局上性能显著下降；参数规模主导性能，但小架构通过监督微调获得更高相对增益；跨域和少样本实验表明视觉理解是DocVQA的主要瓶颈；50个目标域样本即可使模型快速适应甚至超越全监督微调性能。

Conclusion: DocVQA的瓶颈在于视觉理解能力而非VLM的知识缺乏；小模型微调效率更高；少样本跨域迁移是应对新文档领域的有效策略。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该研究的方法论可直接迁移到遥感文档分析领域。具体方案：(1) 选取遥感影像中的地理报告、专题地图、遥感解译图表等作为文档域，采用零样本/少样本跨域评估框架测试VLM在遥感文档上的图文理解能力；(2) 针对遥感文档特有的空间坐标、光谱信息、时序标签等视觉-文本特征，设计专门的评估指标和领域适应策略；(3) 参考本文"视觉理解是瓶颈"的发现，在遥感DocVQA中重点增强模型对地理空间布局、地物边界、图例等视觉元素的解析能力；(4) 利用50-100个遥感文档样本即可实现快速领域适应，显著降低遥感智能解译中的标注成本。

Abstract (英文): Document Visual Question Answering (DocVQA) presents a complex multimodal challenge, requiring models to exploit visual, textual, and layout information from documents. Although Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have shown remarkable performance in text-vision tasks, their robustness and transferability to different document domains remains underexplored. In this study, we present a comprehensive evaluation of 8 open-source pretrained VLMs on DocVQA in three different document domains: industrial documents of varying type, infographics, and presentation slides. We systematically assess model performance under zero-shot evaluations, fully supervised finetuning with inter- and intra-dataset evaluations, and few-shot learning evaluations of knowledge transfer between domains. Our findings demonstrate that while large pretrained VLMs possess strong zero-shot baselines for structured layouts, their performance strongly decreases on visually complex layouts of infographics and slides. Although parameter scaling is a dominant factor on performance, supervised finetuning yields higher relative gains in smaller architectures. Furthermore, our cross-domain and few-shot experiments show that visual understanding is the main bottleneck for DocVQA, not a lack of knowledge from the VLMs. Using 50 target domain samples, the models finetuned in DocVQA with datasets of different domains rapidly adapt to the target domain documents, even surpassing their fully supervised counterparts in some cases.

### [58] [EditVerse3D: High-Quality 3D Object Editing with Region-Aware Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07187)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D局部编辑方法依赖完整的编辑2D图像、精确的3D掩码或复杂的流水线，而人类在交互时更倾向于指定粗略的兴趣区域。这一差距限制了3D编辑的实用性和易用性。

Method: 1）以粗粒度3D边界框和参考2D图像作为输入；2）提出区域自适应损失，强调难学习区域并平衡目标区域与保留区域的优化目标；3）通过缩放3D掩码训练和过滤不真实编辑对等数据增强策略提升鲁棒性和泛化能力；4）构建基于部件信息的大规模3D编辑数据集。

Abstract (英文): Local editing of 3D objects remains a long-standing challenge. When interacting with 3D content, humans naturally tend to specify a coarse region of interest for modification rather than defining precise editing boundaries. However, previous methods rely on fully edited 2D images, precise 3D masks, or redundant pipelines, which present a gap. To bridge this gap, we propose EditVerse3D, a novel 3D editing framework that enables high-quality object editing under such coarse guidance. Our approach takes as input a 3D object to be edited, a coarse 3D bounding box indicating the target region, and a reference 2D image describing the desired modification. It produces a coherent, high-fidelity edited 3D object. To facilitate this editing, we introduce a novel region-aware adaptive loss that emphasizes hard-to-learn regions and balances the objective between target and preserved areas. Complementing our loss function, we enhance model robustness and generalization through targeted data augmentations, such as training with scaled 3D masks and filtering out unrealistic editing pairs. We construct a large-scale 3D editing dataset derived from parts information. Extensive experiments demonstrate that EditVerse3D achieves superior visual quality and quantitative performance compared to existing 3D editing approaches. Please visit our project page at https://editverse3d.github.io.

### [59] [Prototype-Anchored Generalized Manifold Regression for Unknown-Domain Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07192)
*Zihao Zhang,Aming Wu,Yang Li,Yahong Han*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出MR-DCoT方法，通过将未知域泛化建模为流形回归问题，利用视觉-文本双链思维模块生成离群样本，并采用类特定原型锚定学习校正算子，将偏离特征投影回源语义流形，从而解决单域广义目标检测中的分布偏移问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有单域广义目标检测方法依赖模拟驱动策略（如数据增强或文本提示）来扩大训练分布，但有限模拟难以覆盖真实场景的动态变化，容易过拟合到合成风格，对复杂结构退化鲁棒性不足。

Method: 提出MR-DCoT方法：1) 视觉-文本双链思维模块，结合VLM引导的语义演化与扩散驱动的结构扰动，生成结构化离群难例；2) 类特定原型锚定，学习校正算子将偏离特征投影回源语义流形；3) 将离群生成与语义校正集成闭环，缩小分布差异。

Result: 在三个互补基准（恶劣天气检测、真实到艺术泛化、零样本语义分割）上的大量实验证明了方法的有效性和通用性。

Conclusion: 通过将未知域泛化重新定义为流形回归问题，利用离群样本生成与语义校正的闭环机制，有效缩小分布差异，提升模型在未知域偏移下的鲁棒性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。具体方案：1) 遥感图像存在显著域差异（不同传感器、天气、季节、地域），MR-DCoT的流形回归思想可直接应用于遥感目标检测的跨域泛化；2) 视觉-文本双链思维模块可利用遥感领域知识（如地物类别先验、光谱特征）生成语义相关的结构退化样本；3) 类特定原型锚定可针对遥感中典型地物类别（建筑物、车辆、船只等）分别构建原型，提升多类别遥感检测的域泛化能力；4) 扩散模型可模拟遥感图像特有的退化模式（云雾遮挡、光照变化、几何畸变），增强模型对复杂环境鲁棒性。

Abstract (英文): In this paper, we study Single-Domain Generalized Object Detection (Single-DGOD), which aims to transfer a detector trained on a single source domain to multiple unseen domains. Existing methods mainly rely on simulation-driven strategies, such as data augmentation or textual prompts, to enlarge the training distribution. However, finite simulations can hardly cover the dynamic variations of real-world scenarios, often causing overfitting to synthetic styles and limited robustness to complex structural degradations. Inspired by the manifold hypothesis, we argue that semantic features, despite diverse visual changes, should lie on a compact and stable low-dimensional manifold. Therefore, robust generalization requires rectifying deviant samples back to this semantic manifold, rather than exhaustively simulating external perturbations. To this end, we propose Manifold Regression with Visual-Text Dual Chain-of-Thought (MR-DCoT), which formulates unknown-domain generalization as a manifold regression problem. MR-DCoT first uses a Visual-Text Dual Chain-of-Thought module to combine VLM-guided semantic evolution with diffusion-based structural perturbation, generating structured off-manifold hard examples. It then introduces Class-Specific Prototype Anchoring to learn a rectification operator that projects deviant features toward the source semantic manifold. By integrating outlier generation and semantic correction into a closed loop, MR-DCoT effectively narrows the distribution gap and improves robustness under unseen shifts. Extensive experiments on three complementary benchmarks, including adverse-weather detection, real-to-art generalization, and zero-shot semantic segmentation, demonstrate the effectiveness and versatility of our method.

### [60] [DiffCVE: Diffusion-based Compressed Video Enhancement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07195)
*Wenqiang Xiao,Wenzhuo Ma,Junxi Zhang,Zhenzhong Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出DiffCVE，一种基于扩散模型的压缩视频感知质量增强方法。通过编码先验增强双条件（CPDC）分支联合建模压缩视频与编码先验（残差和运动矢量），引入压缩退化语义提示（CDSP）机制利用QP条件文本提示和LoRA微调感知压缩强度，并在VAE解码器中加入编码先验引导加权融合（CPWF）模块。实验表明，该方法在严重压缩场景下显著提升了感知质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 严重压缩视频存在复杂伪影模式和大量信息丢失，现有扩散模型直接应用于压缩视频时忽略了压缩退化特性，且可能产生结构不一致的幻觉（hallucinations）。

Method: 1) Coding Prior-enhanced Dual Conditioning (CPDC)：联合建模压缩视频和编码先验（残差、运动矢量）条件，为扩散去噪提供结构和运动引导；2) Compression Degradation Semantic Prompting (CDSP)：利用QP条件文本提示结合LoRA微调，使扩散过程感知压缩严重程度；3) Coding Prior-guided Weighted Fusion (CPWF)：在VAE解码器中融合VAE编码器和编码先验编码器特征，并使用QP预测权重进行自适应融合。

Result: 大量实验表明，所提方法在提升感知质量方面有效，尤其是在严重压缩设置下表现显著。

Conclusion: 提出的DiffCVE通过引入编码先验和压缩退化感知机制，有效解决了扩散模型在压缩视频增强中的结构不一致问题，在严重压缩下取得了优异的感知质量提升效果。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域常面临高压缩传输（如卫星通信带宽受限）导致的视频/图像质量退化。具体交叉方案：1) 将CPDC中的残差和运动矢量先验替换为遥感特有的编码先验（如光谱残差、多时相运动场），适配遥感视频压缩标准（如CCSDS）；2) CDSP中的QP条件可扩展为遥感图像质量因子（如GSD、信噪比）的文本提示，结合LoRA适应不同传感器特性；3) CPWF可引入空间-光谱注意力融合机制，处理遥感多光谱/高光谱数据的编解码特征融合。

Abstract (英文): Perceptual quality enhancement of severely compressed videos remains challenging due to complex artifact patterns and substantial information loss. Recent diffusion models have demonstrated strong generative capability for visual restoration, but directly applying them to compressed video often ignores compression degradation characteristics and may introduce structure-inconsistent hallucinations. To address this issue, this paper presents a diffusion-based compressed video enhancement method, named DiffCVE. Coding Prior-enhanced Dual Conditioning (CPDC) branches are designed to jointly model compressed video and coding prior conditions, where coding priors including residuals and motion vectors provide complementary structural and motion guidance during the diffusion denoising process. To make the diffusion process aware of compression severity, a Compression Degradation Semantic Prompting (CDSP) mechanism is introduced to leverage QP-conditioned textual prompts together with LoRA fine-tuning. In addition, a Coding Prior-guided Weighted Fusion (CPWF) module is incorporated into the VAE decoder to fuse VAE encoder and coding prior encoder features with QP-predicted weights. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed method in improving perceptual quality, especially under severe compression settings. The project page with enhanced video demonstrations is available at https://wqmaker.github.io/projects/DiffCVE/.

</details>


### [61] [Why Fake ? Unveiling the Semantic Vocabulary of Deepfake Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07216)

TL;DR: 本文提出使用后验可解释人工智能（XAI）方法——编码-解码方向对（EDDP）来分析黑盒深度伪造检测器的决策过程，揭示检测器隐式学习到的真实和伪造特征，实现全局模型理解、空间感知概念定位和反事实分析。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度伪造检测器大多仅输出二元分类标签（真/假），缺乏可解释性，无法满足法律诉讼等实际应用需求。已有的可解释检测方法要么依赖人工标注进行精确伪影定位，要么生成表面合理但缺乏依据的文本解释。

Method: 采用后验可解释人工智能（XAI）方法——编码-解码方向对（EDDP），该技术能够揭示黑盒深度伪造检测器的概念空间（语义词汇表），以及内部表示中写入和读取概念信息的机制。

Result: 揭示了检测器在训练过程中隐式学习的真实和伪造特征，提供了传统方法无法获得的细致解释；实现了全局模型理解、空间感知概念定位和反事实"what-if"分析。

Abstract (英文): Deepfake (DF) technology poses a significant threat to information integrity, driving the need for robust detection methods. Most DF detectors only consider predicting a binary label for whether the input is real or fake, lacking the justification required for real-world applications like legal proceedings. Explainable DF Detection has emerged to address this limitation, but existing techniques frequently fall short by either relying on human annotations for precise artifact localization or generating superficially plausible textual explanations without grounding. This work investigates the use of post-hoc explainable AI (XAI) to analyze the decision-making process of state-of-the-art black-box DF detectors. Specifically, we employ Encoding-Decoding Direction Pairs (EDDP), a technique suitable for uncovering the concept space of DF detectors (their semantic vocabulary) as well as the mechanism for writing and reading concept information to and from internal representations. Our analysis reveals previously hidden real and fake features learned implicitly during detector training, offering nuanced explanations unattainable through conventional methods. This enables global model understanding, spatially aware concept localization, and counterfactual what-if analysis, all contributing to a deeper comprehension of DF detection strategies.

### [62] [`Attention-Guided Cross-Temporal Clustering for Self-Supervised Video Object Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07230)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 监督VOS方法依赖密集标注、成本高且领域覆盖有限；现有自监督方法难以同时保持空间精度和时间一致性，且多依赖光流、合成运动线索或任务特定预训练，限制了可扩展性和泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): Video object segmentation (VOS) is a fundamental task in video understanding, requiring accurate delineation and consistent tracking of objects across frames. While supervised methods achieve strong performance, they rely on densely annotated datasets that are costly to obtain and have limited domain coverage. Self-supervised learning offers a promising alternative by removing the need for manual labels; however, existing approaches often struggle to jointly maintain spatial accuracy and temporal coherence, particularly in unconstrained multi-object scenarios. Many rely on optical flow, synthetic motion cues, or task-specific pretraining, limiting scalability and generalisation. We propose a self-supervised framework, Cross-Temporal Consistency and Clustering, that learns mid-level, part-aware representations by combining attention-guided token selection with lightweight temporal clustering. Instead of operating at the pixel or whole-object level, the method aligns soft part assignments across time using a saliency-weighted symmetric consistency objective. The framework leverages a frozen transformer backbone with lightweight modules for adaptive token selection and multi-offset temporal alignment, enabling efficient scaling across resolutions and motion patterns.

### [63] [Unraveling Machine Behavior by Multi-Level Bias Analysis and Detection: Methodology and Application to Computer Vision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07236)
*Ignacio Serna,Aythami Morales,Julian Fierrez*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种多层次的神经网络偏差检测框架，包含三种方法：SpaceBias（新方法，基于潜空间邻居概率分布）、ActivationBias（扩展方法，基于卷积层激活值）和WeightBias（扩展方法，基于模型参数中的偏模式），在超过127,000个模型上验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有偏差检测方法通常将神经网络视为黑箱，仅评估模型输出结果，无法揭示偏差在网络内部各层级的形成和传播机制。本文旨在通过多层级分析，深入理解偏差如何在潜空间、层激活值和模型参数中表现。

Method: 1) SpaceBias: 利用最终分类层前的潜空间，通过邻居概率分布表征各群体分布，采用双样本Kolmogorov-Smirnov检验量化偏差。2) ActivationBias: 基于InsideBias扩展，分析网络滤波器激活值，利用Mann-Whitney U检验检测欠代表群体在最终卷积层中激活水平较低的现象。3) WeightBias: 基于IFBiD扩展，训练辅助神经网络直接在任务特定模型的参数中识别偏模式。

Result: 在DiveFace数据集（72,000张人脸图像）和彩色MNIST基准上进行实验，训练并评估了超过127,000个不同偏差程度和类型的模型。结果表明，随着训练分布趋于平衡，内部差异及检测性能平滑下降。

Conclusion: 本文提出的多层级偏差检测方法相比传统黑箱方法能提供更深入的模型行为洞察，有助于理解偏差在网络内部的表现形式。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域模型（如地物分类、目标检测模型）同样面临训练数据分布不均衡导致的偏差问题。具体方案：1) 将SpaceBias应用于遥感图像分类模型的潜空间分析，检测不同地理区域或地物类别间的表征偏差；2) 利用ActivationBias检测遥感CNN模型中对稀有地物类别的激活响应不足问题；3) 将WeightBias用于遥感模型的参数审计，识别模型对特定环境条件（如光照、季节）的倾向性偏差。

Abstract (英文): This study investigates the presence and propagation of bias within Neural Networks through a comprehensive multi-level analysis spanning the learned latent space, layer activations, and the network's parameters. Based on this taxonomy, we propose three bias detection approaches: 1) SpaceBias (new method), which characterizes the latent space prior to the final classification layer using neighbor-probability distributions and quantifies bias with the two-sample Kolmogorov-Smirnov test on the per-group distributions. 2) ActivationBias (extension of the existing method InsideBias), which analyzes the activations of neural network filters and quantifies bias via a Mann-Whitney U test, based on the observed fact that underrepresented groups exhibit lower activation levels in the final convolutional layers. 3) WeightBias (extension of the existing method IFBiD), which uses a secondary neural network trained to identify biased patterns directly in the parameters of task-specific models. Unlike conventional methods, which assess neural network outcomes and treat the model as a black box, our proposed techniques provide insight into how biases manifest within the network architecture itself at different levels, offering a more nuanced and detailed understanding. Experiments are conducted on two complementary applications: gender classification in the DiveFace dataset (72,000 face images) and digit classification on a colored-MNIST benchmark with controlled bias severity. In total, more than 127,000 models with varying degrees and types of bias were trained and evaluated. The severity sweep shows that the internal disparity, and with it the detection performance, decreases smoothly as the training distribution approaches balance. The results highlight the importance of methods that provide deeper insight into the behavior of AI models.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SAM在自然图像上表现优异，但在超声图像上由于边界模糊和斑点噪声导致性能下降，亟需针对性的改进方法。

Abstract (英文): Ultrasound image segmentation is essential for delineating anatomical structures and lesions, providing the foundation for accurate diagnosis. While the Segment Anything Model (SAM) has demonstrated remarkable success on natural images, its performance on ultrasound data is often hindered by poor boundary delineation. To address this limitation, we propose EP-SAM, an edge-aware and prompt-enhanced adaptation of SAM. Specifically, we leverage multi-block feature extraction from the image encoder to enrich coarse-to-fine semantic representations, while edge-aware supervision of the image encoder improves robustness to contour ambiguity and speckle noise.
