### [65] [Naming the Concepts Classifiers Rely On: Language-Anchored Decomposition for Faithful Explanation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07264)
*Ahsan Habib Akash,Dipkamal Bhusal,Stacey Jones,Donald A. Adjeroh,Binod Bhattarai,Prashnna Kumar Gyawali*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出语言锚定分解（LAD）框架，无需修改模型或重训练即可同时获得可命名、忠实且空间精确的概念解释，通过LLM生成概念词汇、CLIP定位、非负矩阵分解固定语言锚定矩阵来学习概念基，在多个基准上验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可解释性方法面临权衡：事后概念方法能忠实反映模型行为但概念无名，而命名方法或设计方法需要重训练或修改分类器才能附加可读概念。缺少一种能同时满足命名、忠实且无需修改模型的解释方案。

Method: LAD框架分为三步：(1) 对每个类别，使用大语言模型（LLM）生成候选概念词汇；(2) 利用CLIP相似度图在图像区域中定位这些概念的空间位置；(3) 反转标准非负矩阵分解过程：将语言锚定的概念图固定为系数矩阵，仅学习用于重构冻结编码器激活的概念基，使得命名成为结构约束，由模型自身的特征几何决定保留哪些概念。

Result: 在自然图像、场景和医学影像基准上，LAD生成空间精确的解释，在概念插入和删除测试中均保持决策相关性，同时提供稳定、人类可读的概念名称。移除语言锚定会保留精度但导致归因忠实度崩溃。

Conclusion: LAD成功打破了事后解释中命名与忠实度之间的权衡，证明通过语言锚定作为结构约束，可以在不修改模型的前提下获得既忠实于模型行为又具有人类可读性的概念解释。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。遥感场景中地物分类（如土地利用分类、目标检测）需要可解释决策，LAD可直接应用于遥感CNN/ViT编码器：(1) 利用遥感领域词典或地物标签库替代LLM生成概念词汇，如"水域""植被""建筑阴影"等；(2) CLIP在遥感图像上的相似度匹配可借助遥感预训练模型（如RemoteCLIP）提升定位精度；(3) 可用于分析误分类样本，通过对比保留/删除的概念基诊断模型关注了哪些非目标地物特征，提升遥感模型的可信度和部署安全性。

Abstract (英文): Deep neural networks are widely deployed in high-stakes visual applications where interpretability is critical, yet existing explanations face a trade-off: post-hoc concept methods recover factors that are faithful to a model's behavior but unnamed, while naming and by-design methods attach human-readable concepts only by retraining or altering the classifier. We propose Language-Anchored Decomposition (LAD), a post-hoc framework that delivers concepts which are simultaneously named, faithful, and obtained without modifying the model. For each class, a large language model proposes a concept vocabulary that CLIP-based similarity maps localize across image regions. Inverting standard non-negative matrix factorization, LAD fixes these language-grounded maps as the coefficient matrix and learns only a concept basis that reconstructs the frozen encoder's activations, so naming becomes a structural constraint and the model's own feature geometry determines which concepts are retained. Removing this anchor preserves accuracy but collapses attribution faithfulness. Across natural-image, scene, and medical-imaging benchmarks, LAD produces spatially precise explanations that are decision-relevant under both concept insertion and deletion, while uniquely providing stable, human-interpretable concept names.

</details>


### [66] [InfraQR: Edge-Placed QR-Inspired Structured Patch Attacks on Infrared Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07288)
*Xin Li,Jiaju Han,Ma Yaqi,Chengyin Hu,Yingying Zhao,Jiahuan Long,Fengyu Zhang,Yahui Chai*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出InfraQR——一种受QR码启发的结构化补丁攻击方法，用于攻击红外视觉语言模型。该补丁沿图像边界放置，通过代理CLIP编码器优化可学习的网格单元，形成近似二值化的结构外观。实验表明，该方法能显著降低红外分类、字幕生成和VQA任务的性能，例如将OpenAI CLIP准确率从98.67%降至0.70%，并能黑盒迁移至其他模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 红外视觉语言模型在低光和恶劣视觉条件下的感知应用日益广泛，但其对局部结构化扰动的鲁棒性尚未被充分探索。现有的红外对抗攻击研究主要聚焦于目标检测器，而对红外视觉语言模型安全性的系统研究相对缺乏。

Method: InfraQR方法：1) 设计沿图像边界放置的紧凑结构化补丁，而非附着在目标对象上；2) 通过代理CLIP风格编码器优化可学习的网格单元；3) 补丁具有近似二值化的结构外观，但无需是有效的QR码。在红外分类、字幕迁移和VQA三个任务上评估。

Result: 在300张红外图像基准测试中，InfraQR显著降低了多个CLIP风格分类器的准确率，如将OpenAI CLIP准确率从98.67%降至0.70%。生成的对抗图像可黑盒迁移至字幕生成和VQA模型，导致字幕语义退化及GPT-5.4评估下的回答错误率上升。

Conclusion: 红外视觉语言模型仍然容易受到结构化边缘放置扰动的攻击，需要进一步研究超越直接目标遮挡的跨任务鲁棒性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。红外视觉语言模型在遥感领域同样适用于夜间、烟雾、云层遮挡等低可见度场景的感知任务。具体方案：1) 将InfraQR的攻击框架应用于遥感红外视觉语言模型（如遥感CLIP变体）的安全性评估，检验其对遥感图像分类、遥感图像描述和遥感视觉问答的威胁程度；2) 借鉴InfraQR的边界结构化补丁设计思想，提出面向遥感场景的对抗防御方法，如在红外遥感图像边缘添加防御性结构噪声以提升模型鲁棒性；3) 将InfraQR的优化策略（网格单元学习+代理编码器）用于遥感红外图像的超分辨率或去噪任务，提升模型对结构化噪声的适应能力。

Abstract (英文): Infrared vision-language models are increasingly used for perception under low-light and adverse visual conditions, yet their robustness to localized structured perturbations remains underexplored. Existing infrared adversarial studies mainly focus on object detectors, leaving the security of infrared vision-language models less systematically examined. We present InfraQR, a QR-inspired structured patch attack for infrared vision-language models. Unlike localized attacks that attach perturbations to the target object, InfraQR places a compact structured patch along image boundaries and optimizes learnable grid cells through surrogate CLIP-style encoders. The resulting patch has a near-binary structured appearance, but is not required to be a valid or machine-readable QR code. We evaluate InfraQR on infrared classification, caption transfer, and question-answer-aware visual question answering (VQA) tasks. On a 300-image infrared benchmark, InfraQR sharply reduces the accuracy of multiple CLIP-style classifiers, including reducing OpenAI CLIP accuracy from 98.67% to 0.70%. The generated adversarial images also transfer to black-box captioning and VQA models, causing semantic degradation in captions and more error-prone answers under GPT-5.4-based evaluation. These results show that infrared vision-language models remain vulnerable to structured edge-placed perturbations, motivating further study of cross-task robustness beyond direct object occlusion.

</details>

Abstract (英文): The SoccerNet 2026 Challenges constitute the sixth annual edition of the SoccerNet open benchmarking effort, dedicated to advancing computer vision research in sports video understanding. This paper describes each task and its evaluation protocol, presents the challenge leaderboards, and summarizes the leading submissions, with the aim of documenting the current state of each task as measured on held-out challenge data.

### [68] [BUS: Brain-Inspired Unsupervised Self-Reflection for Advanced Multimodal Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07361)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在8个基准数据集上的广泛实验表明，BUS在使用纯无标注训练数据的情况下，在多种复杂视觉任务上取得了显著优于基线的性能提升。

Abstract (英文): Current Vision-Language Models (VLMs) often struggle to handle complex visual tasks that require consistent and fine-grained reasoning. Recent methods aim to train models to facilitate self-reflective reasoning, i.e., reviewing and improving the generated reasoning. However, they require large volumes of annotated data and lack explicit reflective behavior during test time. This work aims to bridge this gap through inspiration from neuroscience. The human brain exhibits efficient backward prediction, i.e., predicting which current states are likely to precede a given future state. In this work, we first verify that mainstream VLMs can perform backward prediction, similar to the human brain. Then, we propose Brain-inspired Unsupervised Self-reflection (BUS), a label-free training framework to enhance reflective reasoning capability in challenging image analysis. BUS enables VLMs to perform backward prediction and provide explicit learning signals on data without ground-truth labels. In this way, BUS eliminates reliance on annotated data while improving reasoning performance. Notably, BUS is compatible with popular fine-tuning methods, such as Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL). Finally, extensive experiments on 8 benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of BUS across a wide range of complex visual tasks. It achieves notable improvements over the base model while using only unlabeled training data. Our experimental findings validate that backward prediction capability is critical for VLM reasoning.

### [69] [MMAgent-R$^2$: Learning to Rerank and Reject for Agentic mRAG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07383)
*Tao Zhang,Ziqi Zhang,Zongyang Ma,Yuxin Yang,Bing Li,Chunfeng Yuan,Kang Rong,Fengyun Rao,Jing Lyu,Weiming Hu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MMAgent-R²，一个基于智能体的多模态RAG框架，通过视觉重排序和主动拒绝机制解决KB-VQA中视觉相似实体难以区分的问题，在InfoSeek等数据集上达到SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有mRAG方法依赖全局视觉特征匹配知识库实体，当存在大量视觉相似实体时，检索器难以区分，导致错误传播至最终答案。

Method: 提出MMAgent-R²框架，包含两个内部验证机制：1）视觉重排序直接比较查询与候选图像以捕捉细粒度区分性细节；2）主动拒绝丢弃不可靠结果并检索额外候选。设计复合奖励函数，通过GRPO训练联合优化外部检索、内部验证和答案生成。

Result: 在InfoSeek、E-VQA、MMhops数据集上达到SOTA性能，在挑战性检索场景和多图像多跳推理任务中优势显著。

Conclusion: 主动拒绝机制突破了固定候选集的限制，视觉重排序有效区分视觉相似实体，两者结合显著提升了KB-VQA系统的鲁棒性和准确性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域存在大量视觉相似的地物类别（如不同植被类型、建筑风格），可借鉴视觉重排序机制对遥感检索结果进行细粒度排序；主动拒绝机制可用于遥感变化检测中，当候选变化区域置信度不足时主动请求更多时相数据。

Abstract (英文): Knowledge-based Visual Question Answering (KB-VQA) requires models to retrieve visual entities matching the query image from large-scale encyclopedic knowledge bases and answer related questions. Existing multimodal Retrieval Augmented Generation (mRAG) methods rely on global visual features to match candidate entities, yet when the knowledge base contains numerous visually similar entities, the retriever struggles to distinguish them, populating the candidate set with visually similar but factually mismatched distractors. Since subsequent processing steps such as noise filtering are also confined to this fixed candidate set, errors from failed retrieval inevitably propagate to the final answer. To address these challenges, we propose MMAgent-R$^2$, an agentic mRAG framework that integrates visual reranking and active rejection as its internal verification mechanism. Visual reranking directly compares query and candidate images, capturing discriminative details beyond textual descriptions to precisely identify the target entity among similar candidates; active rejection discards unreliable results and retrieves additional candidates when no confident match is found, moving beyond the fixed candidate pool. We design a composite reward function with step-level verification rewards and achieve joint optimization of external retrieval, internal verification, and answer generation via GRPO training. Experiments on InfoSeek, E-VQA, and MMhops demonstrate that \ours{} achieves state-of-the-art performance, with particularly notable advantages in challenging retrieval scenarios and complex multi-image multi-hop reasoning tasks.

### [70] [VCDP: Variation-Conditioned Distributional Proxy Learning for Semi-Supervised Medical Image Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07416)
*Zimu Zhang,Yiheng Zhong,Zhuoru Zhang,Yingzhen Hu,Yanan He,Fanliang Meng,Xiaofeng Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种即插即用的训练时正则化模块VCDP，通过为每个类别学习高斯分布和多个变体原型，实现特征空间的结构化组织，提升半监督3D医学图像分割在复杂解剖结构上的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有半监督3D医学图像分割方法（如一致性正则化、伪标签、协同训练）在预测层面提升了鲁棒性，但缺乏特征空间的结构化组织，难以处理解剖结构复杂、器官小、边界模糊且类内变异大的情况。

Method: VCDP为每个类别学习一个可训练的高斯分布（共享类别语义）和多个变体原型（捕捉细粒度类内模式），并提出变体条件兼容性分数，融合分布相似性和软变体聚合，引导体素嵌入同时对齐全局器官身份和局部解剖变异。该模块在训练时附加在解码器特征上，推理时移除。

Result: 在多器官分割基准上，VCDP提升了多数评估基线方法的性能，尤其在小器官、边界模糊和变异大的器官上效果显著。

Conclusion: VCDP作为一种无额外推理开销的即插即用模块，有效改善了半监督3D医学图像分割的特征空间组织，解决了复杂解剖结构的分割难题。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像分割同样面临小目标（如车辆、船只）、边界模糊（如建筑物与阴影过渡区）及类内变异大（不同地物类型在同一类别中形态差异大）等问题。可将VCDP迁移至半监督遥感图像分割，具体方案：1) 为各地物类别建立高斯分布和变体原型，如将"建筑"类细分为不同密度/形状的子原型；2) 变体条件兼容性分数可处理遥感中典型的光谱-空间域分布差异；3) 替代方案：若遥感特征差异较大，可将高斯分布替换为von Mises-Fisher分布以适应方向性特征。

Abstract (英文): Semi-supervised 3D medical image segmentation reduces the need for dense voxel-level annotations by exploiting unlabeled volumes. Although existing methods such as consistency regularization, pseudo-labeling, and co-training improve prediction-level robustness, they often provide insufficient feature-space organization for anatomically complex structures, especially small organs and ambiguous boundary regions with large intra-class variations. To address this issue, we propose Variation-Conditioned Distributional Proxy Learning (VCDP), a plug-and-play training-only regularization module for semi-supervised 3D medical image segmentation. VCDP represents each class with a learnable Gaussian distribution for shared class semantics and multiple variation prototypes for fine-grained intra-class patterns. A unified variation-conditioned compatibility score is further formulated to fuse distributional similarity and soft variation aggregation, guiding voxel embeddings to align with both global organ identity and local anatomical variations. VCDP is attached to decoder features during training and removed during inference, introducing no additional inference cost. Experiments on multi-organ segmentation benchmarks show that VCDP improves most evaluated baselines, particularly for small, ambiguous, and highly variable organs. Our anonymous code is released at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/VCDP_code-41ED.

### [71] [Two-Stage Multi-Modal Fusion with Adaptive Alignment for Action Quality Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07438)
*Kanglei Zhou,Ruizhi Cai,Xinning Wang,Yijian Zheng,Liyuan Wang,Jianguo Li,Xiaohui Liang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出DualAlign，一个两阶段多模态融合框架，通过自适应对齐解决动作质量评估中跨模态错位和融合不稳定问题，并引入MM-JDM数据集作为多模态运动质量评估基准。实验表明该方法在多个基准上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AQA方法中，多模态输入存在跨模态错位和融合不稳定问题，且多模态标注成本高导致数据集多样性不足。本文旨在解决这些挑战，实现更鲁棒的多模态融合。

Method: 提出两阶段多模态融合框架DualAlign：第一阶段通过最大化RGB视频、光流和骨骼模态间的共享结构信息构建一致的视觉表征；第二阶段在视觉表征稳定后引入文本语义，使高层描述补充而非扭曲视觉流形。同时构建了包含自然模态噪声、类别不平衡和标签稀缺的MM-JDM评估数据集。

Abstract (英文): Action Quality Assessment (AQA) aims to evaluate how well a person performs a movement, which is essential in applications such as sports scoring, skill assessment, and healthcare. However, unimodal approaches often struggle to capture subtle cues of movement quality in real-world settings. Although multi-modal inputs provide complementary information, existing methods still face two major challenges: heterogeneous modalities often lead to cross-modal misalignment and unstable fusion, and reliable multi-modal annotation is costly, resulting in limited dataset diversity. To address these challenges, we propose DualAlign, a two-stage multi-modal fusion framework with adaptive alignment. The framework first constructs a coherent visual representation by maximizing shared structural information across RGB video, optical flow, and skeleton modalities. Textual semantics are then incorporated after visual stabilization, allowing high-level descriptions to complement rather than distort the underlying visual manifold. To evaluate the framework under realistic multi-modal conditions, we introduce MM--JDM, a movement-quality assessment dataset integrating RGB videos, optical flow, skeleton sequences, and structured text. MM--JDM naturally exhibits modality noise, class imbalance, and label scarcity, making it a challenging benchmark for studying multi-modal fusion and alignment. Extensive experiments show that DualAlign improves average correlation on MM--JDM by 21.16% over the state-of-the-art methods and achieves gains of 3.53% and 5.95% on the RG and Fis-V benchmarks, respectively. DualAlign also remains robust under missing-modality and label-scarce conditions.

### [72] [A Theory of Contrastive Learning with Natural Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07470)
*Antonio Torralba,Yair Weiss*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文通过理论分析证明了在简单增强和静止统计图像数据集上，对比学习的最优表示可以通过第一层为正弦滤波器、后接逐点非线性、全局平均池化和部分白化线性层的CNN实现，并提出了一个基于数据集功率谱的注水算法来计算最优频率和权重。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究为什么使用简单图像和增强的对比学习能够为下游任务学习到有用的表示，从理论角度给出解释。

Method: 通过解析计算对比损失的最优表示，利用图像数据集的静止统计特性，推导出最优CNN架构的参数形式，并提出基于功率谱的注水算法。

Result: 证明了最优第一层滤波器为正弦波，更复杂的增强下仍保持正弦形式；CNN通过SGD训练能经验性地学习到第一层的正弦滤波器和部分白化操作。

Conclusion: 对比学习在简单增强下的有效性可归结为学习到数据集频域结构（功率谱）并进行部分白化，这为理解对比学习的工作机制提供了理论基础。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像通常具有丰富的空间频率特征（如地物纹理、边缘、周期性结构），本文提出的基于功率谱的注水算法可直接用于设计遥感对比学习中的最优数据增强策略和网络初始化。具体方案：(1) 利用遥感图像的多波段功率谱特征设计频域增强策略；(2) 将正弦滤波器的理论最优解作为遥感CNN第一层的预初始化权重，加速收敛；(3) 针对遥感图像的非静止统计特性（如不同地物类型具有不同频谱），扩展本文理论到局部频谱分析框架。

Abstract (英文): Why does contrastive learning with simple images and augmentations yield useful representations for downstream tasks? We address this question by analytically computing the optimal representation in terms of a contrastive loss for a range of basic augmentations and any image dataset with stationary statistics. We show that for certain augmentations the optimum can be attained by a CNN whose first layer filters are sinusoids, followed by a pointwise nonlinearity, global average pooling, and a final linear layer that performs partial whitening. We also show that the optimal weights in such CNNs for more complicated augmentations are still sinusoids. The frequencies of the sinusoids and their weights can be computed using a simple waterfilling algorithm given the dataset's expected power spectrum. Experiments with different image datasets and augmentations show that such CNNs trained with SGD empirically learn sinusoids in their first layer and to perform partial whitening

</details>


### [73] [Discovering Geometric Biases in 3D Face Reconstruction: A Curvature-Aware Spectral Framework for Fairness Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07486)
*Veronika Shilova,Emmanuel Malherbe,Giovanni Palma,Panagiotis-Alexandros Bokaris,Laurent Risser,Jean-Michel Loubes*

Abstract (英文): 3D Morphable Models (3DMMs) remain the standard parametric shape priors for many state-of-the-art 3D face reconstruction algorithms. However, as these models are derived from a finite number of 3D face samples, they inherit the morphological biases of their training data, potentially limiting their generalizability across diverse global populations. In this paper, we propose a novel framework to analyze 3DMM reconstructions through the lens of surface curvature, with the objective to discover, quantify and visualize biases. While standard evaluation metrics often rely on Euclidean distances, our reconstruction error captures subtle surface nuances such as local topology or undulations. To do so, we leverage the Laplace-Beltrami Operator (LBO) to generate high-resolution curvature error maps, providing a localized and geometrically meaningful visualization of discrepancies between ground truth faces and reconstructed meshes. We derive from it an error metric that we validated through a user study, observing a significantly higher correlation to human perception compared to traditional methods. Furthermore, we conduct extensive experiments across several 3DMM bases and fitting algorithms, uncovering systematic age-related biases and providing preliminary evidence of biases associated with gender and ethnicity. Our findings highlight the necessity of adopting curvature-aware evaluation protocols to ensure demographic fairness and geometric precision in future 3D face reconstruction research.

Main category: cs.CV

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计一个双向交叉注意力机制，在潜在空间中对可变形形状特征与图像纹理特征进行融合，使每种模态能够基于时空对应关系自适应地加权另一种模态；同时模型动态调整不同心脏相位下形状与纹理表示的贡献权重，而非均匀加权。

Result: 在电影心脏磁共振视频数据集上实现了最先进的分类性能，并通过注意力机制识别出诊断关键的心动周期相位及模态贡献，提升了模型可解释性。

Conclusion: 提出的跨模态双向交叉注意力融合策略有效解决了形状与纹理特征简单拼接的局限性，动态时序加权机制优于均匀加权方法，为心脏视频分类提供了更优的性能与可解释性。

Abstract (英文): Deformable shape representations have proven to be robust complements to texture features in cardiac image classification, offering geometric priors that are invariant to imaging artifacts and intensity variations. However, existing deep networks perform simple concatenation to combine these distinct feature representations, which neither fully exploits their complementary nature nor learns cross-modal feature dependencies. Furthermore, this results in uniform attention across all timepoints; hence ignoring the varying diagnostic importance across the cardiac phases. In this paper, we propose a novel cardiac video classification model that, for the first time, learns temporal features in an integrated space of deformable shape and image texture representations. In particular, we design a bi-directional cross-attention in the latent space to fuse latent deformable shape and image features, allowing each modality to adaptively weight the other based on spatio-temporal correspondence. In contrast to current methods that apply uniform weighting across all the cardiac phases, our approach learns to dynamically adjust the contributions of shape and texture representations, derived from images, over time. We demonstrate state-of-the-art classification performance on a cine cardiac magnetic resonance (CMR) video dataset, achieving improved interpretability from attention mechanisms that identify diagnostically critical cardiac phases and modality contributions.

### [75] [Context-Aware Slum Mapping in Sub-Saharan Africa Using Sentinel-1 Texture and Local Climate Zones](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07532)

Conclusion: 融合SAR衍生特征可在数据稀缺环境下实现跨季节的城市形态制图一致性提升，但跨城市迁移泛化能力有限，需要本地适应性调整策略。

Abstract (英文): Accurate mapping of informal settlements remains a major challenge in Sub-Saharan African (SSA) cities because optical imagery often fails to distinguish Informal Settlements (defined here as LCZ 7) from spectrally similar formal Compact Low-Rise areas (LCZ 3). This study presents a context-aware, reproducible Optical-SAR framework that improves informal settlement delineation using Sentinel-2 spectral features and Sentinel-1 structural information within an adapted Local Climate Zone (LCZ) taxonomy. We implement a three-tier SAR integration strategy: calibrated backscatter, GLCM textures, and a physics-guided feature engineered to capture the high structural disorder and weak radar return characteristic of SSA informal settlements. Using reference data across Nairobi and Eldoret (Kenya), we evaluate performance via a stratified hold-out protocol and a season-aware ablation study. Results show that SAR textures provide the dominant performance gain for LCZ 7 detection. The Optical-SAR model achieves overall accuracy of 0.816 (dry) and 0.807 (wet), significantly outperforming the WUDAPT baseline (OA 0.704) and reducing the critical LCZ 3 - LCZ 7 confusion to 7%. Seasonal analysis indicates that while optical-only separability varies with phenology, SAR-derived textures stabilize informal settlement mapping across seasons. These findings demonstrate that the incorporation of SAR-derived features yields consistent improvements for urban morphology mapping in data-scarce environments across seasons and across the evaluated source cities, while cross-city transfer remains limited without local adaptation strategies.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用冻结的I-JEPA嵌入训练已知生成器分类器；基于能量函数进行OOD拒绝（检测未知生成器）；将拒绝样本的投影I-JEPA特征与法医自描述符（Forensic Self-Descriptors）融合后聚类，发现未知生成器组；将发现阶段扩展到增量场景，处理随时间到达的拒绝样本。

Abstract (英文): Recent advances in generative Artificial Intelligence have made synthetic face images increasingly realistic, creating new challenges for multimedia forensics. Source attribution methods should not only identify the generator of an image when the source is known, but also handle samples produced by previously unseen models. However, most existing approaches address synthetic face attribution in a closed-set setting, where all possible generators are available during training. This assumption does not hold in real-world scenarios, where new generators continuously appear and rejected samples should be organized rather than simply discarded. In this work we propose a pipeline for open-set synthetic face source attribution that combines known generator classification, energy-based OOD rejection, and unknown generator discovery. A classifier is trained on known generators using frozen I-JEPA embeddings, while rejected samples are represented by combining projected I-JEPA features with Forensic Self-Descriptors and then clustered to discover groups of unknown generators. We also extend the discovery stage to an incremental scenario, where rejected samples arrive over time. Experiments on the WILD dataset show that the proposed method achieves 96.73% closed-set attribution accuracy. In the open-set setting, energy-based rejection reaches 71.25% balanced accuracy, while rejected samples are clustered into meaningful unknown-generator groups, obtaining an ARI of 0.81, an NMI of 0.90, and an overall clustering purity of 87.74%. In the incremental setting, the discovered generator space is progressively extended while maintaining a final purity of 99.23%. Cross-dataset experiments suggest that the pipeline can operate beyond the original dataset distribution, although post-processing remains challenging.

### [78] [AA-ViT: Anatomically Aware Vision Transformer with Structural and Frequency Guidance for Contrast Enhanced Brain MRI Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07553)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在BraTS 2021数据集上，PSNR和SSIM均优于现有方法；19例不同胶质瘤病例的临床评估平均得分为3.94/5（满分5分）。

Conclusion: 所提方法可合成高质量的增强MRI图像，降低扫描成本、缩短成像时间、避免钆对比剂风险，并获得了初步的临床验证。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感影像中同样存在因天气、光照或传感器限制导致的对比度不足问题，且常需多模态融合。可将AA-ViT的频率-结构引导策略迁移至遥感场景：（1）SAR与光学影像的跨模态合成，替代缺失模态；（2）云遮挡情况下地表信息重建；（3）利用结构引导保持地物边界和纹理细节，避免生成模糊。需调整频域分支以适应遥感影像的多尺度特征。

Abstract (英文): Accurate tumour localization and diagnosis is a critical component of clinical care for brain cancers. Magnetic Resonance Imaging (MRI) is the most commonly used imaging modality due to its superior soft-tissue contrast. However, standard MRI often exhibits limited contrast and imaging artifacts, which necessitates the use of contrast agents to enhance lesion visibility. The administration of chemical contrast agents is not always feasible and may be contraindicated in patients with renal impairment or other health conditions. As a result, developing accurate and non-invasive contrast enhanced MRI (CEMRI) synthesis methods has clinical importance. In recent years, numerous approaches for CEMRI synthesis have been proposed, predominantly relying on generative artificial intelligence models. While these methods demonstrate promising performance, their dependence on implicit feature learning often limits their ability to preserve anatomical boundaries and tumour-specific fine structures. To address these challenges, we propose an anatomically aware frequency-and-structure-guided vision transformer (AA-ViT), for CEMRI synthesis using pre-contrast MRI modalities (T1, T2, and FLAIR). Experiments on the BraTS 2021 dataset demonstrate that the proposed method preserves anatomical and lesion boundaries, achieving higher PSNR and SSIM than state-of-the-art approaches. Clinical evaluation by three neuroradiologists and a neurosurgeon on 19 randomly selected cases across diverse gliomas yielded a mean score of 3.94/5, providing preliminary clinical validation rarely seen in prior studies. Synthetic post-contrast scans from our model could lower scanning costs, shorten imaging time, and avoid the potential risks of using gadolinium-based contrast agents.

</details>


### [79] [Automatic Echocardiography Segmentation via Transition Probability Correlation for Stable Semantic Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07580)
*Xinran Chen,Xiyuan Wang,Guangquan Zhou,Chuan Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 针对超声心动图中斑点噪声和低信噪比导致的语义模糊和边界碎片化问题，提出了STLSF模块（包含基于窗口匹配的语义校正和语义引导的纹理增强）以及频率感知去噪预训练方法，构建了具有局部归纳偏置和长距离依赖的卷积网络，在CAMUS和EchoNet-Dynamic数据集上达到了SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超声心动图固有的斑点噪声和低信噪比导致语义特征模糊、边界不完整，严重阻碍了深度学习模型在复杂临床病例中的分割精度；此外心脏的时间运动对解剖结构识别至关重要，现有方法未能有效解决这些问题。

Method: 1) 设计了STLSF模块，包含基于窗口匹配的语义校正组件（利用局部转移概率相关性校正语义）和语义引导的纹理增强组件（缓解纹理不稳定性和语义模糊）；2) 提出频率感知去噪预训练方法，使编码器适应超声成像模式的固有先验；3) 构建了同时具备局部归纳偏置和长距离依赖的卷积网络。

Result: 在CAMUS数据集上Dice达到93.87%，HD95为3.29mm；在EchoNet-Dynamic数据集上Dice达到92.62%，HD95为2.73mm，均达到SOTA性能。

Conclusion: 所提出的STLSF模块和频率感知去噪预训练方法能有效应对超声心动图质量差带来的挑战，显著提升分割精度，验证了方法的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像同样存在斑点噪声（如SAR图像）和低信噪比导致的语义模糊与边界不连续问题。具体方案：1) STLSF模块中的窗口匹配语义校正可直接迁移至SAR图像分割，利用局部转移概率校正受噪声干扰的地物分类；2) 语义引导的纹理增强适用于遥感影像中纹理复杂区域（如城市与植被边界）的精细分割；3) 频率感知去噪预训练可改造为适应遥感图像噪声分布（如SAR相干斑噪声、光学图像大气噪声）的预训练策略。需注意遥感图像的空间尺度远大于超声心动图，窗口大小和转移概率的计算范围需相应调整。

Abstract (英文): While echocardiography is essential for cardiovascular diagnosis, inherent speckle noise and low signal-to-noise ratio often lead to ambiguous semantic features and fragmented boundaries. These limitations significantly hinder the segmentation accuracy of deep learning models in complex clinical cases. Moreover, temporal motion of the heart plays a critical role in recognizing anatomical structures. To address these challenges, we designed a STLSF module which comprises a window-matching-based semantic correction component and a semantics-guided texture enhancement component. By leveraging local transition probability correlations to correct semantics and employing semantics-guided texture enhancement, the STLSF module effectively mitigates texture instability and ambiguous semantic interpretations caused by disadvantaged echocardiography quality. Additionally, to facilitate the encoder's adaptation to the intrinsic priors of ultrasound-specific imaging patterns, we propose a frequency-aware denoising pre-training method. The entire work builds a convolution-based network with locality inductive bias and long-range dependencies. Extensive experiments confirm our SOTA performance, achieving 93.87\% Dice on CAMUS and 92.62\% on EchoNet-Dynamic, with respective HD95 values of 3.29mm and 2.73mm.

</details>


### [80] [Cardiac MRI Through-Plane Super-Resolution Guided by Reference and Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07581)
*Shaoming Pan,Chenchuhui Hu,Leon Axel,Meng Ye*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: STRMSR是一种利用同一受试者的高分辨率参考视图和中间超分辨率结果作为记忆的参考与记忆引导的贯穿平面超分辨率框架，通过粗到细的上下文匹配和学习型动态特征聚合模块，在4倍和8倍上采样因子下显著提升了心脏MRI三维体积的重建质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床心脏MRI通常采集时具有高平面内分辨率但粗贯穿平面分辨率，这限制了三维分析和诊断准确性。现有方法缺乏有效利用同一受试者多视图信息及保证切片间一致性的手段。

Method: 提出STRMSR框架，包含：(1) 粗到细的上下文匹配建立低分辨率目标与参考/记忆图像间的鲁棒对应；(2) 可学习的逐块动态特征聚合模块，预测内容自适应混合权重以融合动态信息并抑制不可靠特征传输；(3) 记忆库存储中间SR结果以确保超分辨三维体积的切片间一致性。

Result: 在WHS心脏MRI数据集上，采用正交平面视图和长轴腔视图两种参考协议，在4倍和8倍上采样因子下均一致优于基线方法。

Conclusion: STRMSR能有效利用参考视图和中间记忆实现高质量的心脏MRI贯穿平面超分辨率，提升三维重建的切片间一致性和整体图像质量。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。方案：(1) 遥感图像中多角度/多时相影像可类比参考视图，用于超分辨率重建；(2) 粗到细上下文匹配可处理遥感图像中由于视角或时间差异导致的几何形变；(3) 记忆库机制可用于遥感时序数据处理，保证相邻时相重建结果的一致性；(4) 动态特征融合模块可适应遥感影像中地物类型的空间异质性，实现自适应特征加权融合。

Abstract (英文): Clinical cardiac MRI is commonly acquired with high in-plane resolution but coarse through-plane resolution to reduce scan time and accommodate breath-hold and cardiac-motion constraints, which limits 3D analysis and diagnostic accuracy. We propose STRMSR, a reference- and memory-guided through-plane super-resolution (SR) framework that reconstructs high-resolution (HR) cardiac volumes by leveraging HR reference views acquired from the same subject and intermediate SR results as the memory. Our method uses coarse-to-fine contextual matching to establish robust correspondence between low-resolution target and reference/memory images under spatial misalignment. A learnable patch-wise dynamic feature aggregation module predicts content-adaptive mixture weights for each local patch, effectively fusing dynamic information while suppressing unreliable feature transfers. The intermediate SR results stored in the memory bank ensure slice-to-slice consistency for the super-resolved 3D volume. Experiments on the WHS cardiac MRI dataset under two reference protocols, orthogonal-plane views and long-axis chamber views, demonstrate consistent improvements over baselines at 4x and 8x upsampling factors.

</details>


### [81] [MedPMC: A Systematic Framework for Scaling High-Fidelity Medical Multimodal Data for Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07673)
*Hyunjae Kim,Dain Kim,Pan Xiao,Serina S. Applebaum,Younjoon Chung,Xuguang Ai,Yu Yin,Roy Jiang,Yuexi Du,Yawen Wei,Yiming Kong,Tuo Guo,Zhiyuan Cao,Mengmeng Du,Yuelei Fu,Yan Hu,Rui Shi,Gui Yang,Kevin W. Jin,Yuntian Liu,Yuxuan Tian,Jonathan Marquez,Zhen Chen,Sheng Zhang,Hoifung Poon,Hua Xu,Jaewoo Kang,Qingyu Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MedPMC 是一个自动化、可持续更新的框架，从 PMC 文献中提取高质量医学图像-文本对，用于训练多模态基础模型。从 610 万篇论文中筛选出 1100 万对数据，经专家审核医学相关性达 95.3%，训练出的 CLIP 模型在 26 个基准上平均零样本 AUC 提升 7.1 个百分点，并在临床皮肤科照片检索等任务中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医学多模态基础模型因缺乏大规模、高质量、临床可验证的数据而进展受限。现有从 PubMed Central 提取的数据集在保真度、可复现性和临床验证方面存在不足，亟需一种高保真、可自动更新的数据基础设施。

Method: 提出了 MedPMC 自动化框架，包含初始筛选（F1=93.2）、多面板图像检测（F1=96.5）、图像分割（mAP=89.8）、标题分离与对齐（F1=81.4; ROUGE-L=85.3）以及医学图像分类（F1=96.5）等组件。对 610 万篇 PMC 论文进行处理，最终获得 1100 万医学图像-文本对，并由五名标注员（三人有医学背景）进行人工审核。

Result: 1) MedPMC 图像医学相关性达 95.3%（先前数据集仅 19.7%）；2) 在 26 个跨 11 个专科的基准上，MedPMC 训练的 CLIP 模型零样本 AUC 平均提升 7.1 个百分点，且使用不到一半的训练数据；3) 作为多模态大语言模型的视觉编码器，在医疗视觉问答任务上分别提升 1.9 和 16.9 个百分点；4) 在耶鲁纽黑文健康系统 10,524 张皮肤科照片的形态学-图像检索中 Recall@5 提升 11.7 个百分点。

Conclusion: 高保真的文献数据筛选能够显著强化医学多模态基础模型在基准测试和临床应用上的表现。框架、数据集、基准和预训练模型均已公开释放。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。遥感领域同样面临海量多源异构数据（卫星影像、SAR、光谱数据等）的标注难题。借鉴 MedPMC 的思路，可从遥感学术文献（如 IEEE GRSL、Remote Sensing of Environment）中自动提取图像-文本对：1) 利用多面板检测与分割技术处理复合图（如对比不同传感器的影像）；2) 通过图注分离与对齐提取语义描述；3) 构建高保真的遥感多模态训练数据集，用于遥感 CLIP/视觉-语言模型的预训练，提升零样本场景分类、目标检测与检索能力。

Abstract (英文): Medicine is inherently multimodal, requiring clinicians to synthesize information across diverse data streams. Yet the development of multimodal foundation models is constrained by limited access to large-scale, high-quality clinical data. Although PubMed Central (PMC) offers a complementary source of expert-authored image-text data, existing PMC-derived resources remain limited in fidelity, reproducibility, and clinical validation. We introduce MedPMC, an automated, continuously updatable framework that transforms permissively licensed literature into high-fidelity infrastructure for medical multimodal models. Applied to 6.1 million PMC articles, MedPMC curated 11 million medical image-text pairs. Component evaluations showed strong performance for initial screening (F1 = 93.2), multi-panel figure detection (F1 = 96.5), figure separation (mAP = 89.8), caption separation and alignment (F1 = 81.4; ROUGE-L = 85.3), and medical figure classification (F1 = 96.5). Manual review by five annotators, three with medical training, found 95.3% of MedPMC images medically relevant, versus 19.7% in a prior PMC-derived dataset. Across 26 benchmarks spanning 11 specialties, a MedPMC-trained CLIP-style model improved average zero-shot AUC by 7.1 percentage points over the strongest architecture-matched biomedical CLIP baseline despite using fewer than half as many image-text pairs. As the vision encoder in a multimodal large language model, it improved medical visual question-answering by 1.9 and 16.9 percentage points across two benchmarks. In 10,524 Yale New Haven Health System dermatology photographs, it improved morphology-to-image retrieval Recall@5 by 11.7 percentage points. These findings show that high-fidelity literature curation strengthens medical multimodal foundation models across benchmark and clinical settings. We publicly release the framework, corpus, benchmarks, and pretrained models.

### [82] [Scaling Mixture-of-Experts Video Pretraining for Embodied Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07675)
*Shuailei Ma,Jiaqi Liao,Xinyang Wang,Jingjing Wang,Chaoran Feng,Zijing Hu,Chong Bao,Zichen Xi,Yuqi Gan,Weisen Wang,Yanhong Zeng,Qin Zhao,Zifan Shi,Wei Wu,Hao Ouyang,Qiuyu Wang,Shangzhan Zhang,Jiahao Shao,Yipengjing Sun,Liangxiao Hu,Lunke Pan,Nan Xue,Kecheng Zheng,Yinghao Xu,Xing Zhu,Yujun Shen,Ka Leong Cheng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LingBot-Video是一个基于DiT的MoE视频预训练模型，专门面向具身智能，通过架构、数据和训练三方面改进，弥合视频生成与机器人控制之间的领域差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频生成模型主要用于内容创作，注重视觉保真度和创意，但在计算效率和物理真实性方面不足，难以直接用于机器人控制。亟需一个面向具身智能的视频基础模型。

Method: 架构上采用MoE替代密集注意力机制，平衡建模能力与推理效率；数据上构建数据画像引擎，增强机器人操作、导航和第一人称视角视频；训练上设计多维奖励系统，对齐物理合理性和任务完成度。

Result: 综合评估验证了LingBot-Video作为视频基础模型的性能和效率，是首个大规模开源MoE视频基础模型。

Conclusion: LingBot-Video成功弥合了数字创意与物理执行之间的鸿沟，为具身智能提供了专用的视频预训练范式。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。遥感视频分析（如变化检测、目标追踪）可借鉴其MoE架构提升效率；其数据画像引擎可扩展遥感领域（如卫星视频中的运动模式、灾害监测）；多维奖励系统可用于遥感视频生成的质量评估，但需重新设计物理合理性的度量标准以适应遥感场景。

Abstract (英文): Despite the recent promise in robot control, video generative models suffer from a domain mismatch due to their primary focus on content creation. For example, their design inherently prioritizes visual fidelity and creativity over computational efficiency and physical realism. In this work, we present LingBot-Video, a DiT-based video pretraining paradigm specifically tailored for embodied intelligence. From the architecture perspective, we adopt the Mixture-of-Experts (MoE), instead of dense, framework to achieve a better trade-off between modeling capacity and inference efficiency, and manage to scale it up from scratch. From the data perspective, we construct a data profiling engine that augments standard internet videos with extensive robot-oriented footage, encompassing manipulation, navigation, and egocentric perspectives, to equip the base model with an intrinsic understanding of actions and world dynamics. From the training perspective, we develop a multi-dimensional reward system to enforce the alignment regarding physical rationality and task completion, going beyond standard criteria such as aesthetics, prompt-following, and motion consistency. Comprehensive evaluations validate its performance and efficiency as a video foundation model. We contribute LingBot-Video as the inaugural large-scale, open-source MoE video foundation model to the community, in a pioneering effort to bridge digital creativity and physical actuation.

</details>

### [86] [PoseIDON: 6DoF pose estimation with foundation model features for marine sediment burial mapping](https://doi.org/10.1016/j.isprsjprs.2026.06.032)
*Jerry Yan,Chinmay Talegaonkar,Nicholas Antipa,Eric Terrill,Sophia Merrifield*

Main category: ISPRS J P&RS

TL;DR: 本文提出PoseIDON计算机视觉管线，结合深度基础模型特征与多视图摄影测量，从ROV视频中估计物体六自由度姿态及周围海床方向，通过CAD模型对齐和局部海床平面拟合推断掩埋深度。在San Pedro Basin历史海洋倾倒场的54个物体（包括桶和弹药）上验证，平均掩埋深度误差约10厘米，可反映沉积物输运过程的空间掩埋模式，实现可扩展的非侵入式海床掩埋测绘。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 海床上人造物体的掩埋状态对于评估局部沉积动态、生态风险、污染物迁移以及危险材料（如弹药）的回收或缓解策略至关重要。然而，由于部分遮挡、能见度差和物体退化，从遥感图像准确估计掩埋深度仍然困难，亟需一种非侵入式、可扩展的解决方案。

Method: 提出PoseIDON管线，结合深度基础模型特征与多视图摄影测量，从ROV视频中估计物体的六自由度（6DoF）姿态和海床方向。通过将物体CAD模型与观测图像对齐，并拟合海床局部平面近似来推断掩埋深度。

Result: 在San Pedro Basin历史海洋倾倒场的54个物体（包括桶和弹药）上验证，平均掩埋深度误差约10厘米，并能解析反映底层沉积物输运过程的空间掩埋模式。

Conclusion: 该方法实现了可扩展的非侵入式海床掩埋测绘，支持污染场地的环境评估，为理解局部沉积动力学和危险材料管理提供了有效工具。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该方法的计算机视觉管线可直接迁移至遥感领域的海岸带浅水区人工目标（如沉船、管道、水下设施）掩埋状态监测。具体改进方案：(1) 将ROV视频替换为无人机或卫星多视角遥感影像，结合水深反演模型适配光学遥感数据；(2) 引入多光谱/高光谱特征增强基础模型对水下目标的识别能力；(3) 针对大范围海床场景，采用卫星遥感影像生成数字表面模型（DSM）替代局部平面近似，提升掩埋深度估计的空间覆盖范围；(4) 结合合成孔径雷达（SAR）穿透能力，验证在浑浊水体中的适用性。

Abstract (英文): The burial state of anthropogenic objects on the seafloor provides insight into localized sedimentation dynamics and is also critical for assessing ecological risks, potential pollutant transport, and the viability of recovery or mitigation strategies for hazardous materials such as munitions. Accurate burial depth estimation from remote imagery remains difficult due to partial occlusion, poor visibility, and object degradation. This work introduces a computer vision pipeline, called PoseIDON, which combines deep foundation model features with multiview photogrammetry to estimate six degrees of freedom object pose and the orientation of the surrounding seafloor from ROV video. Burial depth is inferred by aligning CAD models of the objects with observed imagery and fitting a local planar approximation of the seafloor. The method is validated using footage of 54 objects, including barrels and munitions, recorded at a historic ocean dumpsite in the San Pedro Basin. The model achieves a mean burial depth error of approximately 10 cm and resolves spatial burial patterns that reflect underlying sediment transport processes. This approach enables scalable, non-invasive mapping of seafloor burial and supports environmental assessment at contaminated sites.

</details>

### [87] [AgentLens: Production-Assessed Trajectory Reviews for Coding Agent Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06624)
*Andrey Podivilov,Vadim Lomshakov,Sergey Savin,Matvei Startsev,Roman Pozharskiy,Maksim Parshin,Sergey Nikolenko*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AgentLens 是一个面向交互式代码智能体的生产级基准测试，通过对完整运行轨迹（指令遵循、工具使用、自我验证、错误恢复、用户交互）进行形式化验证与 LLM 评审，提供可解释的评分，可用于诊断模型行为、比较代理版本及捕捉产品回归。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码智能体基准测试仅以单比特（成功/失败）评估任务结果，忽略了实际使用中用户所经历的完整轨迹（如指令遵循、工具使用、自我验证、错误恢复及交互过程），缺乏对智能体行为过程的细粒度评估与可解释性。

Method: AgentLens 结合形式化验证（存在客观检查时）与 LLM 生成的轨迹评审及两两对比，为每次运行提供可读的评分解释。通过生产环境中的夜间评估流水线，对智能体行为进行诊断、版本间比较及产品回归检测。

Result: 成功构建了一个不仅可用于模型排名，更能诊断模型行为、比较代理迭代版本及捕获产品回归的生产级基准测试，并以开源形式发布。

Conclusion: AgentLens 通过完整的轨迹级评估与可解释评分，弥补了现有代码智能体基准测试仅评估结果二值的缺陷，为实际生产环境中的智能体开发与迭代提供了更有价值的诊断工具。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。具体方案：遥感领域中代码智能体（如自动化遥感图像处理、地理空间分析）的评估可借鉴 AgentLens 的轨迹级评估框架。1）将遥感任务（如影像分割、变化检测、目标识别）分解为多步操作（数据加载、预处理、模型推理、后处理、结果验证），使用 AgentLens 评估智能体每一步的工具使用与指令遵循情况；2）结合地理空间验证（如精度指标、位置准确性）作为形式化验证，辅以 LLM 对中间结果（如处理流程合理性、参数选择）进行轨迹评审；3）用于诊断遥感智能体在处理复杂流程（多时相影像配准、多源数据融合）时的错误恢复与自我验证能力，提升自动化遥感分析系统的可靠性。

Abstract (英文): We present AgentLens, a production-assessed benchmark for interactive code agents. Most code-agent benchmarks reduce a run to a single bit -- did the task pass? -- but the people who actually use these agents experience the entire trajectory: how the agent follows instructions, uses its tools, verifies its own work, recovers from mistakes, and talks to them along the way. AgentLens evaluates that whole trajectory. It pairs formal verification, where an objective check exists, with LLM-written trajectory reviews and side-by-side comparisons, so that each run yields a readable explanation of why the score is what it is. This makes AgentLens useful for more than ranking models: we use it to diagnose model behavior, compare successive versions of our own agent, and catch product regressions in a nightly evaluation pipeline. We release the benchmark as open source at https://github.com/agent-lens/agent-lens-bench.

</details>


### [88] [When Does In-Context Search Help? A Sampling-Complexity Theory of Reflection-Driven Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06720)
*Yotam Wolf,Noam Wies,Amnon Shashua*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文对基于推理的大语言模型（LLM）的上下文搜索（in-context search）进行理论分析，将其建模为推理轨迹上的近似推断，推导了推理时的采样复杂度，证明了当反射（self-reflection）能够准确定位早期错误时，上下文搜索能以多项式次数的尝试实现指数级性能提升，并验证了理论在真实大规模推理模型上的定性预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型通过扩展推理能力实现了上下文搜索（迭代生成、批判、修正解决方案），但这种方法的理论基础尚不明确，尤其是其采样复杂度（达到高成功概率所需的顺序尝试次数）缺乏严格的数学分析。

Method: 将上下文搜索建模为推理轨迹上的近似推断：基模型定义先验，自我反思提供后验更新的反馈。通过分析推理时的采样复杂度，研究顺序尝试次数与成功概率之间的关系。进一步分析鲁棒性（近似后验更新的充分性）、可学习性（交叉熵训练恢复所需行为）以及与强化学习中最优策略扩展的关系。

Result: 当反射能准确定位早期错误时，上下文搜索可带来指数级改进——零样本通过率呈指数小的问题只需多项式次顺序尝试即可解决；当该性质不成立时，条件化过去尝试相比并行采样无渐进优势。这些增益是鲁棒且可学习的。在真实大规模推理模型上验证了关键定性预测。

Conclusion: 上下文搜索的理论基础得以建立，其有效性依赖于反射能否可靠定位早期错误，且该增益在实践中是可获得的。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该理论分析虽针对LLM推理，但遥感领域中的复杂推理任务（如多时相变化检测、遥感链式推理问答）可直接借鉴：(1) 将遥感模型的推理过程建模为上下文搜索，利用遥感先验知识（如地物光谱、空间关系）作为先验，通过多步自我修正提升复杂场景下的推理准确性；(2) 遥感数据中标签稀缺问题可通过该理论中多项式样本复杂度的学习保证来指导主动学习策略设计；(3) 遥感领域的可验证奖励（如变化检测的像素精度）可直接对应论文中的强化学习框架，用于优化遥感推理模型的策略扩展。

Abstract (英文): Training large language models (LLMs) with extended reasoning has enabled in-context search, in which models iteratively generate, critique, and revise solution attempts. We provide a theoretical analysis of in-context search by modeling it as approximate inference over reasoning traces, where the base model defines a prior and self-reflection provides feedback for posterior updates, and study the resulting inference-time sampling complexity - the number of sequential attempts needed to achieve high success probability. We show that when reflections reliably localize early mistakes, in-context search can yield exponential improvements over the base model, solving problems with exponentially small zero-shot pass rates using only a polynomial number of sequential attempts, whereas when this property fails, conditioning on past attempts offers no asymptotic benefit over parallel sampling. We further show that these gains are robust and learnable: approximate posterior updates suffice, and cross-entropy training on search rollouts recovers the required behavior with polynomial sample complexity. Finally, we show that under a stagewise abstraction of reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards, the optimal policy extension implements the same posterior reweighting rule. We validate key qualitative predictions of the theory on real large reasoning models.

</details>


### [89] [LLM-powered reasoning in agent-based modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06757)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统ABM依赖静态先验知识，无法适应实时变化，存在信息滞后问题，亟需引入动态决策预测能力。

Method: 构建HALE（Hybrid Agent-based and Language-driven Epidemic）框架，将LLM嵌入ABM模拟中，利用LLM预测每个智能体在疫情情境下的人类决策行为，实现动态自适应仿真。

Result: 以COVID-19在犹他州盐湖县的仿真作为概念验证，展示了LLM驱动的ABM在模拟人类决策方面的可行性。

Conclusion: LLM与ABM的混合建模范式能够弥合传统静态模型与实时动态决策之间的信息鸿沟，为政策制定提供更灵活、适应性更强的仿真工具。

Abstract (英文): Agent-based modeling (ABM) has the capability to model millions of individuals and their interactions, which is useful for policy making. However, ABMs have traditionally relied on static prior, which prevents the models from adapting to real-time changes. Our research provides a novel approach to addressing this information gap. Large language models (LLMs) offer new opportunities to predict human decision-making. Here, we introduce a scalable Hybrid Agent-based and Language-driven Epidemic (HALE) modeling framework that leverages LLMs to predict human decision-making in an ABM simulation. As a proof-of-concept, we use HALE to simulate COVID-19 and its effects in Salt Lake County, UT.

### [90] [QANTIS: Hardware-Calibrated Sequential POMDP Belief Updates on IBM Heron](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06760)
*Bayram Yuksel Eker,Suayb S. Arslan,Ozgur Nazli,Mustafa Serhat Demirgil,Furkan Deligoz*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究QANTIS——一种将量子处理器作为校准信念更新服务的框架，在部分可观测的Tiger POMDP环境中，验证了其在不同量子放大方案下（无放大、Grover放大、全步固定点放大）能否在不破坏后验概率的前提下跨时间步复用。实验在IBM Heron硬件上完成，结果表明全步FPAA在8步和12步运行中保持了Tiger后验，所有决策检查中硬件后验与精确贝叶斯后验选择了相同行动。边界感知BIQAE稳定了近零和近一的幅度估计，稀有事件扫描映射了百万分之一证据的逻辑样本复杂度包络。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在部分可观测自主系统中，智能体需基于信念（而非原始传感器事件）行动。量子处理器有潜力加速信念更新中的稀有事件证据项估计，但关键问题是：量子服务能否在序列决策过程中跨时间步复用而不破坏后验质量？本文通过硬件案例研究回答这一问题，为量子增强的信念更新原语建立操作包络。

Method: 采用Tiger POMDP基准问题，在IBM Heron量子硬件上实现QANTIS框架。比较三种方案：无放大、守卫Grover放大、全步固定点放大（FPAA）。对同一轨迹在不同时间步评估后验是否改变下游动作。引入边界感知BIQAE技术稳定极端概率（近0和近1）的幅度估计，并通过稀有事件扫描映射样本复杂度包络。

Result: 全步FPAA在8步和12步主运行中成功保持Tiger后验；20步和32步控制运行保持在同一操作带内。所有决策检查中，硬件后验与精确贝叶斯后验选择相同即时行动。BIQAE稳定了近零和近一的估计，稀有事件扫描刻画了百万分之一证据的样本复杂度边界。

Conclusion: QANTIS信念更新服务可以在序列POMDP中跨时间步复用而不破坏下游决策，但当前结果是一个硬件校准信念更新原语的操作包络，而非独立的硬件优势声明。该工作为量子处理器在自主系统信念更新中的实用化提供了可行性证据。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：(1) 遥感图像解译中常面临部分可观测问题（如云遮挡、多时相不一致），QANTIS的量子信念更新可用于融合多源遥感数据中的不确定性，实现鲁棒的场景分类；(2) 目标检测与跟踪任务可建模为POMDP，利用量子加速稀有事件（如小目标、异常变化）的似然估计；(3) BIQAE技术可用于遥感变化检测中概率接近0或1的边界稳定估计，提升低概率变化事件的检测可靠性；(4) 需注意当前量子硬件规模和保真度限制，建议从简化的遥感二分类任务（如有云/无云判定）开始验证。

Abstract (英文): Autonomous systems under partial observability act on beliefs, not raw sensor events. QANTIS treats the quantum processor as a calibrated belief-update service in that loop: it receives a prior and an observation model, estimates the rare-event evidence term, and returns an ordinary posterior to a classical planner. This paper asks whether that service can be reused across a sequential Tiger POMDP horizon on present IBM Heron hardware without corrupting the planner-facing posterior. We answer with a controlled hardware case study rather than an end-to-end autonomy or wall-clock speedup claim. The study compares no amplification, guarded Grover amplification, and all-step fixed-point amplification on the same trajectory, then checks whether the returned posterior would change the downstream action. All-step FPAA preserves the Tiger posterior across the reported 8-step and 12-step primary runs, and the 20-step and 32-step controls remain inside the same operating band. In every reported decision check, the hardware posterior and the exact Bayes posterior select the same immediate action. Boundary-aware BIQAE stabilizes amplitude estimation near zero and near one, while a rare-event sweep maps the logical sample-complexity envelope for one-in-a-million evidence. The result is an operating envelope for a hardware-calibrated belief-update primitive, not a standalone hardware-advantage claim.

</details>


### [91] [Cost-Effective Agent Harnesses for Abstract Reasoning and Generalization on ARC-AGI-1](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06764)
*Kabir Moghe,Peter Chin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文探索了第三种范式：在无ARC特定微调、严格预算下，使用开源模型（DeepSeek V3.2）的非思考模式，通过纯架构设计提升ARC-AGI-1性能。提出Explorer-Definer Pipeline（两阶段智能体流水线，分离模式发现与可执行变换合成）和Reflective Orchestrator（增强自适应重探索），分别达到57.50%和67.25%的pass@2，将15.50%的基线提升约52个百分点。无偏分析表明系统受生成能力限制而非选择能力限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ARC-AGI-1进展主要依赖两种范式：一是针对前沿模型的重测试时计算（进化搜索、穷举采样、扩展思维链），二是基于基准特定训练（小模型在ARC数据上微调，常配合任务专用架构）。这两种范式均存在计算成本高、泛化性受限等问题。本文旨在探索第三种范式：使用开源模型的非思考模式，在严格预算下，不进行基准特定微调，仅通过架构设计提升抽象推理能力。

Method: 1) Explorer-Definer Pipeline：将模式发现与可执行变换合成分离为两阶段智能体流水线；2) Reflective Orchestrator：在训练对上的假设失败时，自主探索新变换来增强流水线；3) 使用无偏pass@k分析诊断系统瓶颈（生成受限vs选择受限）；4) 基于诊断预测，通过自适应重探索实现改进。

Result: 在ARC-AGI-1公开400任务评估集上，Explorer-Definer Pipeline达到57.50% pass@2（每任务$0.25），Reflective Orchestrator达到67.25% pass@2（每任务$0.62）。将15.50%的一次性基线提升约52个百分点。无偏分析表明系统是生成受限而非选择受限，训练对准确率可捕获约95%的候选上限。移除think工具导致pass@2下降5.75个百分点。

Conclusion: 通过纯架构设计（无基准特定微调、无重测试时计算），开源模型的非思考模式可以在ARC-AGI-1上达到有竞争力的性能。生成能力而非选择能力是当前瓶颈，自适应重探索可有效缓解该瓶颈。此外，think工具是流水线中的重要组件。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。1) 遥感场景中的模式发现可借鉴Explorer-Definer两阶段分离架构：第一阶段检测地物变化/异常模式（如时间序列变化检测），第二阶段生成变换规则并执行。2) Reflective Orchestrator的自适应重探索机制可用于遥感多模态融合失败时的回溯推理，如SAR与光学影像配准失败时的自适应重搜索。3) 该文诊断方法（生成受限vs选择受限）可直接迁移至遥感目标检测/分割模型的瓶颈分析。4) 注意遥感任务对推理效率有实时性要求，需权衡探索深度与计算成本。

Abstract (英文): Recent progress on ARC-AGI-1 from disclosed architectures has come broadly from two regimes: heavy test-time compute over frontier models (evolutionary search, exhaustive sampling, extended chain-of-thought), or benchmark-specific training in which small models are fine-tuned on ARC data, often with task-specialized architectures. We study a third regime: an open-weight model in non-thinking mode (DeepSeek V3.2) under a strict budget, with no ARC-specific fine-tuning. We study what is recoverable through architecture alone, building agentic harnesses that decompose pattern-discovery and program-synthesis stages explicitly. First, we introduce an Explorer-Definer Pipeline that separates pattern discovery from executable transformation synthesis, implemented as a two-stage agent pipeline. Next, we present the Reflective Orchestrator, which augments the pipeline with autonomous exploration of new transformations when previous hypotheses fail on training pairs. On the ARC-AGI-1 public 400-task evaluation set, the pipeline reaches 57.50% pass@2 at \$0.25 per task, and the orchestrator reaches 67.25% pass@2 at \$0.62 per task. Together these architectures lift a 15.50% one-shot baseline by ~52 points without benchmark-specific training or heavy test-time compute. Furthermore, the orchestrator-driven lift tests a falsifiable diagnostic the pipeline produces; unbiased pass@k analysis suggests the pipeline is generation-bound, not selection-bound (selection via training-pair accuracy captures ~95% of the candidate ceiling) and predicts that significant improvement requires broader generation, not better ranking. The orchestrator implements this prediction via adaptive re-exploration and confirms it (unbiased pass@1 lift +9.81 pp, matching selection-mediated pass@2 lift). An additional pipeline ablation identifies its think tool as a significant component, with removal reducing pass@2 by 5.75 pp.

</details>


### [92] [Evaluating SageMath-Augmented LLM Agents for Computational and Experimental Mathematics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06820)
*Pavel Snopov,German Magai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合LLM推理与SageMath计算系统的ReAct风格智能体框架，用于解决数学研究问题。在RealMath基准测试中，该方法使所有模型平均提升+9.7个百分点（最高达27.8pp），GPT-5.5达到75.2%最高求解率。同时改进了RealMath基准的后处理和验证流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI for Mathematics研究主要关注自动形式化和定理证明，而计算机代数系统(CAS)在智能体LLM工作流中的作用尚未充分探索。

Method: 提出ReAct风格智能体框架，将LLM推理与SageMath的可验证反馈相结合，并使用Context7获取最新文档。同时提出RealMath基准的改进方案，包括多步后处理和多阶段验证流程。

Result: SageMath接入带来平均+9.7pp的性能提升（范围1.5pp-27.8pp），缩小了开源与闭源模型差距。Qwen 3.7-Max受益最大，GPT-5.5达到75.2%最高求解率且token消耗最低。

Conclusion: CAS增强的智能体是辅助数学家进行计算探索的有前景方向，此工作向自动猜想发现迈出了一步。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：(1) 将SageMath替换为遥感专用计算工具（如GDAL、Orfeo ToolBox用于图像处理，或GRASS GIS用于空间分析）作为可验证反馈源；(2) 在遥感解译中构建ReAct智能体，结合LLM推理与遥感计算工具的数值反馈（如波段运算、植被指数计算、分类精度验证）；(3) Context7用于检索最新遥感数据格式和处理标准文档；(4) 多步后处理和多阶段验证流程可直接迁移至遥感产品生成的质量控制环节。

Abstract (英文): Recent advances in AI for Mathematics have focused largely on autoformalization and theorem proving, leaving the role of Computer Algebra Systems (CAS) in agentic LLM workflows underexplored. We propose a ReAct-style agentic setup that combines LLM reasoning with verifiable feedback from SageMath, together with Context7 for the up-to-date documentation. We evaluate this agentic setup across frontier models for solving research-level mathematical problems from the RealMath benchmark in a setting that emulates a computational-mathematics research loop. We also propose a refinement to the RealMath benchmark by introducing a multi-step post-processing procedure and a multi-stage validation pipeline, both of which improve the quality and reliability of the extracted problem set. Our experiments reveal substantial performance gains from SageMath access across all evaluated models on +9.7~pp on average, the gains range from 1.5~pp to 27.8~pp and narrow the gap between open-weight and closed models. Qwen~3.7-Max benefits from SageMath the most, while GPT-5.5 achieves the highest solve rate of $75.2\%$ and the lowest token usage among tool-enabled configurations. Our findings suggest that CAS-augmented agents represent a promising direction for assisting mathematicians in computational exploration, and we believe that this work is a step towards automated conjecture discovery. The project repository is available online.

### [93] [The Harness Effect: How Orchestration Design Sets the Token Economics of Enterprise Agentic AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06906)
*Muayad Sayed Ali,Aliaksandra Novik,Anji Boddupally,Artem Yavorskyi,Chris Nickerson,Daniel Rica,Emily DuGranrut,Felix Leung,Garrett Prince,Grace Barnett,Heath Robinson,Hosain Al Ahmad,Jesse Resnick,Juan Carlos Farah,Jyothi Swaroop Meruga,Leonid Kuznetsov,Luke Gorham,Marie Schmoll,Michael Paciullo,Saumya Das,Sharath Sheripally,Tommy Griscom,Mykyta Osadchyi,Neha Mantri,Nick Westrum,Olivia Benowitz,Parikshith Kulkarni,Radik Chernyshov,Rakshith Vasudev,Rohith Nadimpally,Vikas Gangadevi,Waseem AlShikh*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 通过对比实验证明，Agent编排层（Harness）相比基础模型选择对成本效率影响更大，可降低41%任务成本、44%耗时和38%token消耗，且质量持平或略升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前Agentic AI开发陷入"token maxing"困境——通过不断增加推理长度、交互轮次、工具负载和回放上下文来换取能力，导致每任务token消耗增长速度远超任务价值增长速度。虽然token单价在下降，但总支出仍在攀升。需要找到真正有效的杠杆来打破这一模式。

Method: 设计受控对比实验：固定22个评估任务和6个基础模型（Claude Sonnet 4.6、Gemini 3.1、Gemini Flash 3.5、Qwen 3.6、GLM 5.1、Palmyra X6），仅更换编排层——将传统生产循环与Writer Agent Harness对比，测量成本、耗时、token消耗和任务完成质量。

Result: Harness使混合成本降低41%（$0.21→$0.12）、中位耗时降低44%（48s→27s）、每任务token降低38%（14.2k→8.8k），任务质量持平（0.78→0.81，小幅提升但样本量不足）。质量每美元提升82%，每百万token完成任务数从54.9增至92.0。编排层对成本的影响超过整个模型菜单的跨度。

Conclusion: 编排层（Harness）是打破token maxing的决定性杠杆，其效率提升在所有模型上一致（33-61%），且质量增益与模型基础能力高度相关（r=0.99）。提出了"Harness Leverage"现象，并形式化了token经济学、六种机制族（包括缓存形状约束、失败支出治理等），认为编排层是唯一能跨所有模型（现在和未来）倍增效率的组件。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域当前也在大量使用多模态大模型进行变化检测、目标识别、图像分割等任务，同样面临token消耗暴涨的问题。具体方案：(1) 将Harness的编排架构引入遥感工作流，对多时序/多模态遥感数据的上下文组装进行智能管理，减少冗余token；(2) 利用缓存形状约束机制优化遥感大模型的高分辨率图块拼接调用；(3) 将失败支出治理机制应用于遥感检测流程，当某块检测失败时快速回退而非堆叠更多推理；(4) 针对遥感场景建立任务代价模型，类似本文的token经济学分析来评估不同编排策略的ROI。

Abstract (英文): Agentic AI development today runs on token maxing: buying capability with tokens -- longer reasoning traces, more turns, wider tool payloads, bigger replayed contexts -- so tokens per task grow faster than task value. Falling per-token prices mask the pattern; total spend rises anyway. We argue the decisive lever against token maxing is the harness: the orchestration layer that assembles context, exposes tools, sequences turns, delegates work, and carries enterprise observability and governance. We isolate it with a controlled swap: 22 locked evaluation tasks, six foundation models (Claude Sonnet 4.6, Gemini 3.1, Gemini Flash 3.5, Qwen 3.6, GLM 5.1, Palmyra X6), changing only the orchestration layer -- a frozen conventional production loop versus the Writer Agent Harness. Holding models constant, the harness cuts blended cost per task 41% ($0.21->$0.12), median wall-clock 44% (48s->27s), and tokens per task 38% (14.2k->8.8k), with task-completion quality at parity (0.78->0.81, directional at this sample size). Efficiency is model-invariant -- every model gets cheaper (33-61%) -- while quality gains are capability-dependent: a model's gain correlates almost perfectly with its baseline strength (r=0.99, n=6), a phenomenon we term harness leverage. Quality per dollar rises 82%; task-completions per million tokens rise from 54.9 to 92.0. On this workload the orchestration layer moved cost per task more than the full spread of the model menu did. We formalize token economics at the orchestration layer (including effective input price under prompt caching), detail the six mechanism families behind the effect -- cache-shape discipline to failure-spend governance -- compare six widely used agent systems on the same axes, and argue the harness is the one component whose efficiency multiplies across every model an organization runs -- present and future.

</details>


### [94] [Grounding Spatial Relations in a Compact World Model: Instruction Leakage and a Goal-Free Dynamics Fix](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06925)
*Yufeng Wang,Lu Wei,Haibin Ling*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了目标条件世界模型中的一个关键陷阱：当指令直接命名了要预测的答案时，模型会通过“指令转录”（instruction transcription）而非真正的感知来达到高准确率。通过去除指令或使用反事实指令可暴露这一问题，并提出了通过将目标排除在动态模型之外、监督读取路径的修复方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究目标条件世界模型是否真正基于感知来理解语言指令（如“将红色方块放在蓝色方块左边”），还是仅仅从指令中转录答案，而非实际理解场景中的空间关系。

Method: 通过三种测试检测指令泄漏：（1）去掉指令后准确率从0.90骤降至0.27；（2）使用反事实指令时，预测锚点跟随虚假指令的比例达94.5%，真实场景仅2.3%；（3）在桌面场景和BabyAI基准测试中验证泄漏，而Language-Table世界模型在指令命名指称物时不泄漏。修复方法：将目标从动态模型中移除（归入规划器的代价函数），并监督读取路径。

Result: 目标条件预测器达到0.90的关系读出准确率，但这是指令转录而非感知；反事实指令使预测跟随虚假指令94.5%；修复后达到0.88准确率，且有无指令结果一致。

Conclusion: 指令泄漏的核心特征是被评分的量可以从指令中转录（指令命名了答案），且与非指令输入的预测能力基本无关。诊断即修复：将目标从动态中移除并监督读取路径，可恢复真正的、与指令独立的感知。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域中的视觉-语言任务（如“找到建筑物南侧的水体”）可能面临同样问题：模型可能仅从指令中转录答案而非真正理解遥感影像。可引入反事实指令测试和条件消融实验来诊断泄漏；修复上可借鉴本文方法，将语言指令从视觉-语言模型的动态预测中分离，由规划器或解码器单独处理指令语义，避免监督信号泄漏。

Abstract (英文): Compact world models that condition on a language goal promise to ground relations such as ``put the red block left of the blue block'' using a sparse set of explicit \emph{reference anchors}. We ask when such references actually ground a relation, and identify a trap: a goal-conditioned predictor reaches a striking $0.90$ relation-readout accuracy, yet this is \emph{instruction transcription}, not perception. Withholding the goal collapses it to chance ($0.90\!\to\!0.27$, three seeds) and a counterfactual instruction makes the predicted anchors follow the \emph{false} instruction $94.5\%$ of the time (true scene $2.3\%$; $N{=}256$). Tested across three settings and a within-task ablation, our central claim characterizes the confound: \textbf{instruction leakage occurs when the scored quantity is transcribable from the instruction (when the instruction names the answer) and is essentially independent of how predictive the non-instruction inputs are.} Our tabletop and the external BabyAI benchmark leak, whereas a Language-Table forward-dynamics world model whose instruction names \emph{referents} does not, until the instruction is augmented to name the direction; and degrading the action never increases leakage, the opposite of what predictor-competition predicts. The diagnosis prescribes the fix: keep the goal out of the dynamics (it belongs to the planner's cost) and supervise the \emph{read} path, recovering genuine, instruction-independent grounding ($0.88$, identical with and without the goal). The detection protocol and remedy apply to any goal-conditioned world model whose instruction names the scored quantity.

</details>

*Wachiravit Modecrua,Krittin Pachtrachai,Touchapon Kraisingkorn*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出大型行为模型(LBM)，通过统一的人-环境框架从大规模零售交易中学习客户决策，在购买预测、硬负样本区分、购物篮完成、促销响应和跨域优惠券兑换等任务上优于通用大语言模型，消融实验表明持续预训练是行为泛化的主要驱动力。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Person-Environment统一公式表达客户状态（基于历史购买的行为画像）和产品上下文（检索增强生成），通过行为数据口头化的持续预训练、决策生成的监督微调、以及基于可验证奖励的强化学习三阶段训练。

Conclusion: 交易历史中编码的行为知识可以被语言模型有效学习，为构建客户数字孪生和行为仿真提供了可扩展的基础。

Abstract (英文): Customer behavior modeling underpins recommendation, marketing, and decision support, yet existing approaches either optimize predictive accuracy without explaining decisions or simulate users without grounding them in real behavioral data. We present the Large Behavioral Model (LBM) that learns customer decision making directly from large-scale retail transactions through a unified Person-Environment formulation. Customer state is represented by a behavioral profile derived from historical purchases, while product context is incorporated through retrieval-augmented generation. The model is trained using continued pre-training on verbalized behavioral data, supervised fine-tuning for decision generation, and reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards for evidence-based calibration. We evaluate the proposed framework on purchase prediction, hard-negative discrimination, basket completion, promotion response, and cross-domain voucher redemption. The model consistently outperforms frontier general-purpose language models on in-domain retail tasks while demonstrating strong zero-shot and fine-tuned transfer across retailers and decision domains. Ablation studies show that continued pre-training is the primary driver of behavioral generalization, retrieval is most effective when applied during both training and inference, and reinforcement learning improves reliance on explicit behavioral evidence over generic language-model priors. These results demonstrate that behavioral knowledge encoded in transaction histories can be effectively learned by language models, providing a scalable foundation for customer digital twins and behavior simulation.

### [96] [Learning social norms enhances compatibility in dynamic human-AI coordination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07021)
*Yi Yang,Siyuan Liu,Xin Gao,Huamu Sun,Chao Liu,Qing Zhou,Bingbing Nie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了人类与AI在动态交互中的协调问题，以行人-车辆交互为场景，从3456个动态人际交互中识别出三种社会规范原则：结果可预测性、价值对齐和优势感知。将这些原则纳入LLM智能体后，其在人机闭环交互任务中的总分比基线策略提高近四倍，并超越人际交互43%。研究表明将隐性社会规范形式化为可量化原则能显著提升人机协调效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的AI智能体（包括LLM）在与人类进行动态交互时，往往无法以有效、体贴和自然的方式协调。作者假设这是因为现有方法仅将模型行为与人类演示对齐，而没有显式量化产生行为的潜在社会规范。

Method: 以行人-车辆交互为代表性动态交互场景，开发简化实验平台收集3456个动态人际交互数据，从中识别出三项社会规范原则（结果可预测性、价值对齐、优势感知），并将其形式化后纳入LLM智能体。

Result: 社会规范感知的LLM在闭环人机交互任务中总分比基线策略提高近四倍，比人类-人类交互高出43%。

Conclusion: 将隐性社会规范形式化为显式、可量化的原则，能使AI智能体在动态交互中实现互利协调，支持其更自然地融入人类社会。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。方案：（1）遥感中的多智能体协同任务（如无人机编队、卫星自主避障）可借鉴本文三项原则——结果可预测性用于轨迹预测与冲突消解，价值对齐用于多任务目标优化，优势感知用于资源分配与决策优先级；（2）将社会规范原则形式化为损失函数或奖励信号，用于强化学习训练遥感智能体在动态环境中的协同行为；（3）可应用于遥感人机协同解译系统，使AI在标注或判读过程中更好地理解人类操作员的意图和习惯。

Abstract (英文): Humans continuously coordinate with others in dynamic interactions, often through implicit, hard-to-quantify social norms that act as shared tacit expectations among interacting agents. As AI agents, including large language models (LLMs), become embedded in daily life, they increasingly participate in such interactions and reshape social interaction structures. Yet they often fail to coordinate with humans in an effective, considerate, and natural manner. We hypothesize that this gap arises because existing approaches align model behavior with human demonstrations without explicitly quantifying the underlying norms that generate such behavior. We selected pedestrian-vehicle interaction as a representative dynamic interaction and developed a simplified experimental platform that captures its key interactive features. From 3,456 dynamic human interactions collected via this platform, we identified three principles underlying human social norms: outcome predictability, value alignment, and advantage awareness. Incorporating these principles into AI agents significantly improves human-AI coordination. In the closed-loop interaction task with humans, the social-norm-informed LLM achieved a nearly fourfold higher total score than the baseline strategy and outperformed human-human interactions by 43%. These findings indicate that formalizing tacit social norms into explicit, quantifiable principles can enable AI agents to achieve mutually beneficial coordination in dynamic interactions, supporting their more natural integration into human society.

### [97] [Measuring Intelligence Beyond Human Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07040)
*Jerry Han,Rafael Moschopoulos,Ella Colby,Vishrut Goyal,Andrew Tu,Kia Ghods,Mark Braverman,Elad Hazan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于相对测量的对抗心理测量评级系统，通过让模型生成公共挑战来区分其他系统，从而解决绝对尺度评估中超越人类能力后的智能测量难题。该系统支持无裁判裁决、抵抗私有信息攻击，并能随智能体能力自然扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统人类编写的基准测试在达到人类能力上限后会饱和，且当任务难度超越人类水平时，评估者难以知道哪些任务既困难又可验证。这种困难是绝对尺度评估固有的，因此需要新的评估范式。

Method: 提出基于相对测量的对抗心理测量评级系统：模型生成公开挑战任务来区分其他系统，通过聚合对抗评估结果形成评级。设计了具体的实用协议以降低私有信息攻击动机、支持无裁判裁决，并使其能随智能体能力自然扩展。

Result: 将框架实例化到可验证和开放式的非可验证领域，证明了模型生成的评估可以在人类前沿之外继续测量系统。

Conclusion: 相对测量范式取代绝对尺度评估，能够持续衡量超越人类能力的智能水平，为未来超人类智能的评估提供了可行的理论框架和实践协议。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该框架可应用于遥感领域的模型评估：1) 让不同遥感模型（如目标检测、变化检测、语义分割模型）相互生成挑战性遥感影像任务（如合成罕见的场景组合、对抗性噪声样本），通过相对排名评估模型鲁棒性和泛化能力；2) 在无真实标注的开放场景（如新型地物分类）中，利用模型间博弈生成可验证的评估协议；3) 解决遥感基准数据集饱和问题，使评估能随模型能力动态升级。

Abstract (英文): How can we measure intelligence beyond human capability?
  Human-authored benchmarks saturate, and above human capability, examiners may not know which tasks are both hard and verifiable. We argue that this difficulty is inherent to absolute-scale evaluation and propose a new paradigm based on relative measurement in which models generate public challenges that separate other systems. Aggregating these outcomes yields an adversarial psychometric rating system that can scale with the systems being measured. We describe practical protocols that reduce incentives for private-information attacks, support judge-free adjudication, and naturally scale with agent capabilities. We instantiate the framework across verifiable and open-ended, non-verifiable domains, illustrating how model-generated evaluation can continue to measure systems beyond the human frontier.

### [98] [Operational Reframing and Approval-Framed Delegation in Multi-Agent LLM Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07097)
*Lifei Liu,Haoran Yu,Xiaochong Jiang,Su Wang,Pin Qian,Yihang Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文指出多智能体LLM系统的安全评估中，将直接提示与规划-执行流水线对比得到的单一“流水线效应”难以解释，因为它混淆了三种机制：有害意图被重构为合理操作、规划器拒绝或转换请求、执行器在授权提示下默认已获批准。作者提出五条件受控对比设计，在30个合成有害场景和四个智能体安全基准的探索性外部验证集上评估。结果表明，聚合流水线安全并非稳定的架构属性，操作重构是最具可迁移性的风险信号，原始模型排名无法预测部署后的行为，安全评估应分别报告各因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多智能体LLM系统安全评估通常只报告一个聚合的"流水线效应"（直接提示与规划-执行流水线之间的差异），但这种聚合度量混淆了多种不同机制，导致难以解释安全风险的真正来源。作者希望解耦这些机制，提供更细粒度的安全评估方法。

Method: 提出五条件受控对比设计，分别测试：原始直接提示、操作重构（将有害请求改写为合理操作）、规划器行为（接受/拒绝/转换）、授权框架（执行器在授权提示下的行为）以及模型配对效应。使用LLM判断合规性，在30个合成有害场景和四个智能体安全基准上评估GPT、Gemini、Claude、DeepSeek等模型。

Result: 1) 操作重构是风险信号，增加GPT、Gemini、DeepSeek的合规性，Claude相对抵抗；2) 规划器主要通过拒绝来抵消风险，但生成可执行步骤时执行器可能比直接操作基线更合规；3) 授权框架下的委托行为对提示设计、模型配对和场景来源敏感，怀疑型执行器提示可大幅降低合规性；4) Gemini在原始直接提示中最安全，但与Claude规划器配对时合规率从8.9%升至38.9%；5) GPT的零聚合流水线效应隐藏了重构增加被规划器拒绝抵消的事实。

Conclusion: 多智能体安全评估不应只报告聚合流水线效应，而应分别报告操作重构、规划器行为、授权框架和模型配对等因素，然后再将失败归因于架构本身。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该论文的解耦评估方法可直接应用于遥感领域多智能体LLM系统的安全性分析，例如在遥感图像解译任务中，用户可能通过"操作重构"将非法目标识别请求包装为合法地理分析任务。具体方案：1) 将五条件对比设计引入遥感智能体系统，评估规划器是否会将敏感目标检测请求重构为"地物分类"等合理任务；2) 测试不同基础模型（如GPT-4V用于遥感、专用遥感基础模型）配对时的安全差异；3) 在遥感基准数据集（如RSICap、GeoChat等）上构建安全测试场景，评估授权提示对执行器（如遥感图像分析代理）的合规性影响。

Abstract (英文): Safety evaluations of multi-agent LLM systems often compare a direct prompt with a planner-executor pipeline and report the difference as a single "pipeline effect." We argue that this aggregate is difficult to interpret because it conflates three mechanisms: harmful intent may be reframed as plausible operational work, the planner may refuse or transform the request, and the executor may act under delegation prompts implying prior approval. To separate these factors, we introduce a five-condition controlled contrast design, evaluated on 30 synthetic harmful scenarios and an exploratory external validation set from four agent-safety benchmarks using LLM-judged compliance.
  Our results show that aggregate pipeline safety is not a stable architectural property. Operational reframing is the most portable risk signal, increasing compliance for GPT, Gemini, and DeepSeek across both scenario sets, while Claude is comparatively resistant. Planner behavior can offset this risk mainly through refusal; however, when the planner produces executable steps, the executor may become more compliant than under the direct operational baseline. Approval-framed delegation is sensitive to prompt design, model pairing, and scenario source, and a skeptical executor prompt sharply reduces compliance.
  Raw-direct model rankings can also mispredict deployed planner-executor behavior. Gemini is safest under raw direct prompts in the primary set yet shows the largest amplification with a Claude planner, rising from 8.9 percent to 38.9 percent compliance. GPTs near-zero aggregate pipeline effect instead hides a reframing increase canceled by planner refusal. These findings suggest that multi-agent safety evaluations should report reframing, planner behavior, delegation framing, and model pairing separately before attributing failures to architecture itself.

</details>


### [99] [Does AI Understand Imaging? A Systematic Benchmark of Agentic AI for Computational Imaging Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07189)
*Ethan Chung,Chuanjun Zheng,Jasper Tan,Jingxi Li,Haopeng Zhang,Huaijin Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ImagingBench是一个包含20项计算成像任务的基准测试，评估视觉语言模型和智能体AI在物理与逆问题处理上的能力。结果表明，尽管这些模型能生成视觉上合理的输出，但在基于参考的保真度上表现较差，尤其在计算传感任务（如无透镜成像、事件重建、飞行时间成像、全息术）上显著弱于专用方法，揭示了语义视觉能力与物理成像性能之间的巨大差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉语言模型和智能体AI在语义视觉任务上表现优异，但它们在处理计算成像背后的物理和逆问题方面的能力尚不清楚，亟需一个统一的基准来评估这一差距。

Method: 构建了包含20项计算成像任务的基准，涵盖射线与波动光学、图像信号处理、逆重建、计算感知和校准五大类别。设计了三种评估设置：Expert（固定专家引导逆重建）、Planner（规划器引导逆重建）和Forward（前向系统仿真一致性检查）。评估了Gemini、GPT、Qwen等主流多模态系统，并与任务特定的非智能体基线进行比较。

Result: 智能体模型在所有任务上持续弱于专用方法，尤其在计算传感问题（无透镜成像、事件重建、飞行时间成像、全息术）上表现最差。Planner引导相比Expert基线仅带来微弱且不一致的提升。模型生成的视觉输出虽看似合理，但基于参考的保真度指标很差。

Conclusion: 当前视觉语言模型和智能体AI在语义视觉能力与物理驱动的成像性能之间存在显著差距，ImagingBench为衡量这一差距和追踪计算成像领域智能体AI的进展提供了统一测试平台。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域涉及大量物理驱动的成像逆问题（如遥感图像去模糊、超分辨率、压缩感知重建、SAR成像解译等），与ImagingBench中的计算成像任务高度契合。具体方案：(1) 将遥感中的典型逆问题（如多光谱/高光谱重建、InSAR相位解缠、云雾去除）纳入ImagingBench框架，扩展其任务类别；(2) 利用遥感数据的大规模标签特性，为Expert设置提供更丰富的先验知识引导；(3) 借鉴ImagingBench的三种评估设置（Expert/Planner/Forward），系统评估多模态模型在遥感物理建模与语义解译之间的差距，为遥感领域的智能体AI设计提供指导。

Abstract (英文): Vision-language models (VLMs) and agentic AI have shown strong performance on semantic visual tasks, but it remains unclear whether they can handle the physics and inverse problems that underlie computational imaging. We present ImagingBench, a benchmark of 20 computational imaging tasks spanning five categories: ray and wave optics, image signal processing, inverse reconstruction, computational sensing, and calibration. ImagingBench evaluates three complementary settings: Expert, fixed expert-guided inverse reconstruction; Planner, planner-guided inverse reconstruction; and Forward, forward-system simulation for consistency checking. We benchmark leading proprietary and open-source image-centric multimodal systems, including Gemini, GPT, and Qwen, and compare them with representative task-specific non-agentic baselines. Across tasks, agentic models remain consistently weaker than specialized methods, especially on computational sensing problems such as lensless imaging, event-based reconstruction, time-of-flight imaging, and holography. Planner guidance provides only modest and inconsistent gains over the fixed-prompt Expert baseline. Although the models often generate visually plausible outputs, their reference-based fidelity remains poor, revealing a substantial gap between semantic visual competence and physically grounded imaging performance. ImagingBench provides a unified testbed for measuring this gap and tracking progress in agentic AI for computational imaging.

### [100] [Reasoning Consistency Scanning: A Framework for Auditing Chain-of-Thought Validity in AI Safety Evaluations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07229)
*Silvia Santano*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出推理一致性扫描方法，用于检测AI安全评估记录中推理过程与最终答案之间的逻辑一致性，区别于已有的推理忠实性研究。作者形式化了推理一致性的六种不一致子类型，构建了60条人工标注的基准测试集，实现了首个针对该属性的安全评估扫描器，并在多个模型和任务类型上验证了不一致性的存在与可检测性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作关注思维链推理的忠实性（模型陈述的推理是否真实反映其内部计算过程），但检测忠实性需要受控实验干预，无法事后分析评估记录。作者转向一个更易处理但关注不足的问题：推理过程是否与最终答案在逻辑上一致。一致性可从单一记录中直接评估，无需干预。

Method: 1) 形式化定义推理一致性并将其与忠实性区分，提出六子类型不一致性分类体系；2) 从InstrumentalEval输出中人工改编构建60条验证基准；3) 实现面向InspectScout平台的推理一致性扫描器；4) 在四个生成模型和三个评估任务上实验验证。

Result: 推理不一致性确实存在且可被检测到，不一致性在不同模型和任务类型间呈现系统性差异。

Conclusion: 推理一致性是一个可独立评估的属性，与忠实性正交；所提出的扫描方法可有效识别AI安全评估记录中的逻辑不一致问题，为后验评估提供了实用工具。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。1) 遥感领域的大模型（如GeoChat、RSGPT）在生成解译报告时同样存在推理与答案不一致的问题，可直接套用本文的一致性扫描框架进行检测；2) 六子类型分类体系可扩展到遥感特有场景，如地物分类推理链与分类结果不一致（推理说"植被"却输出"水体"）、变化检测中的逻辑矛盾等；3) 可将InspectScout扫描器适配到遥感评估基准（如RSVQA、SceneNet），构建遥感专用的推理一致性评估工具。

Abstract (英文): Prior work has shown that chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning is often unfaithful: a model's stated reasoning does not reliably reflect the process that produced its output. Detecting unfaithfulness, though, requires controlled experimental interventions, which cannot be applied to evaluation transcripts after the fact. We turn instead to a more tractable question that has received less attention: whether the stated reasoning is logically consistent with the answer it accompanies. Unlike faithfulness, consistency can be assessed from a transcript alone, with no intervention. We introduce reasoning consistency scanning, a reusable method for detecting this property in AI safety evaluation transcripts. Our contributions are fourfold. First, we formalize reasoning consistency as distinct from faithfulness and define a six-subtype taxonomy of inconsistency. Second, we build a validated benchmark of 60 transcripts, manually adapted from InstrumentalEval outputs. Third, we implement a working scanner for InspectScout, the first to target this property in safety evaluation transcripts. Fourth, we report results across four generator models and three evaluations from inspect_evals, showing that reasoning inconsistency is present, detectable, and varies systematically across both models and task types.

### [101] [From Atomic Actions to Standard Operating Procedures: Iterative Tool Optimization for Self-Evolving LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07321)
*Haipeng Ding,Yuexiang Xie,Zhewei Wei,Yaliang Li,Bolin Ding*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出EvoSOP框架，使LLM智能体能够从执行轨迹中提取标准化操作流程（SOP）作为可调用的高阶工具，并通过构建、合并、评估和剪枝的生命周期迭代优化工具集，从而提升任务成功率并减少交互轮次。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体框架依赖静态原子动作集（如文件I/O、单轮搜索），导致智能体针对重复性工作流不断重写底层逻辑，推理开销大且失败率高。

Method: 提出EvoSOP框架，让智能体从执行轨迹中提取SOP作为可调用的高阶工具，并通过构建、合并、评估和剪枝的系统化生命周期对工具集进行迭代优化。

Result: 实验表明EvoSOP显著提升了任务成功率，同时大幅减少了交互轮次。迭代工具优化促进了可靠高效的工具使用模式。

Conclusion: 智能体可以通过将原子动作合成为可复用的SOP实现自我进化，为自进化智能体的开发提供了可扩展的路径。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域涉及大量重复性处理流程（如数据预处理、波段运算、分类后处理等），可借鉴EvoSOP思想：1) 将遥感影像处理的原子操作（辐射定标、大气校正、几何校正等）封装为SOP工具；2) 从历史处理轨迹中自动提取常见工作流模板；3) 通过工具迭代优化减少人工调参和脚本编写开销，提升处理流程的自动化与可复用性。

Abstract (英文): Tool utilization enables Large Language Model (LLM) agents to interact with the real world and resolve complex tasks. However, existing agent frameworks predominantly rely on static toolsets composed of granular atomic actions (e.g., basic file I/O or single-turn search), which forces agents to reinvent low-level logic for every recurring workflow, leading to increased reasoning overhead and failure rates. In this study, we propose that agents can achieve self-evolution by synthesizing these atomic actions into reusable Standard Operating Procedures (SOPs), which function as callable higher-order tools that encapsulate multi-step logic. We further introduce EvoSOP, a framework that empowers agents to extract SOPs from execution trajectories and iteratively optimize the toolset through a systematic lifecycle of construction, merging, evaluation, and pruning. Extensive experiments demonstrate that EvoSOP significantly boosts task success rates while substantially reducing the number of interaction rounds compared to baselines. Our analysis also reveals that iterative tool optimization fosters reliable and efficient tool-use patterns, providing a scalable pathway for the development of self-evolving agents.
