### [164] [A Deep Learning-Based Method for Enhancing the Signal-to-Noise Ratio of Star Sensor Images](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132178)
*Jian Guan,Hanye Yu,Yanpeng Wu,X Li,Rongzheng Cao*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 针对星敏感器窗口跟踪模式下恒星信号被杂散光和读出噪声淹没的问题，本文以自监督时空去噪模型ASTERIS为基础，引入逐帧空间可变形卷积和复值频域损失（含高频加权掩膜）两项改进，在极低信噪比星图上将PSNR提升约17.8 dB，质心定位误差降至约0.1像素，显著优于原始ASTERIS和多帧叠加方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 星敏感器在窗口跟踪模式下，杂散光和探测器读出噪声会淹没星点信号，导致质心提取精度下降甚至失败，进而影响姿态确定精度。现有自监督时空去噪模型ASTERIS虽优于多帧叠加等传统方法，但缺乏对在轨星图亚像素抖动的自适应补偿，且难以保持星点高频形态，限制了去噪性能和质心定位精度。

Method: 1) 在解码器上采样阶段引入逐帧空间可变形卷积，自适应补偿亚像素偏移并主动抑制背景噪声，同时降低参数量；2) 设计复值频域损失函数并加入高频加权掩膜，联合约束幅度谱和相位谱，以保留星点高频细节。以ASTERIS为基线模型。

Result: 在极低信噪比星图上，本文方法PSNR提升约17.8 dB，质心定位误差约0.1像素；原始ASTERIS为PSNR提升约9.5 dB、误差约0.4像素；多帧叠加为PSNR提升约6.0 dB、误差约0.5像素。在模拟强噪声条件下实现了有效的质心提取。

Conclusion: 本文方法在极低信噪比星图上显著优于ASTERIS和多帧叠加方法，展现了在轨星敏感器数据处理的潜力。未来工作将进一步解决工程部署问题。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感领域（星敏感器）的论文。改进方向：1) 可变形卷积可进一步推广到遥感图像配准中的亚像素偏移补偿；2) 复值频域损失可应用于遥感图像融合（如全色与多光谱融合）中的高频细节保持；3) 该自监督框架可拓展至其他遥感传感器（如热红外、高光谱）的噪声抑制任务，但需针对不同传感器的噪声特性重新设计掩膜权重。

Abstract (英文): In window tracking mode, stray light and detector readout noise can submerge star spot signals in star sensor images. The resulting degradation reduces centroid extraction accuracy and may even cause extraction failure, thereby preventing precise attitude determination. This study uses the self-supervised spatiotemporal denoising model ASTERIS as the baseline. ASTERIS integrates 3D spatiotemporal inputs with a global attention mechanism for joint noise modeling, thereby providing stronger denoising and restoration capability than conventional methods such as multi-frame stacking. However, ASTERIS lacks adaptive compensation for subpixel jitter in on-orbit star images and has difficulty preserving the high-frequency morphology of star spots, affecting denoising performance and centroiding accuracy. To address these limitations, this study introduces two improvements: First, frame-by-frame spatial deformable convolution is incorporated into the decoder upsampling stage to adaptively compensate for subpixel offsets, actively suppress background noise, and lower the parameter count. Second, a complex-valued frequency domain loss with a high-frequency weighted mask is designed to jointly constrain the amplitude and phase spectra, thereby preserving high-frequency star spot details. Experimental results show that, for star images with extremely low signal-to-noise ratios, the proposed method improves the peak signal-to-noise ratio by approximately 17.8 dB and reduces the centroid localization error to approximately 0.1 pixels. This performance is substantially better than that of the original ASTERIS model, which improves the peak signal-to-noise ratio by approximately 9.5 dB and yields an error of approximately 0.4 pixels, and the multi-frame stacking method, which improves the peak signal-to-noise ratio by approximately 6.0 dB and yields an error of approximately 0.5 pixels. Under the simulated strong noise conditions considered in this study, the proposed method achieves effective centroid extraction, demonstrating its potential for on-orbit star sensor data processing. Future work will further address its engineering deployment.

### [165] [Prior-Informed Local Landslide Susceptibility Modelling Using National-Scale Landslide Information: A Case Study of the Parlung Tsangpo Alpine Gorge Basin](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132167)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 以青藏高原东南部帕隆藏布流域为研究区，对比了四种引入国家尺度信息的策略：局部基线建模、国家模型直接迁移、加权源-目标联合训练、以及先验信息引导的局部建模。先验策略将国家模型生成的易发性概率视为可解释的地学外部先验，再通过局部样本进行重新学习与校准。所有策略使用相同的条件因子、数据处理流程、空间独立测试集和评价指标。

Conclusion: 国家尺度的滑坡信息转化为局部重新校准的概率先验比直接迁移更有效，为数据稀缺的山地盆地易发性评估提供了一条实用路径。

Abstract (英文): Landslides pose widespread threats to mountainous communities and infrastructure worldwide, yet susceptibility mapping in alpine gorge basins is often constrained by sparse and incomplete local inventories. Whether national-scale landslide information can be transformed into reliable local knowledge remains unclear, particularly where strong topographic and environmental heterogeneity limits the direct transfer of broad-scale models. Here, we use the Parlung Tsangpo Basin on the southeastern Tibetan Plateau as a test case and compare four strategies for introducing national-scale information: local baseline modelling, direct national-model transfer, weighted source–target joint training, and prior-informed local modelling. The experiments use the same conditioning factors, data-processing workflow, spatially independent test set, and evaluation metrics, allowing the transfer strategies to be assessed under controlled conditions. The prior-informed strategy treats the susceptibility probability produced by the national model as a geoscientifically interpretable external prior, which is then relearned and recalibrated by local samples, and achieves the best overall performance. On the independent test set, it reaches an area under the receiver operating characteristic curve (AUC) of 0.901 and reduces the expected calibration error (ECE) to 0.055, outperforming the local baseline, direct transfer, and joint training strategies. Its susceptibility map shows an extensive low-susceptibility background with spatially concentrated high-susceptibility patches, thereby reducing broad-scale overprediction while preserving local landslide-prone zones. These results indicate that national-scale landslide information is more effective when converted into a locally recalibrated probability prior than when transferred directly, providing a practical pathway for susceptibility assessment in data-scarce mountainous basins.

### [166] [A Vertically Structured Machine Learning Approach for Cloud Liquid and Ice Water Content Profiling](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132177)
*Zhengyu Pan,Yansong Bao,Wei Hong,Haoran Li,Fang Pang,Wei Tao*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种垂直结构化的机器学习框架，通过构造垂直增强特征、异构树模型集成和廓线级精炼步骤，联合地基云雷达反射率与微波辐射计热力学廓线，显著提升了云液态水含量（LWC）和冰水含量（IWC）垂直廓线的反演精度。在Lindenberg站点的Cloudnet观测数据上，IWC的RMSE从0.0152降至0.0092 g m⁻³，R²从0.412提升至0.784；LWC的RMSE从0.0786降至0.0591 g m⁻³，R²从0.303提升至0.606，尤其在云边界区域改善显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有云水含量垂直廓线反演受限于强垂直变异性和观测变量间的非线性依赖关系；虽然云雷达和微波辐射计可提供互补约束，但联合使用时存在时空匹配不一致和预测因子偏差控制问题，且逐点建模无法有效捕捉廓线的垂直结构信息。

Method: 1) 构建垂直结构增强特征，编码局部梯度和上下文信息以显式表示廓线级依赖关系；2) 采用廓线感知的堆叠策略，集成多个异构树基学习器；3) 引入廓线级精炼步骤，抑制层间不一致性。

Result: 在Lindenberg站全年Cloudnet观测数据上：IWC反演RMSE从0.0152降至0.0092 g m⁻³，R²从0.412提升至0.784；LWC反演RMSE从0.0786降至0.0591 g m⁻³，R²从0.303提升至0.606；边界区域改善尤为显著。

Conclusion: 将云反演视为垂直结构化学习问题能够减少逐点模型固有的不一致性，为将垂直约束融入大气廓线反演建立了数据驱动基线。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该框架可直接迁移至遥感领域的气溶胶廓线反演、大气温湿廓线融合、降水廓线估计等问题。具体方案：1) 将垂直结构增强特征引入星载雷达/辐射计联合反演中，替代传统逐像素反演；2) 将廓线感知堆叠策略用于多源遥感数据（如主动+被动传感器）的协同；3) 廓线级精炼步骤可推广到其他垂直结构显著变化的遥感产品后处理中。

Abstract (英文): Accurate retrieval of cloud liquid water content (LWC) and ice water content (IWC) vertical profiles remains limited by strong vertical variability and nonlinear dependencies among observed variables. Ground-based cloud radar reflectivity and microwave radiometer-derived thermodynamic profiles provide complementary constraints, but their joint use requires consistent time–height matching and bias-controlled predictors. This study develops a vertically structured machine-learning framework that explicitly represents profile-level dependencies by constructing vertical-structure-enhanced features to encode local gradients and contextual information, integrating multiple tree-based learners with heterogeneous configurations through a profile-aware stacking strategy, and introducing a profile-level refinement step to suppress layer-to-layer inconsistencies. The framework is evaluated using year-round Cloudnet observations from the Lindenberg site, where IWC RMSE decreases from 0.0152 g m−3 to 0.0092 g m−3 with R2 increasing from 0.412 to 0.784, and LWC RMSE decreases from 0.0786 g m−3 to 0.0591 g m−3 with R2 increasing from 0.303 to 0.606. Additional boundary-region evaluation shows that the improvement is particularly evident near radar-derived cloud boundaries, where cloud structure and hydrometeor content may vary rapidly with height. These results indicate that treating cloud retrieval as a vertically structured learning problem reduces inconsistencies inherent in pointwise models and establishes a data-driven baseline for incorporating vertical constraints into atmospheric profile retrieval.

</details>


### [167] [MIGA-Net: A Graph Interaction and Gated Context Network for High-Resolution Remote Sensing Change Detection](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132155)
*Jingtong Yang,Xiaorong Xue,Yishuo Tian,Wen Zhang,Bingyan Lu,Xin Zhao,W X Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: MIGA-Net是一种端到端遥感变化检测框架，通过时空图交互（ST-GIM）、自适应门控上下文金字塔（AGCP）和层次边界精炼（HBAR）三个模块，分别解决跨时相外观不一致、目标尺度变化和边界模糊问题。在LEVIR-CD、WHU-CD和SYSU-CD数据集上取得了领先的F1和IoU分数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高分辨率遥感变化检测中，跨时相外观不一致（如光照、季节变化导致的伪变化）、目标尺度变化大以及多级解码过程中的边界模糊这三个挑战严重影响了检测性能，现有方法难以同时有效解决这些问题。

Method: 提出MIGA-Net框架，包含三个核心模块：(1) 时空图交互模块（ST-GIM），结合交互注意力与图推理抑制伪变化；(2) 自适应门控上下文金字塔模块（AGCP），通过内容驱动的尺度选择与门控残差机制减少噪声放大；(3) 层次边界感知精炼模块（HBAR），融合语义通道滤波与显式边界注意力进行渐进式轮廓恢复。

Result: 在LEVIR-CD上F1 91.84%、IoU 84.91%；WHU-CD上F1 92.52%、IoU 86.08%；SYSU-CD上F1 82.92%、IoU 70.83%。在定量指标和结构边界质量上均有一致提升。

Conclusion: MIGA-Net在伪变化抑制和结构保真预测方面表现优异，验证了联合建模时空交互、多尺度上下文聚合和层次边界精炼的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。作为遥感变化检测论文，MIGA-Net的改进方向包括：(1) ST-GIM可引入时序注意力或跨模态图推理（如结合SAR与光学影像），进一步提升跨模态变化检测能力；(2) AGCP可扩展为可变形卷积或动态稀疏卷积，更好地处理不规则地物尺度变化；(3) HBAR可结合主动轮廓模型或水平集方法，实现亚像素级边界精炼；(4) 可引入扩散概率模型或掩码自编码器进行特征增强，提升对小目标变化和弱变化区域的敏感性。

Abstract (英文): Remote sensing change detection (CD) aims to localize land-surface changes from bi-temporal imagery and plays an important role in applications such as urban monitoring, disaster assessment, and environmental analysis. In high-resolution scenarios, CD performance is often degraded by cross-temporal appearance inconsistency, large variations in target scale, and boundary ambiguity introduced during multi-level decoding. To address these challenges, we propose MIGA-Net, an end-to-end framework that jointly models spatio-temporal interaction, adaptive multi-scale context aggregation, and hierarchical boundary refinement. Specifically, the Spatio-Temporal Graph Interaction Module (ST-GIM) combines interactive attention and graph reasoning to suppress pseudo-changes caused by illumination or seasonal shifts; the Adaptive Gated Context Pyramid Module (AGCP) performs content-driven scale selection and regulates context injection through a gated residual mechanism to reduce noise amplification; and the Hierarchical Boundary-Aware Refinement Module (HBAR) integrates semantic channel filtering and explicit boundary attention for progressive contour recovery. Experiments on LEVIR-CD, WHU-CD, and SYSU-CD demonstrate that MIGA-Net achieves F1 scores of 91.84%, 92.52%, and 82.92%, and IoU scores of 84.91%, 86.08%, and 70.83%, respectively. The proposed method yields consistent improvements in both quantitative metrics and structural boundary quality, indicating its effectiveness for robust pseudo-change suppression and structurally faithful prediction in high-resolution remote sensing CD.

### [168] [Assessing the Reliability of Sentinel-2 for Turbidity Estimation in a Shallow Coastal Lagoon](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132176)
*Adriana Castro,Humberto Pereira,João Miguel Días,Carina L. Lopes*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究针对葡萄牙Aveiro潟湖，开发了一种基于Sentinel-2卫星影像的局部浊度反演模型。通过2025年5月28日野外同步观测数据，比较了ACOLITE软件中多种现有算法，发现其在该区域高浊度值低估问题。最终基于665 nm与560 nm波段比值（RGratio）构建的新模型表现最优（R² = 0.822, RMSE = 1.77 NTU），强调了局部校准模型在浅水潟湖浊度反演中的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 沿海系统浊度理解对可持续管理至关重要，而现有卫星浊度算法在局部浅水潟湖（如Aveiro潟湖）中适用性不足，存在高浊度低估问题，亟需开发本地化校准模型。

Method: 2025年5月28日与Sentinel-2过境同步开展野外测量，获取近表层浊度和Secchi深度数据；利用ACOLITE软件（v20250114.0）提取遥感反射率（Rrs）并应用多种现有算法；基于Rrs数据构建新浊度模型并进行经验调整，以决定系数（R²）和均方根误差（RMSE）评估性能。

Result: 现有ACOLITE算法在Aveiro潟湖直接适用性差，严重低估最高浊度值；665 nm与560 nm波段比值（RGratio）是最佳光谱指数，浊度估计R²=0.822，RMSE=1.77 NTU。

Conclusion: 在浅水沿海潟湖中，局部校准模型优于标准ACOLITE算法；但所提模型仅针对当日潮汐、风和河流排放条件校准，尚未经独立验证，需进一步评估其泛化能力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本研究的Sentinel-2局部浊度建模方法可直接应用于中国沿海潟湖（如珠江口、杭州湾、渤海湾等），具体改进/交叉方案：（1）针对不同浑浊度梯度的中国潟湖/河口区域，开展多时相同步观测，构建区域化RGratio模型；（2）结合中国自主卫星（如高分系列、HY-1C/D）的多光谱数据，验证并适配RGratio指数；（3）引入潮汐、风场和径流等多源辅助数据，提高模型在不同水动力条件下的鲁棒性；（4）探索RGratio与悬浮泥沙浓度（SSC）的关系，扩展模型输出能力。

Abstract (英文): Understanding turbidity in coastal systems is essential to ensure the sustainable management of these ecosystems, which are increasingly under pressure from natural factors and human activities. Thus, this study aims to develop a local Sentinel-2-based turbidity model for the Aveiro lagoon (Portugal) by combining Sentinel-2 records with in situ measurements. A field campaign synchronized with a Sentinel-2 overpass was conducted across the lagoon channels on 28 May 2025, to capture spatial variability by measuring near-surface turbidity and Secchi depth, for correspondence with the spectral records of satellite. Remote Sensing Reflectance (Rrs) and turbidity were derived using various algorithms integrated within the ACOLITE software (v20250114.0). Additionally, new turbidity models were developed and empirically adjusted based on the Rrs data, with their performance quantified through the coefficient of determination (R2) and Root Mean Square Error (RMSE). The results showed that the existing algorithms are not directly suitable for the Aveiro lagoon, as they underestimate the highest turbidity values. The ratio between 665 and 560 nm bands (RGratio) proved to be the most suitable spectral index, performing best in estimating turbidity (R2 = 0.822 and RMSE = 1.77 NTU). This study highlights the importance of locally calibrated models over standard ACOLITE algorithms for turbidity retrieval in shallow coastal lagoons, while emphasizing that the proposed model was calibrated for the tidal, wind, and river discharge conditions sampled during the campaign and has not yet been independently validated.

### [169] [Local Calibration Enhances the Transferability of UAV-LiDAR Models for Tree-Level Carbon Estimation in Radiata Pine Plantations](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132161)
*Michael S. Watt,Sadeepa Jayathunga*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文利用新西兰20个辐射松人工林样地数据（35,201棵树），比较了线性混合效应模型（LMM）、广义加性模型（GAM）和随机森林（RF）三种建模策略（多站点、局部事后校准、全局部模型）在UAV-LiDAR估算单木碳储量中的表现。结果表明：多站点模型泛化能力差（相对RMSE 35.9%-56.9%），但使用50棵树进行事后校准可将误差降低30-60%（相对RMSE 22.8-25.0%），接近全局部模型效果（21.9-23.1%），且样本量超过50棵后精度提升有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 森林碳储量的准确且可迁移估算是森林经营管理和国家温室气体报告的关键需求，但现有UAV-LiDAR单木碳模型在不同样地间的迁移性较差，缺乏系统比较不同建模策略（多站点、事后校准、局部模型）在统一框架下表现的研究。

Method: 使用新西兰20个辐射松人工林样地（35,201棵树）的UAV-LiDAR数据，在留一样地外（LOSO）交叉验证框架下比较LMM、GAM和RF三种模型，分别评估多站点模型迁移性、基于50棵样本的事后校准策略和全局部模型拟合策略，并分析不同样本量和采样策略（随机选树 vs. 基于样地采样）对精度的影响。

Result: 多站点模型泛化能力差（相对RMSE 35.9%-56.9%且存在样地级偏差）；50棵树事后校准将误差降低30-60%（相对RMSE 22.8-25.0%）并大幅减少偏差；全局部模型仅略优于事后校准（21.9-23.1%）；事后校准超过50棵树、全局部模型超过175棵树后精度增益很小；不同采样策略差异不大。

Conclusion: 对多站点UAV-LiDAR模型进行少量本地样本（50棵树）的事后校准是一种实用高效的单木碳储量估算方法，平衡了精度与采样成本，适用于人工林经营。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。本文本身就是遥感（UAV-LiDAR）应用于森林碳估算的论文。改进方向：1）可引入深度学习（如PointNet++、DGCNN）直接从LiDAR点云提取特征替代手工特征工程，进一步提升模型表现；2）事后校准策略可扩展到时序监测场景，利用少量地面实测更新模型以适应森林动态变化；3）本文仅针对单一树种（辐射松），可推广到多树种混交林，并考虑树种分类作为协变量；4）结合高光谱或多光谱UAV数据，利用光谱-结构融合特征提升碳估算精度；5）采样策略方面可探索自适应采样（如主动学习）以进一步减少所需本地样本量。

Abstract (英文): Accurate and transferable estimation of forest carbon is essential for operational forest management and national greenhouse gas reporting, yet it remains challenging because of variation in stand structure and site conditions. Unmanned aerial vehicle-based light detection and ranging (UAV-LiDAR) provides detailed structural information for modelling tree-level carbon, but model transferability across sites is often limited. In this study, we compared three modelling approaches—a linear mixed-effects model (LMM), a generalised additive model (GAM), and Random Forest (RF)—within a unified framework of multi-site, locally post hoc calibrated, and fully local model-fitting strategies. Using data from 20 radiata pine (Pinus radiata D. Don) plantation stands across New Zealand (35,201 trees), a leave-one-site-out (LOSO) framework was used to assess multi-site model transferability and support post hoc calibration, while local models were evaluated using repeated within-site train/test splits. We also evaluated how prediction accuracy changed with increasing local sample size and compared random tree selection with plot-based sampling. Multi-site models showed poor generalisation, with mean relative RMSE ranging from 35.9% to 56.9% and substantial site-level bias. Applying post hoc calibration to the multi-site model using a 50-tree sample reduced prediction error by 30 to 60% (mean relative RMSE 22.8–25.0%) and substantially reduced bias across sites. The fitting of fully local models with the same sample size yielded only modest further improvements (mean relative RMSE 21.9–23.1%). Gains in accuracy were minimal with increasing sample sizes above 50 trees for post hoc calibration and 175 trees for the fully local models, and differences in accuracy between sampling strategies were small. These results show that post hoc calibration of multi-site UAV-LiDAR models with a small local sample provides a practical and efficient approach for tree-level carbon estimation in plantation forests.

</details>


### [170] [Cloud Microphysical Characteristics in the Northeast China Cold Vortex Derived from Satellite Measurements](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132165)
*Qin Zheng,Qi Liu,Yuan Li,Zhenci Lu,Jiahao Cheng*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文利用MODIS卫星云产品，分析了东北冷涡（NCCV）背景下云系统的云型频率及四种关键云微物理特性（液态有效半径、冰晶有效半径、液态水路径、冰水路径）。发现NCCV与非NCCV样本在云型组成上高度相似（以层积云为主，占比超40%），但微物理特性差异显著，其中液态水路径在NCCV中明显更大。空间结构上，液态水路径和冰水路径的空间异质性更强，液态水路径在北至西北区域显著增大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 东北冷涡是影响中国东北、华北及江淮地区的典型天气尺度系统，常引发雷暴、大风和强降水，但与之相关的云系统微物理特性长期缺乏观测表征，现有研究对此认知不足。

Method: 利用MODIS云产品数据，对比分析NCCV与非NCCV条件下的云型频率和四种云微物理参数（Re_liq、Re_ice、LWP、IWP），并从空间结构角度分析NCCV区域内云微物理的分布特征。

Result: NCCV与非NCCV样本云型组成高度相似，均以层积云（Sc）为主（占比>40%），但NCCV云系统的液态水路径（LWP）显著更大。空间上，层积云、高积云、层云和雨层云构成主要背景，LWP和IWP的空间异质性高于Re_liq和Re_ice，LWP在北至西北区域明显增大，IWP在径向和方位角维度上变化更大。

Conclusion: 研究从卫星观测角度揭示了NCCV相关云系统的统计微物理特征，为深入理解其独特的云和降水物理过程提供了参考依据。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该研究为纯遥感应用工作，可从以下方面改进：(1) 融合多源遥感数据（如CloudSat/CALIPSO的垂直廓线、GPM降水雷达）以获取三维微物理结构，弥补MODIS仅提供柱积分/单层信息的局限；(2) 引入机器学习（如随机森林或CNN）建立NCCV强度/位置与云微物理参数的非线性映射模型；(3) 结合再分析资料（ERA5）分析环境风切变和水汽输送对微物理空间异质性的影响机制；(4) 可拓展至其他冷涡系统（如蒙古冷涡）进行对比研究，增强结论普适性。

Abstract (英文): The Northeast China Cold Vortex (NCCV), a typical synoptic-scale system in Northeast China, North China, and the Jianghuai region, frequently triggers thunderstorms, strong winds, and heavy precipitation, making it significant for meteorological monitoring and operational forecasting. However, the cloud microphysical properties of NCCV-associated cloud systems remain poorly characterized, as long-term cloud microphysical observations are limited. This study utilizes cloud products from the Moderate Resolution Imaging Spectroradiometer (MODIS) to analyze cloud-type frequencies and four key cloud microphysical properties under NCCV conditions: liquid effective radius (Re_liq), ice effective radius (Re_ice), liquid water path (LWP), and ice water path (IWP). Nearly identical cloud-type compositions are found for the two groups, NCCV and non-NCCV samples with similar cloud fractions on the regional scale, which are dominated by stratocumulus (Sc), altostratus (As), cumulus (Cu), and stratus (St), with Sc accounting for above 40% of total cloud occurrence. Yet microphysical properties differ markedly between these two groups. LWP shows the most contrast and it is evidently larger in NCCV than in non-NCCV cloud systems. As for the spatial structure of cloud microphysics in the NCCV domain, it is found that Sc, As, St, and nimbostratus (Ns) constitute the primary background, and Sc remains the dominant cloud type in almost all spatial sectors. LWP and IWP tend to have stronger spatial heterogeneity than Re_liq and Re_ice. LWP gets notably larger in the northern to northwestern sectors, whereas IWP shows much higher variations in both radial and azimuthal dimensions. These results reveal the statistical microphysical characteristics of cloud systems associated with NCCV from the perspective of satellite observations, providing a reference for a deeper understanding of their unique cloud and precipitation physical processes.

</details>


### [171] [YOLO-Based Landslide Identification and Causal Inference Using Double Machine Learning in Longyan, Fujian](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132157)
*Jiaqi He,Lingsheng Luo,Weiwei Li,Yuedan Luo,Xinyi Huang,H Wang,CL Guo,Shengdong Chen,Chuanan Xia*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文基于YOLO深度学习模型和双重机器学习模型，利用2024年福建省龙岩市卫星影像识别了1185处滑坡（总面积31.02 km²），并通过因果推断分析了降雨、NDVI、距道路距离等因素对滑坡的影响，发现6-7月降雨对滑坡有显著正向因果效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 滑坡及其次生灾害对公共基础设施和居民安全构成重大威胁，快速准确地识别大规模滑坡事件是工程地质领域的重大挑战，现有方法在效率和精度上仍存在不足。

Method: 基于YOLO深度学习模型构建滑坡识别框架，利用2024年福建省龙岩市卫星影像构建训练数据集；采用双重机器学习模型进行因果推断分析，研究降雨、NDVI、距道路距离等致灾因子与滑坡之间的因果关系；结合SHAP值进行特征重要性排序。

Result: 共识别1185处滑坡，面积约31.02 km²，主要集中在上杭、武平、长汀和新罗南部；滑坡集中在海拔300-500 m、坡度10°-25°、年降雨量1600-1700 mm区域；SHAP值显示关键因子排序为NDVI > 降雨 > 距道路距离 > 距河流距离 > 坡向；因果推断表明6-7月降雨对滑坡有显著正向因果效应。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架和研究成果为闽西南地区的滑坡识别与风险评估提供了有价值的技术和理论支持，且因果推断结果与降雨诱发滑坡的物理机制及政府报告的滑坡数据一致。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。作为一篇遥感与深度学习结合的滑坡识别论文，可改进方向包括：（1）引入多时相遥感影像（如Sentinel-1 SAR数据）进行时序变化检测，提升对缓慢变形滑坡的识别能力；（2）融合多源遥感数据（光学+InSAR+LiDAR）构建多模态输入，提高复杂地形下的识别鲁棒性；（3）将YOLO模型与地理空间注意力机制结合，增强对空间上下文信息的建模；（4）引入迁移学习策略，解决不同区域遥感影像风格差异导致的泛化问题；（5）结合高分辨率遥感影像（如GF-2、WorldView）提升小规模滑坡的检测精度。

Abstract (英文): Landslides and their associated secondary hazards present substantial threats to both public infrastructure and resident safety. The rapid and accurate identification of large-scale landslide events remains a critical challenge in the field of engineering geology. In this study, a YOLO-based deep learning model is developed for landslide identification relying on a training dataset constructed using the satellite imagery of Longyan City, Fujian Province, in 2024. Adopting the double machine learning model, we examine the causal inference relationships between landslide and causative factors, including rainfall (R), mean Normalized Difference Vegetation Index (NDVI) and Distance to roads (DRoa). A total of 1185 landslides is identified in 2024, covering an area of approximately 31.02 km2. The landslides are predominantly concentrated in Shanghang, Wuping, Changting, and the southern part of Xinluo. The landslides mainly correspond to elevations around 300–500 m, slopes among the interval of [10°, 25°], and annual rainfall intensities ranging from 1600 m to 1700 mm. The top five key factors for landslide occurrence in descending order are NDVI, R, DRoa, Distance to Rivers (DRiv) and Aspect (A), in terms SHAP values. Causal inference analysis reveals that the rainfall in June and July shows significant positive causal effects to landslide, which is consistent with the physical mechanism of rainfall-induced landslide and the landslide data reported by the government. The framework proposed and the findings in this study offer valuable technical and theoretical support for landslide identification and risk assessment in southwestern Fujian.

### [172] [MS3CHFormer: A Multi-Scale Spatial–Spectral Convolutional Hybrid Transformer for Hyperspectral Image Classification](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132173)
*Jian Yu,Haixin Sun,Fanlei Meng,Jiaqi Liang,Xing Zhou*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出了一种多尺度空间-光谱卷积混合Transformer模型（MS3CHFormer），通过多分支多感受野的卷积模块、Token选择性稀疏Transformer编码器、局部-全局特征融合模块和细节保留增强模块，在高光谱图像分类任务中取得了优于现有方法的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有高光谱图像分类方法存在多尺度空间-光谱特征建模不充分、局部与全局特征缺乏高效交互机制、Transformer计算复杂度高且存在冗余信息等问题，限制模型性能。

Method: 1) MS3ConvM：多分支多感受野设计，联合建模不同尺度的空间和光谱特征；2) TSSTE：通过动态相关性感知注意力（DCAA）机制自适应选择token并进行稀疏建模，降低计算复杂度并抑制冗余；3) LGFFM：将CNN和Transformer特征映射到不同表示空间实现深度互补融合；4) DPEM：通过残差连接引入原始细节信息补偿高层语义表示的细节损失。

Result: 在四个公开高光谱数据集上的实验表明，MS3CHFormer优于现有最先进方法，在有限训练样本下表现出卓越的分类精度、鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: 所提出的MS3CHFormer通过多尺度卷积与稀疏Transformer的混合设计，有效解决了高光谱图像分类中的多尺度建模、局部-全局交互和计算效率问题，是一种高性能的分类框架。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感高光谱图像分类领域的论文。改进方向：1) MS3ConvM中的多分支卷积可进一步引入可变形卷积或动态卷积以适应地物形态多样性；2) TSSTE的稀疏注意力机制可结合频域分析（如FFT）进一步加速；3) LGFFM可引入自适应门控机制动态调整CNN与Transformer特征的融合权重；4) DPEM可结合超分辨率重建或边缘检测损失函数进一步强化细节保持能力；5) 模型可扩展至多模态遥感数据（如LiDAR+HSI）的分类任务。

Abstract (英文): Deep learning methods that integrate convolutional neural networks (CNNs) and Transformers have achieved remarkable progress in hyperspectral image (HSI) classification. However, existing methods still suffer from insufficient multi-scale spatial–spectral feature modeling, a lack of efficient interaction mechanisms between local and global features, and the inherent high computational complexity and redundant information of Transformers, which limit model performance. To address these issues, a Multi-Scale Spatial–Spectral Convolutional Hybrid Transformer model (MS3CHFormer) is proposed in this article. Specifically, a Multi-Scale Spatial–Spectral Convolution Module (MS3ConvM) is first constructed. Through a multi-branch and multi-receptive-field design, it jointly models spatial and spectral features at different scales, thereby enhancing the representation capability of complex ground objects. Then, a Token-Selective Sparse Transformer Encoder (TSSTE) is designed, which adaptively selects tokens and performs sparse modeling via a Dynamic Correlation-Aware Attention (DCAA) mechanism, effectively reducing computational complexity while suppressing redundant information and further reinforcing key feature representations. Furthermore, a Local–Global Feature Fusion Module (LGFFM) is designed to achieve deep complementary fusion of CNN and Transformer features by mapping them into different representation spaces. Finally, a Detail-Preserving Enhancement Module (DPEM) introduces original detail information through residual connections to compensate for detail loss in high-level semantic representations, thereby enhancing the representation capability of boundaries and fine-grained structures. Experiments and comparative analyses on four public HSI datasets demonstrate that the proposed MS3CHFormer outperforms state-of-the-art methods and achieves superior classification accuracy under limited training samples, exhibiting excellent robustness and generalization ability.

Furthermore, compared to approaches that rely solely on UAV images or on the fusion of UAV and all ground-based images for modeling, the method proposed in this paper restores building texture information in occluded areas and improves the accuracy of 3D real-scene modeling while simultaneously reducing data-processing and storage requirements and enhancing operational efficiency. ### [174] [A Scalable Clustering-Based Method for Vegetation Mapping in Large Areas Using Satellite Image Time Series](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132162)
*Baggio Luiz de Castro e Silva,Karine Reis Ferreira,Gilberto Ribeiro de Queiroz,Juliana Santos da Mota,Erison Carlos dos Santos Monteiro,Mayara Teodoro,Isabel Cristina de Oliveira Silva,Murilo Brasil da Silva,Rodrigo Delgado Inácio,Rafael Andrade Aluvei,Agata Fabielle Gomes,Cláudio Almeida,Marcos Adami*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出一种基于GPU加速自组织映射与动态时间规整层次聚类的半自动化方法，通过时间序列聚类减少训练样本需求，将巴西塞拉多地区次生植被制图周期从两年缩短至六个月，总体精度96.45%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 巴西塞拉多生物多样性热区面临农业扩张和原生植被转化的巨大压力，需要高效监测支持保护与环境政策。然而在异质景观中，监督分类方法面临大规模高质量训练数据集获取的瓶颈，亟需减少训练样本依赖的可扩展制图方法。

Method: 两阶段方法：第一阶段，无监督过程集成GPU加速自组织映射与基于动态时间规整的层次聚类，生成光谱时间聚类；第二阶段，专家通过目视解译对聚类进行标注和细化，将专家知识从像素级迁移到聚类的光谱时间模式级。

Conclusion: 所提半自动化聚类方法能在保持大尺度监测所需精度前提下，显著降低训练样本需求和人工标注成本，大幅提升制图效率，适用于大规模业务化遥感监测。

Abstract (英文): The Brazilian Cerrado, a global biodiversity hotspot, is under increasing pressure from agricultural expansion and native vegetation conversion, underscoring the need for efficient monitoring to support conservation and environmental policies. In heterogeneous landscapes, land use and land cover (LULC) mapping using supervised classification methods faces a major bottleneck: the need for extensive and high-quality training datasets. To address this challenge, we propose a semi-automated, clustering-based methodology for mapping secondary vegetation within previously deforested areas, reducing training-sample requirements and enabling scalable mapping through the clustering of satellite image time series. In the first stage, an unsupervised process integrates graphics processing unit (GPU)-accelerated Self-Organizing Maps and hierarchical clustering with Dynamic Time Warping to produce spectro-temporal clusters. In the second stage, specialists label and refine these clusters by visual interpretation, transferring expert knowledge from individual pixels to grouped spectro-temporal patterns. Applied to 692,000 km2 of previously deforested land in the Cerrado biome, the methodology produced a mapped secondary vegetation area of 81,209 km2 (11.74%). The design-based estimated area was 98,683 ± 10,071 km2, with an overall accuracy of 96.45 ± 1.52%, a user’s accuracy of 96.27 ± 2.40%, a producer’s accuracy of 79.22 ± 7.94%, and an F1-score of 86.90%. The initial cluster labeling accounted for 86.3% of the final secondary vegetation area and limited the interpretation task to approximately 3000 cluster-level decisions. Implemented in the TerraClass Cerrado 2024 cycle, the workflow reduced the secondary vegetation mapping phase from approximately two years to six months while maintaining the thematic accuracy required for large-scale operational monitoring.

### [175] [Integrating Gross Error Identification with Deep Learning for InSAR Topography-Dependent Delay Correction: A Case Study of the Baihetan Hydropower Station Area](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132168)
*Yuanyuan Liu,H T Chen,Dan Liu,Bo Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出一种结合粗差识别与多层感知机（MLP）的EiMLP模型，用于地形相关对流层延迟校正，在白鹤滩水电站区域验证，SSIM达0.970，RMSE为0.673 rad，校正后干涉图相位标准差平均降低83%，有效抑制地形相关相位并揭示被大气误差掩盖的形变信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出EiMLP模型，包含粗差识别模块（基于相位梯度检测解缠相位跳变）和MLP模型（利用单幅干涉图的解缠相位和DEM高程信息重建大气相位），实现对地形相关对流层延迟的校正。

Abstract (英文): Tropospheric delay poses a major limitation to high-precision InSAR observations, particularly in high mountain and canyon regions. To address this issue, this study proposes a combined model (EiMLP) that integrates gross error identification with a multilayer perceptron (MLP) for topography-dependent tropospheric delay correction. The gross error identification module detects unwrapped phase jumps based on phase gradients, followed by an MLP model that reconstructs the atmospheric phase using unwrapped phase and elevation information from a single interferogram. The proposed method is validated in the Baihetan Hydropower Station area and compared with traditional correction methods. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method achieves a Structural Similarity Index Measure (SSIM) of 0.970 and a Root Mean Square Error (RMSE) of 0.673 rad for the simulated atmospheric phase. After atmospheric correction, the average phase standard deviation of the interferograms is reduced by 83%, and the topography-related correlation is significantly suppressed. Furthermore, after correction by the proposed method, the signals that are masked by atmospheric errors in the original interferograms can be clearly revealed, indicating the potential for slope instability. These findings indicate that the EiMLP model, operating on a single interferogram, exhibits robust applicability and provides a reliable reference for future InSAR tropospheric delay correction.

### [176] [Trait-Dependent Effects of Band Selection on Predicting Soybean Biomass, Leaf Area Index, and Canopy Cover from Hyperspectral Reflectance](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132179)
*Etsushi Kumagai,Takayuki Yabiku,Yusuke Masuya,Kensuke Kimura,Erina Fushimi,Ryosuke Nomiyama*

TL;DR: 本研究评估了不同波段选择算法（全波段PLS、PLS-VIP、BoLASSO和集成方法）对大豆冠层高光谱反射率（501-801 nm）预测地上生物量（AGB）、叶面积指数（LAI）和冠层覆盖度（CC）的影响。结果表明，波段选择效果依赖于目标性状；BoLASSO在减少波段数量的情况下对LAI和CC取得了与全波段PLS相当的精度；年际可迁移性对AGB较LAI和CC更困难；所选波长主要集中在可见光、红边和近红外区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高光谱反射可提供详细光谱信息，但波段选择在基于回归的冠层性状预测中的作用尚不清楚。本研究旨在系统评估不同波段选择算法对大豆关键冠层性状预测精度的影响，并探索简化传感的候选光谱区域。

Method: 使用大豆冠层VNIR（501-801 nm）高光谱反射率数据，涵盖多个地点、年份、品种和灌溉处理。比较全波段PLS回归与三种波段选择方法（PLS-VIP、BoLASSO、集成方法），采用Kennard-Stone验证和留一年交叉验证评估模型性能。

Conclusion: 波段选择策略应根据目标性状定制，选定的VNIR波段可为大豆冠层性状的简化传感提供候选光谱区域。

Abstract (英文): Predicting canopy traits non-destructively is important for understanding crop growth and improving phenotyping efficiency. Hyperspectral reflectance provides detailed spectral information, but the role of band selection in regression-based trait prediction at the canopy scale remains unclear. In this study, we evaluated the effects of different band-selection algorithms on the prediction accuracy of aboveground biomass (AGB), leaf area index (LAI), and canopy cover (CC) in soybeans using canopy hyperspectral reflectance in the visible to near-infrared (VNIR) range from 501 to 801 nm. The dataset included multiple sites, years, cultivars, and irrigation treatments. We compared a full-band partial least squares regression (PLS) model with three band-selection methods (PLS-Variable Importance in Projection (VIP), Bootstrapped least absolute shrinkage and selection operator (LASSO) (BoLASSO), and an ensemble approach). Model performance was assessed using Kennard–Stone validation and leave-one-year-out cross-validation. The results showed that the effectiveness of band selection depended on the target trait. Full-band PLS performed well for AGB under Kennard–Stone validation, whereas BoLASSO achieved comparable accuracy to PLS for LAI and CC using a reduced number of selected bands. Leave-one-year-out cross-validation showed that year-to-year transferability was more difficult for AGB than for LAI and CC. The selected wavelengths were located mainly in the visible, red-edge, and near-infrared regions. These results indicate that band-selection strategies should be tailored to the target trait and that selected VNIR bands can provide candidate spectral regions for simplified sensing of soybean canopy traits.

### [177] [Spatial and Temporal Variability of Terrestrial Water Storage and Their Relationship with Groundwater Level with GRACE, GLDAS and Observations: A Case Study of Murray–Darling Basin](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132206)
*Chongya Ma,Jiping Liu,Guobin Fu*

TL;DR: 利用GRACE卫星数据、GLDAS陆面模型和气候观测数据，研究了Murray-Darling流域陆地水储量的时空变化规律及其与地下水位的关系。结果显示：2002-2009年TWS负异常呈下降趋势，2010-2017年正异常呈下降趋势，2018-2025年混合异常呈上升趋势；识别出5个主导聚类模式；TWS与降雨强相关但与蒸发和径流也有关联；TWS衍生的地下水储量变化与实测地下水位变化既有相似性也有差异，反映复杂的水文地质过程和人类活动影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Murray-Darling流域陆地水储量的时空变化规律，明确TWS与地下水位的关联性，为利用GRACE卫星信息和陆面模型支持地下水资源管理提供科学依据。

Method: 采用GRACE卫星反演TWS数据、GLDAS陆面模型模拟结果及气候观测数据（降雨、蒸散发、径流），通过时间序列分析、聚类分析识别空间模式，并结合地下水观测数据进行对比验证。

Result: (1)TWS呈现三段式时间变化：2002-2009年负异常下降、2010-2017年正异常下降、2018-2025年混合异常上升；(2)识别出5个主导空间聚类模式；(3)TWS与降雨整体强相关但局部偏弱；(4)蒸发和径流对TWS有影响，组合模型显著提升解释力；(5)TWS反演的地下水储量变化与实测地下水位变化存在异同。

Conclusion: GRACE卫星数据与陆面模型结合能够有效揭示流域尺度水储量时空变化规律，为地下水资源管理提供重要支撑，但需考虑复杂水文地质过程和人类活动（如地下水开采）的影响。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该论文本身就是遥感（GRACE重力卫星）与水文模型结合的典型应用。改进方案：(1)引入更高分辨率的重力卫星数据或融合多源遥感数据（如SMAP土壤湿度、ICESat-2高程变化）提升空间分辨率；(2)结合机器/深度学习方法（如LSTM）改进TWS时间序列预测和缺失数据重建；(3)耦合地下水数值模型（如MODFLOW）提升地下水储量反演精度；(4)利用InSAR地表形变数据辅助约束地下水储量变化。

Abstract (英文): Spatial and temporal patterns of terrestrial water storage (TWS), and their relationship with groundwater levels, were investigated with the Gravity Recovery and Climate Experiment (GRACE) satellite data, the Global Land Data Assimilation System (GLDAS) land surface model results, and climate observations for the Murray–Darling Basin (MDB). The results show that: (1) TWS displays a clear temporal variability: a negative TWS anomaly with a declining trend during 2002–2009, a positive TWS anomaly with a decreasing trend during 2010–2017, and a period of mixed positive and negative TWS anomalies being accompanied by an increasing trend from 2018 to 2025; (2) five dominant cluster patterns were identified that explain the spatial variability of temporal TWS across the MDB; (3) overall, TWS temporal variability is strongly correlated with rainfall, although it is weak at certain locations; (4) TWS is also influenced by evaporation (both actual and potential evapotranspiration, AET and PET) and runoff, and a combined model significantly improves the overall performance in explaining TWS temporal variability; and (5) TWS-derived groundwater storage changes show both similarities and differences in comparison with groundwater level observation changes, reflecting complex hydrogeological processes and the influence of human activities such as groundwater extraction. These findings provide valuable insights to support improved groundwater resource management with GRACE satellite information and land surface models.

### [178] [S2M-Net: Dynamic Hyperspectral Unmixing Network Integrating Spectral Sequence Mamba and Local Spatial–Spectral Awareness](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132228)
*Yi Yang,Mei‐Yan Xu,Weidong Zhang,Ji Zhang,Yuquan Gan*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种动态高光谱解混网络，结合光谱序列Mamba（选择性状态空间模型，线性复杂度全局扫描）与局部空间-光谱感知（注意力增强CNN），通过非对称双流协同架构和空间自适应门控融合模块，在多个公开高光谱数据集上实现了显著优于现有方法的解混精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于深度学习的解混方法中，CNN感受野有限难以捕获长距离光谱依赖，Transformer虽有全局建模能力但计算复杂度呈二次增长且无法自适应过滤连续光谱波段中的冗余噪声，亟需一种兼具全局建模效率与局部细节感知能力的解混网络。

Method: 提出非对称双流协同架构：(1) 光谱序列Mamba分支将高光谱数据建模为一维连续序列，利用选择性状态空间模型以线性复杂度进行全局扫描，自适应过滤冗余波段以提取高纯度全局光谱语义；(2) 局部空间-光谱感知分支采用注意力增强CNN捕获局部连续光谱变化和空间纹理，为丰度估计提供细粒度几何边界约束；(3) 空间自适应门控融合模块根据不同空间区域的像素混合复杂度动态平衡全局光谱语义与局部空间-光谱细节。

Result: 在多个公开高光谱数据集上的大量实验表明，所提方法在解混精度上相较于对比方法取得了显著提升。

Conclusion: 将Mamba引入高光谱解混领域，以线性计算复杂度实现全局光谱建模并自适应过滤噪声，同时结合局部空间-光谱感知和自适应融合机制，有效解决了现有方法的瓶颈，为高光谱解混提供了新的高效范式。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。作为直接面向高光谱遥感解混的论文，改进方向包括：(1) 可引入多尺度Mamba机制，在不同光谱分辨率尺度上并行建模，增强对复杂混合像元的表征能力；(2) 局部分支可考虑使用可变形卷积或图卷积，更好地适配地物边界不规则几何结构；(3) 空间自适应门控融合可扩展为频谱-空间协同注意力机制，进一步提升融合的动态性与可解释性；(4) 可探索将Mamba与物理模型（如线性混合模型、双线性混合模型）结合，提升光谱语义的物理可解释性。

Abstract (英文): Hyperspectral unmixing aims to extract pure endmembers and their corresponding abundance from mixed pixels. Existing deep learning-based unmixing methods predominantly rely on convolutional neural networks (CNNs) or Transformer architectures. However, CNNs suffer from limited receptive fields and struggle to capture long-range spectral dependencies across the entire spectral sequence. While Transformers possess global modeling capabilities, they are constrained by quadratic computational complexity and lack the ability to adaptively filter redundant noise in consecutive spectral bands. To address these limitations, this paper proposes a dynamic hyperspectral unmixing network integrating a spectral sequence Mamba with local spatial–spectral awareness. Specifically, the network features a novel asymmetric dual-stream collaborative architecture. The first branch, the spectral sequence Mamba, models hyperspectral data as a one-dimensional continuous sequence and employs the selective state space model to perform global scanning with linear complexity. This adaptively filters redundant spectral bands to accurately extract high-purity global spectral semantics. The second branch, dedicated to local spatial–spectral awareness, uses an attention-augmented CNN to capture local continuous spectral variations and spatial textures, providing fine-grained geometric boundary constraints for abundance estimation. Furthermore, a spatially adaptive gated fusion module is designed to dynamically balance global spectral semantics and local spatial–spectral details according to the pixel mixing complexity of varying spatial regions. Extensive experiments on multiple public hyperspectral datasets demonstrate that the proposed method achieves significant improvements in unmixing accuracy over comparative methods.

### [179] [Spatiotemporal Evolution of Ecological Environment Quality and Driving Factors in the Loess Plateau of Northern Shaanxi](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132219)
*Ruize Tang,Z L Li,Shuangcheng Zhang,Junkai Gu,Jiandong Xiao*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究利用RSEI模型评估了2000-2024年陕北黄土高原生态环境质量的时空演变，发现整体呈波动上升趋势（均值从0.376升至0.545），空间上呈“南高北低、西北最低”格局，改善区域占91.21%，地貌类型是主导驱动因素（q=0.701），地貌-土地利用交互作用持续影响空间分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建RSEI遥感生态指数模型；采用Theil-Sen估计量、Mann-Kendall检验和Hurst指数检测变化显著性并预测未来趋势；运用Geodetector模型探索驱动因素。

Result: (1) EEQ呈波动上升趋势，均值从0.376升至0.545；(2)空间呈“南高北低、西北最低”格局，优良等级比例增加约20个百分点；(3)改善区域占91.21%，与未来改善预测高度重叠；(4)地貌类型影响最大（q=0.701），地貌-土地利用交互作用持续影响空间分布。

Conclusion: 研究表明陕北黄土高原生态环境质量整体改善，为精准生态修复规划和空间优化提供了科学依据。

Abstract (英文): Accurately assessing the spatiotemporal evolution of ecological environment quality (EEQ) on the Loess Plateau of Northern Shaanxi is of great significance for consolidating the ecological security barrier of the Yellow River Basin. Most of the existing research focuses on a single ecological theme, which does not reflect the overall ecological status of the region. In this study, a remote sensing ecological index (RSEI) model was constructed to systematically assess the EEQ from 2000 to 2024. The Theil–Sen estimator, Mann–Kendall test, and Hurst exponent were jointly employed to detect change significance and predict future trends, while the Geodetector model was applied to explore driving factors. The results were as follows: (1) EEQ exhibited a fluctuating but overall upward trend, with the mean RSEI rising from 0.376 in 2000 to 0.545 in 2024—an average annual increase of approximately 0.00569. (2) Spatially, a distinct pattern of “higher in the south, lower in the north and the lowest in the northwest” was observed. Over the 25-year period, the combined proportion of “excellent” and “good” grades increased by roughly 20 percentage points, and the “moderate” grade expanded from 13.61% to 47.12%. (3) Areas showing an improving trend accounted for 91.21% of the total area and highly overlapped with those projected to improve in the future. (4) Single-factor detection revealed that geomorphological type exerted the greatest influence on the spatial heterogeneity of EEQ, with a multi-year mean q-value of 0.701. Interaction detection further indicates that the geomorphology–land use interaction may continue to shape the regional EEQ’s spatial distribution. These findings provide a scientific basis for precise ecological restoration planning and spatial optimization on the Loess Plateau of Northern Shaanxi.

### [180] [Automated On-Orbit Absolute Radiometric Calibration: A Preliminary Method and Results](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132186)
*Xiaojie Yang,Qiuyan Liu,Song Yang,Yang Bai,Shuai Huang,Yingshan Sun,Jiangpeng Li,Hongyu Wu,Xing Zhong,Weibin Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文针对缺乏星上定标系统的吉林一号商业卫星星座，提出了一种利用MCD43A2和MCD12Q1产品生成定标区域矢量、结合MODTRAN查找表实现全自动在轨绝对辐射定标的方法，无需地面同步实验和额外成像资源，精度优于4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低成本商业卫星星座缺乏星上定标系统，现有替代方法难以实现低资源消耗下的大规模传感器星座自动化可靠定标，亟需一种适用于大量成像仪、使用广泛可得晴空地面目标的自动化定标方法。

Method: 利用MCD43A2和MCD12Q1产品生成定标区域矢量，将MODIS辐射基准传递至吉林一号；构建MODTRAN模型输入参数的查找表（LUT）；从吉林一号影像中提取定标像素和模型输入参数，插值LUT获取各像元各波段入瞳辐亮度，计算在轨绝对辐射定标系数。

Result: 基于RadCalNet对吉林一号GF02F PMS1传感器的场地定标验证显示，该方法所有波段的相对差异最大不超过4%。

Conclusion: 所提方法无需地面同步实验、自动化程度高、不占用商业成像资源，有效解决了吉林一号等无星上定标系统的商业卫星星座的大规模自动化定标问题。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：（1）将该方法推广至其他无星上定标的商业遥感星座（如高景、珠海一号等），构建通用化的自动定标流程；（2）引入深度学习替代MODTRAN查找表插值，提高大气参数反演效率与精度；（3）利用多源参考传感器（如Sentinel-2、Landsat 8/9）替代单MODIS基准，增强定标基准的鲁棒性；（4）扩展至SAR或高光谱传感器的交叉定标，利用MODIS等中分辨率数据生成矢量掩膜实现跨传感器定标传递。

Abstract (英文): On-orbit absolute radiometric calibration tracks sensor radiometric degradation and ensures accuracy for quantitative applications. Low-cost commercial satellites lack expensive on-board calibration systems, and traditional alternative methods cannot achieve automated, reliable calibration for large sensor fleets with low resource consumption. Pseudo-invariant calibration sites require no ground instruments, but commercial satellites’ heavy imaging schedules hinder frequent PICS observations. The Jilin-1 constellation is a large commercial constellation composed of satellites carrying multispectral imagers with resolution better than 1 m, and it has no on-board calibration system. Thus, an automated calibration method applicable to numerous imagers is needed, one that requires widely available clear-sky ground targets. Using MCD43A2 and MCD12Q1 products, we generate calibration region vectors to transfer the MODIS radiometric reference to Jilin-1. A look-up table (LUT) is constructed for the input parameters of the MODTRAN model. Calibration pixels and model input parameters are then extracted from Jilin-1 imagery using the region vectors, the LUT is interpolated to obtain the at-aperture radiance for each pixel and band, and on-orbit absolute radiometric calibration coefficients are calculated. The proposed method requires no ground-based synchronous experiments, achieves a high level of automation, and does not consume commercial imaging resources. The site calibration validation based on RadCalNet for the JL1GF02F PMS1 sensor shows that the maximum relative difference in the method across all bands is less than 4%.

### [181] [Assessing the Potential of EMIT Hyperspectral Data Combined with DEM-Derived Terrain Variables for Predicting Soil As, Cu and Zn Concentrations in a Mountainous Region of Southwest China](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132211)
*Guangping Qie,Minzi Wang,Ziping Pan,Z X Sun,Wenjin Xie,Zhiyi Liu,Guangxing Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究利用EMIT高光谱数据与地形变量，在贵州仁怀山区评估土壤砷(As)、铜(Cu)、锌(Zn)浓度。随机森林和XGBoost模型经空间交叉验证后，As模型效果尚可(R²=0.460)，Cu效果较弱(R²=0.188)，Zn未优于基准模型(R²=-0.028)。表明EMIT数据在该区域对As有中等预测潜力，对Cu和Zn的预测能力有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 星载成像光谱为区域尺度土壤属性监测提供了新机遇，但在山区环境（尤其是使用EMIT高光谱数据）预测土壤重金属浓度的能力尚未得到充分验证。该研究旨在填补这一空白，评估EMIT数据在复杂地形条件下预测土壤As、Cu、Zn含量的可行性。

Method: 1) 使用EMIT Level-2A地表反射率数据与DEM衍生的地形变量作为预测因子；2) 仅保留在有效EMIT覆盖范围内的土壤样本（As:139, Cu:136, Zn:130）；3) 对EMIT光谱变量和地形因子进行筛选以降低多重共线性；4) 采用随机森林和XGBoost模型，并通过重复空间交叉验证评估性能。

Result: As最优模型结合EMIT预测因子与高程，验证R²=0.460；Cu模型验证R²=0.188；Zn模型验证R²=-0.028，未优于均值基准。空间预测图与残差模式表明：As具有中等预测潜力，Cu预测价值有限，Zn仅为探索性制图而非可靠预测。

Conclusion: EMIT高光谱数据在山区土壤重金属预测中表现因元素而异：对As有一定应用潜力，对Cu预测能力较弱，对Zn在当前样本和预测因子条件下不具备可靠预测能力。未来需要更大样本量和更优的预测变量来提升模型性能。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：70%。改进方向：1) 引入更多辅助变量，如植被指数、土壤母质类型、土地利用数据等，弥补纯光谱信息的不足；2) 尝试深度学习方法（如CNN、LSTM）提取光谱-空间联合特征；3) 采用迁移学习或域适应方法，利用其他区域已训练的土壤重金属模型提升泛化能力；4) 增加样本量，或采用半监督学习利用未标注样本；5) 对Zn等弱相关元素，可探索光谱微分变换或连续谱去除等预处理增强光谱-浓度关联。

Abstract (英文): Spaceborne imaging spectroscopy has created new opportunities for monitoring soil properties at regional scales. Its use for predicting soil heavy metal concentrations in mountainous environments, however, remains insufficiently tested, especially when EMIT hyperspectral data are used. In this study, EMIT Level-2A surface reflectance data were integrated with DEM-derived terrain variables to estimate soil arsenic (As), copper (Cu), and zinc (Zn) concentrations in Renhuai, Guizhou Province, Southwest China. Only soil samples falling within valid EMIT coverage were used for element-specific modeling, resulting in 139 samples for As, 136 for Cu, and 130 for Zn. To reduce redundancy among predictors, EMIT spectral variables and terrain factors were screened before model construction. Random forest and XGBoost models were then tested using repeated spatial cross-validation. The best-performing model for As combined EMIT predictors with elevation and achieved a validation R2 of 0.460. Model performance was considerably weaker for Cu, with a validation R2 of 0.188. For Zn, the model failed to outperform the mean-based benchmark, producing a negative validation R2 of −0.028. The spatial prediction maps and residual patterns suggested that the EMIT-based prediction showed moderate potential for As, limited predictive value for Cu, and exploratory rather than reliable mapping capability for Zn under the current sample and predictor conditions.

Abstract (英文): Imagery is fundamental to modern scientific research, making robust intrinsic camera calibration indispensable for accurate visual inference. The checkerboard-based calibration method has long been favored for its simplicity and ease of deployment and is widely used even in mission-critical computer vision pipelines. However, its limitations in modeling high-precision camera geometry can compromise downstream performance in tasks requiring geometric accuracy. In this work, camera calibration is revisited through the lens of photogrammetric self-calibration (PSC), and it is demonstrated that the PSC consistently outperforms the checkerboard method in both accuracy and precision across a range of vision tasks, including 3D reconstruction with structure from motion (SfM), visual simultaneous localization and mapping (SLAM), and novel-view synthesis and reconstruction. Our findings advocate for a paradigm shift toward calibration methods that better reflect the physical and projective properties of camera systems in real-world deployments for critical computer vision applications.

### [183] [Multi-Modal Multi-Scale Mamba with Frequency and Semantics-Guided Spectral Modeling for Hyperspectral Image Classification](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132207)
*Hui Peng,Wenzhun Huang,Kaihong Chen,Zhongyan Zhou,Zhen Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出M3-Mamba框架，结合语言引导、多层级和基于Mamba的状态空间建模，用于高光谱图像分类。该框架利用多模态语义先验指导光谱建模，引入频域感知的Mamba模块高效捕获长程光谱依赖，并通过文本引导调制策略自适应重加权光谱响应。在Indian Pines、Pavia University、Salinas和Houston四个基准数据集上取得竞争性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高光谱图像分类面临光谱冗余度高、光谱-空间相关性复杂、标注样本有限等挑战，现有方法难以在捕获长程光谱依赖的同时避免二次计算复杂度，且缺乏有效的语义引导机制来抑制噪声波段和增强类判别性光谱响应。

Method: (1) 语言引导的多层级Mamba光谱建模框架(M3-Mamba)；(2) 频域感知的Mamba状态空间模块，高效捕获长程光谱依赖，避免注意力机制的二次复杂度；(3) 文本引导调制策略，在语义指导下自适应重加权光谱响应，抑制冗余/噪声波段，增强类相关光谱响应。

Result: 在Indian Pines、Pavia University、Salinas和Houston四个基准数据集上，M3-Mamba在总体精度、平均精度和Kappa系数上均取得竞争性结果。消融实验验证了各关键组件的有效性。

Conclusion: M3-Mamba框架通过语言引导的语义-光谱调制有效应对光谱变异和类间混淆问题，为高光谱图像分类提供了一种有前景的方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感高光谱图像分类的论文，改进方向包括：(1) 可将语言引导的语义先验扩展为遥感领域专用的地理/地物知识图谱，提供更精准的语义约束；(2) 频域Mamba模块可进一步与空间Mamba结合，构建光谱-空间双分支Mamba架构，同时捕获光谱和空间长程依赖；(3) 文本引导调制策略可迁移至多模态遥感数据融合（如HSI+LiDAR+SAR），实现跨模态语义-光谱协同调制。

Abstract (英文): Hyperspectral image (HSI) classification remains a challenging task due to high spectral redundancy, complex spectral–spatial correlations, and the limited availability of labeled samples. To address these issues, this paper proposes a novel framework termed M3-Mamba, which integrates language-guided, multi-level, and Mamba-based spectral modeling for hyperspectral image classification. The proposed M3-Mamba leverages high-level semantic priors derived from multimodal representations to guide discriminative spectral modeling, enabling effective interaction between semantic information and fine-grained spectral features. In addition, a frequency-aware Mamba-based state space module is introduced to efficiently capture long-range spectral dependencies while avoiding the quadratic computational complexity of conventional attention mechanisms. Meanwhile, a text-guided modulation strategy is designed to adaptively reweight spectral responses under semantic guidance, suppressing redundant or noisy bands and enhancing class-relevant spectral responses without compromising spectral fidelity. This semantic-to-spectral modulation allows M3-Mamba to better cope with spectral variability and inter-class confusion. Extensive experiments conducted on four widely used benchmark datasets, including Indian Pines, Pavia University, Salinas, and Houston datasets, demonstrate thatM3-Mamba achieves competitive overall accuracy, average accuracy, and Kappa coefficient under the adopted benchmark settings. Ablation studies further validate the effectiveness of each key component, confirming that the proposed framework demonstrates promising effectiveness for hyperspectral image classification.

Abstract (英文): Semantic segmentation of high-resolution remote sensing (HRRS) imagery is a fundamental task in Earth observation but remains challenging due to severe scale variations and complex boundary structures. Although State Space Models (SSMs), particularly Mamba, have shown strong potential for efficient global modeling with linear complexity, existing methods are still limited in capturing multi-scale context and fine-grained spatial details. To address these issues, we propose a novel framework named WASP-Mamba for HRRS image segmentation. A Mamba-based spatial pyramid pooling module is introduced at the encoder bottleneck to enhance multi-scale feature aggregation and improve robustness to scale variations. In addition, a wavelet-inspired Mamba decoder is designed to decouple and reconstruct low-frequency semantic information and high-frequency details, mitigating boundary degradation caused by conventional upsampling. Extensive experiments on the LoveDA, ISPRS Vaihingen and ISPRS Potsdam datasets demonstrate that the proposed method achieves 53.90%, 84.32% and 87.06% mIoU, respectively. Compared with recent state-of-the-art methods, WASP-Mamba achieves superior segmentation performance.

A specific combination of binary forest maps from global products, where the output forest area consisted of forests mapped at the same time by all three products and forests mapped at the same time only by GDW and ESA WC yielded better accuracy indicators than any single product and other tested combinations (F1-score equal to 80.4%, and IoU against S2GLC PL equal to 87.1%).

### [186] [SMMNet: A Plug-and-Play Lightweight Detection Framework for UAV Aerial Imagery](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132232)
*Minna Liu,Zhigang Luo,Yaowen Hu,Jialang Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出SMMNet，一种轻量级即插即用的无人机航拍图像目标检测框架，通过结构化扩散特征提取、Mamba驱动的上下文聚合和贝叶斯框精化三个模块，在保持实时性的同时显著提升检测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无人机航拍图像中的目标检测面临密集小目标、尺度变化大、背景复杂以及机载计算资源严格受限等挑战，现有方法难以在精度与效率之间取得良好平衡。

Method: SMMNet包含三个核心模块：1）结构化扩散特征提取器（SDFE），利用各向异性扩散在下采样过程中保留边界敏感特征；2）Mamba驱动的感受野上下文聚合器（MRCA），通过多方向选择性状态空间扫描以线性复杂度捕获长程上下文；3）掩码引导的贝叶斯框精化（MBBR），利用MobileSAM掩码证据和ELBO伪阳性过滤实现MAP启发的置信度自适应框更新。整体框架即插即用，兼容YOLO系列检测器。

Result: 以YOLOv13-S为主检测器，SMMNet在VisDrone2019上达到32.8% mAP@0.5:0.95和52.6% mAP@0.5，在A800 GPU上87 FPS，相比基线分别提升3.6和4.5个点。三独立种子实验显示平均增益：VisDrone2019为3.60±0.10 mAP，DroneVehicle为2.53±0.12 mAP，SeaDronesSee为2.77±0.06 mAP。在Jetson Orin NX上15W TDP下TensorRT FP16推理达30 FPS。

Conclusion: SMMNet在无人机航拍目标检测中实现了优异的精度-延迟权衡，模块化设计使其易于集成到现有检测器，边缘部署验证了其在资源受限场景下的适用性，为实时无人机感知提供了可行的轻量化方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感领域（无人机航拍）的论文。改进方向：1）SDFE模块可进一步引入多尺度各向异性扩散策略以适应遥感图像中更极端的尺度变化；2）MRCA的Mamba扫描可结合遥感图像特有的空间谱信息进行多模态融合；3）MBBR的贝叶斯框架可扩展至遥感目标的不确定性量化，用于云遮挡等场景的鲁棒检测；4）当前仅验证了YOLO系列，可探索与ViT、DETR等基于注意力的遥感检测器结合。

Abstract (英文): Object detection in UAV aerial imagery is challenged by dense small targets, large-scale variation, complex backgrounds, and strict onboard computation limits. To address these issues, this paper proposes SMMNet (Structured-diffusion Mamba Mixture Network), a lightweight plug-and-play detection framework evaluated with YOLO family detectors. SMMNet contains three modules. The Structured Diffusion Feature Extractor (SDFE) uses anisotropic diffusion to preserve boundary-sensitive features during downsampling. The Mamba-driven Receptive-field Context Aggregator (MRCA) performs multi-directional selective state-space scanning to capture long-range context with linear complexity. The Mask-guided Bayesian Box Refinement (MBBR) applies a MAP-inspired confidence-adaptive box update using MobileSAM mask evidence and ELBO-based false-positive filtering. Using YOLOv13-S as the main detector, SMMNet achieves 32.8% mAP@0.5:0.95 and 52.6% mAP@0.5 on VisDrone2019 at 87 FPS on an NVIDIA A800 GPU, improving the YOLOv13-S baseline by 3.6 and 4.5 points, respectively. The added modules reduce throughput compared with the detector-only baseline (168 FPS), but the resulting 87 FPS remains real-time and provides a favorable accuracy–latency trade-off. Three independent-seed runs further show a mean paired gain of 3.60 ± 0.10 mAP on VisDrone2019, 2.53 ± 0.12 mAP on DroneVehicle, and 2.77 ± 0.06 mAP on SeaDronesSee for the YOLOv13-S setting. Additional experiments on DroneVehicle and SeaDronesSee, together with cross-backbone evaluations on YOLOv5/v6/v7/v8/v10/v11/v13 across different UAV benchmarks, show aligned performance trends under matched settings. Edge deployment on an NVIDIA Jetson Orin NX reaches 30 FPS under TensorRT FP16 inference at 15 W TDP, indicating the suitability of SMMNet for resource-constrained UAV perception.

### [187] [Enhanced DINO for Cross-Domain Transmission Tower Detection Using Remote Sensing Images](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132198)
*Junjie Wang,Jiahe Tian,Lingli Zhao,Ningsheng Liao,Jie Yang,Lei Shi*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于增强DINO的跨域输电塔检测框架，通过查询级目标门控（QOG）模块、MPDIoU回归和质量感知评分模块（QSM）三个轻量化优化模块，有效缓解了不同地理区域遥感图像中输电塔检测的域偏移问题，在10%目标域标注设置下F1-score达0.8556，mAP@0.5达0.8684，优于DINO基线及YOLOv8/v9/v11等主流检测器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不同地理区域的遥感图像中，输电塔的结构、规模和背景纹理差异显著，导致在一个区域训练的模型直接应用于另一区域时检测精度大幅下降。现有方法难以有效解决这种跨域检测中的域偏移问题。

Method: 提出基于增强DINO的跨域输电塔检测框架，包含三个轻量化优化模块：(1) 查询级目标门控（QOG）模块，通过估计每个查询的目标性分数自适应地重新加权解码器查询，抑制背景主导的查询；(2) MPDIoU回归损失，提高细长输电塔目标的定位精度；(3) 质量感知评分模块（QSM），利用预测的定位质量logits校准分类置信度，减少因边界框对齐不佳导致的高置信度误检。

Result: 在两个不同地理区域的遥感图像数据集上，10%目标域标注设置下：精度0.8947，召回率0.8199，F1-score 0.8556，mAP@0.5 0.8684，优于原始DINO基线及YOLOv8、YOLOv9、YOLOv11等主流检测器。

Conclusion: 提出的框架为遥感图像中细长输电塔目标的鲁棒跨域检测提供了有效解决方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：(1) QOG模块可进一步引入多尺度特征融合机制，增强对不同尺寸输电塔的适应性；(2) 可引入自监督对比学习或域对抗训练策略，进一步提升跨域泛化能力；(3) MPDIoU可结合旋转目标检测（如RPN）以更好适配遥感图像中任意朝向的细长目标；(4) QSM可与不确定性估计结合，提供更鲁棒的置信度校准；(5) 可扩展至其他细长线性地物（如电力线、桥梁、道路）的跨域检测。

Abstract (英文): Transmission towers are fundamental components of electric power networks. However, their structure, scale and background textures vary substantially across remote sensing images acquired from different geographic regions. These discrepancies often reduce the detection accuracy of a model trained in one region when it is applied to another region. This paper proposes an enhanced DINO-based framework for cross-domain transmission tower detection that incorporates three lightweight optimisation modules. First, a Query-level Objectness Gating (QOG) module adaptively reweights decoder queries by estimating per-query objectness scores, thereby suppressing background-dominated queries. Second, MPDIoU regression is used to improve the localisation accuracy of elongated transmission tower targets. Third, a Quality-aware Scoring Module (QSM) calibrates classification confidence using predicted localisation-quality logits, thereby reducing high-confidence false detections caused by poor box alignment. Experiments are conducted on two remote sensing image datasets from different geographic regions. Under the 10% target-domain annotation setting, the proposed method achieves a precision of 0.8947, a recall of 0.8199, an F1-score of 0.8556 and an mAP@0.5 of 0.8684, outperforming the original DINO baseline and mainstream detectors including YOLOv8, YOLOv9 and YOLOv11. The results demonstrate that the proposed framework provides an effective solution for robust cross-domain detection of slender transmission tower targets in remote sensing images.

### [188] [TreeFlow: Conditional Flow Matching for 3D Tree Point Cloud Generation from Inventory Attributes](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132197)
*Anthony Marcozzi,Johnathan Tenny,Daithi Martin,Juan Castorena,Zachary Crennen,Lucas Wells,Samuel Hillman*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: TreeFlow是一种基于条件流匹配模型，利用真实激光扫描数据训练Transformer，根据树种、采集平台和树高生成逼真的三维树木点云，在六项评估指标中五项达到了接近真实树木的水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 树木的三维结构对于火灾建模、辐射传输模拟、合成数据生成和森林数字孪生至关重要，但现有方法使用光滑几何体近似树冠，忽略了真实树木中的聚集、间隙和不规则分枝结构，缺乏精确的三维树木表示。

Method: 采用条件流匹配模型（conditional flow matching），基于Transformer架构，在FOR-species20K基准的真实激光扫描数据上训练，学习一个将高斯分布样本传输到源数据分布的velocity field，输入条件为树种、采集平台和树高。

Result: 在六项指标中的五项达到或接近同类基线水平，Chamfer距离为0.581 m（真实树木为0.559 m）；在25 m以下性能最佳，随树高增加性能下降。

Conclusion: TreeFlow能够基于标量清单属性生成单棵树木的点云，完全基于真实激光扫描数据训练，为大规模获取三维树木结构提供了可行方案。

Abstract (英文): Accurate three-dimensional representations of tree structure are essential for fire modeling, radiative transfer simulation, synthetic data generation, and digital twins of forests, yet detailed 3D structure is rarely available at required scales. Current approaches approximate crowns with smooth geometric primitives, discarding the clumping, gaps, and irregular branching present in real trees. We present TreeFlow, a conditional flow matching model that generates realistic 3D tree point clouds from species, acquisition platform, and height. The model uses a transformer trained on real laser scanning data from the FOR-species20K benchmark to learn a velocity field transporting samples from a Gaussian distribution to the source data distribution. We evaluate generation quality by comparing conditioning and distributional fidelity metrics to scans of real trees. Generated trees match or approach the intra-class baseline on five of six metrics, with a Chamfer distance of 0.581 m versus 0.559 m for real trees of the same genus and height class. Performance is strongest below 25 m and degrades with increasing height. TreeFlow generates individual-tree point clouds conditioned on scalar inventory attributes using a model trained entirely on real laser scanning data.

### [189] [Fine-Grained Spaceborne SAR Ship Classification into Nine Categories via AIS Association](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132223)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SAR舰船检测已取得显著进展，但SAR舰船分类研究相对不足，主要原因是缺乏可靠的类别标签。AIS系统能提供船舶身份、类型和动态轨迹信息，可弥补SAR图像难以直接获取船舶类型信息的缺陷。

Method: 1) 将原始AIS船舶类型重新组织为九种细粒度SAR舰船类别；2) 通过全局最优匹配策略将AIS船舶类型信息迁移至SAR检测结果；3) 仅保留高置信度的SAR-AIS匹配对并裁剪对应SAR舰船切片，构建含4472个舰船切片的分类数据集；4) 训练ConvNeXt-Tiny等分类器实现仅依赖SAR图像的舰船分类。

Result: 在基于真实AIS记录的蒙特卡洛实验中，所提关联策略在近距离舰船模糊、空间扰动、干扰AIS候选和AIS静态尺寸误差等场景下，比对比关联方法生成更可靠的高置信度标签。在构建的分类数据集基准实验中，ConvNeXt-Tiny在主流分类器中取得最佳性能。

Conclusion: AIS关联可为SAR舰船分类提供可靠的类别监督，训练后的分类器能够仅利用SAR图像完成舰船分类任务。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感领域论文。改进方向：1) 可引入多时相SAR图像与时序AIS匹配，进一步提升匹配可靠性；2) 探索利用自监督学习或半监督学习减少对高置信度匹配对的依赖；3) 可扩展至更大规模的细粒度分类（>9类）或增加对非合作船舶的识别能力；4) 融入SAR极化信息提升分类器对相似类型舰船的区分能力；5) 考虑AIS数据缺失或稀疏场景下的鲁棒分类方法。

Abstract (英文): Spaceborne Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR) provides all-weather, day and night and wide-area imaging capability, and plays a critical role in maritime surveillance. While substantial progress has been achieved in SAR ship detection, SAR ship classification remains relatively underexplored, mainly due to the scarcity of reliable category labels. Automatic Identification System (AIS) provides vessel identity, type, and dynamic trajectory information, and thus offers vessel type information that is difficult to obtain directly from SAR imagery. This paper proposes a fine-grained nine-category SAR ship classification method based on AIS association, which reorganizes the original AIS vessel types into nine fine-grained categories of SAR ship, transfers AIS vessel type information to SAR detection through a global optimal matching strategy, and supports SAR-only vessel category recognition. By retaining only high-confidence SAR and AIS matched pairs and cropping the corresponding SAR ship chips, an SAR ship classification dataset containing 4472 ship chips across the nine categories is constructed. In Monte Carlo experiments based on real AIS records, the proposed association strategy achieves more reliable high-confidence label generation than the compared association methods under close ship ambiguity, spatial perturbation, distractor AIS candidates, and AIS static size errors. In the benchmark experiment on the constructed classification dataset, ConvNeXt-Tiny achieves the best performance among the compared mainstream classifiers. These results demonstrate that AIS association can provide reliable category supervision for SAR ship classification, and the trained classifier can perform ship classification using SAR imagery alone.

### [190] [Assessing Potential Spatial Conflicts Between Projected Quercus Habitat Suitability and Future Land-Use Patterns in China: A Multi-Scenario MaxEnt–PLUS Simulation](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132195)
*Jiali Duan,Dongdong Zhang,Zhongke Feng,Zhichao Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 该研究开发了MaxEnt与PLUS模型的软耦合框架，结合16种SSP气候与土地利用情景组合，评估了中国栎属植物未来适宜栖息地与人类土地利用模式之间的空间重叠。结果表明：气候变暖将导致栎属栖息地向北/向西扩张和低纬度地区收缩，但未来建设用地和耕地扩张可能显著压缩其实际可用空间；高排放情景下新增适宜栖息地与建设用地重叠高达5.90×10⁴ km²、与耕地重叠达36.42×10⁴ km²；生态保护情景下与非生态用地重叠更少，可实现的栖息地扩张面积更大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仅考虑气候变化的物种分布评估可能高估未来适宜栖息地的空间可用性，因为忽略了动态土地利用变化的影响。需要将气候驱动的栖息地适宜性变化与人类土地利用格局进行综合评估，以识别潜在的空间冲突。

Method: 采用软耦合框架，集成MaxEnt模型（气候适宜性建模）和PLUS模型（土地利用模拟），并构建Habitat-Land-Use Conflict Index (HLCI) 作为分类空间叠加框架，在格网尺度上对16种SSP气候路径与土地利用情景组合下的适宜栖息地与未来用地类型进行重叠分类评估。

Result: (1) 气候变暖可能重塑栎属栖息地适宜性，表现为向北/向西扩张和部分低纬度地区收缩；(2) 未来土地利用模式可能通过增加与建设用地和耕地的重叠来降低适宜栖息地的空间可用性，高排放情景下新增适宜栖息地与建设用地重叠达5.90×10⁴ km²，与耕地重叠达36.42×10⁴ km²；(3) 生态保护情景下与非生态用地类别的重叠较低，可实现的栖息地扩张面积更大。

Conclusion: 该研究为未来栎属栖息地适宜性与人类土地利用格局的重叠提供了基于情景的空间评估，可为适应性森林保护和国土空间规划提供大尺度支撑。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该研究本身即为遥感与生态学交叉的范例，可从以下方面改进：(1) 引入更高分辨率遥感数据（如Sentinel-2、Landsat时序）替代粗分辨率土地利用数据，提升栖息地-用地冲突识别的空间精度；(2) 集成微波遥感数据（如Sentinel-1）监测森林冠层结构和物候变化，弥补光学数据在云雨地区的不足；(3) 利用遥感植被指数（NDVI/EVI/KNDVI）时序特征作为MaxEnt模型的环境变量替代或补充，提高栖息地适宜性建模的生态真实性；(4) 将HLCI框架扩展到遥感变化检测中，结合时序遥感影像实现冲突区域的动态监测与早期预警。

Abstract (英文): Global warming is driving large-scale shifts in the climatically suitable habitats of many species. However, climate-only species distribution assessments may overestimate the spatial availability of future suitable habitats when dynamic land-use change is not considered. To assess potential spatial overlaps between climate-driven habitat suitability shifts and human land-use patterns, this study focuses on Quercus L. as a widely distributed keystone forest taxon in China. The genus-level assessment was designed to identify broad-scale habitat–land-use conflict patterns under multiple climate pathways and territorial spatial planning scenarios, rather than to predict species-specific distribution responses. We developed a soft-coupled framework integrating the Maximum Entropy (MaxEnt) model and the Patch-generating Land-Use Simulation (PLUS) model, and applied the Habitat–Land-Use Conflict Index (HLCI) as a categorical spatial overlay framework to classify potential overlaps between projected suitable habitats and future land-use categories across 16 exploratory scenario combinations integrating Shared Socioeconomic Pathway (SSP)-based climate projections and land-use/land-cover (LULC) scenarios for the 2040s at the grid scale. The results indicate that: (1) climate warming may reshape Quercus habitat suitability, characterized by northward/westward expansion and southward contraction in some low-latitude regions; (2) future land-use patterns may reduce the spatial availability of projected suitable habitats by increasing their overlap with built-up land and cultivated land. Under high-emission scenarios, potential newly suitable habitats overlapped with built-up land by up to 5.90 × 104 km2 and with cultivated land by up to 36.42 × 104 km2; and (3) the Ecological Protection scenario showed lower overlap with non-ecological land-use categories and a larger area of potentially realizable habitat expansion. This study provides a scenario-based spatial assessment of where future Quercus habitat suitability may overlap with human land-use patterns, offering broad-scale support for adaptive forest conservation and territorial spatial planning.

### [191] [3D Gaussian Splatting for Large-Scale Remote Sensing: A PRISMA-Informed Scoping Review of Scalability, Geometric Reliability, and Benchmarking Across UAV/Aerial and Satellite Imagery](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132224)
*Wenbao Fan,Bo Wang,Junqiang Ye,Ruoyu Zha,H T Chen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3DGS在遥感领域（无人机/航空摄影测量、卫星重建、大场景缩放、表面建模、地理空间评估）的应用碎片化，缺乏系统性综述和统一的评估基准，亟需梳理现有方法、分类体系并建立可靠的评估框架。

Method: 采用PRISMA-informed范围综述方法，从Web of Science、Scopus、IEEE Xplore等数据库筛选55篇核心文献；提出分面分类法（按平台、传感器模型、可扩展性策略、几何监督组织文献）；综合分析可扩展性策略（划分、层次、压缩、前馈推理）及其对度量几何的保障能力。

Result: 划分、层次、压缩和前馈推理改善了可扩展性，但不能保证度量几何；可靠的部署还需要传感器一致性投影、几何/地理配准约束、显式监督标签和产品级评估；在无控制点场景下，内部一致性与独立验证精度需区分对待。

Conclusion: 提出了一个平台感知的基准框架，统一记录无人机/航空、卫星和混合场景下的视觉保真度、计算成本、度量几何、产品效用、失败行为和可重复性元数据，为3DGS在遥感中的可靠应用提供了标准化评估路径。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感领域的3DGS综述，提出的建议可直接用于改进：1）在3DGS框架中集成传感器一致性投影模型（如RPC模型用于卫星、共线方程用于航空影像）；2）引入几何/地理配准约束（如GPS/IMU先验、地面控制点）作为优化正则项；3）采用产品级评估指标（如绝对定位精度、表面法向一致性）替代仅依赖渲染视觉质量；4）构建统一基准时需区分不同平台（UAV/卫星/混合）的误差特性。

Abstract (英文): 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) offers efficient explicit rendering, but large-scale remote-sensing use remains fragmented across UAV/aerial photogrammetry, satellite reconstruction, large-scene scaling, surface modeling, and geospatial evaluation. We present a Preferred Reporting Items for Systematic Reviews and Meta-Analyses (PRISMA)-informed scoping review based on 55 core studies identified through Web of Science, Scopus, IEEE Xplore, and supplementary searches completed on 3 June 2026. A faceted taxonomy organizes the literature by platform, sensor model, scalability strategy, and geometric supervision. The synthesis shows that partitioning, hierarchy, compression, and feed-forward inference improve scalability but do not guarantee metric geometry. Reliable deployment additionally requires sensor-consistent projection, geometric or georeferencing constraints, explicit supervision labels, and product-level evaluation. In control-point-free settings, internal consistency should be distinguished from independently validated accuracy. We therefore propose a platform-aware benchmark framework that jointly records visual fidelity, computational cost, metric geometry, product utility, failure behavior, and reproducibility metadata for UAV/aerial, satellite, and hybrid settings.

### [192] [SC-Net: Structural Constrained Contrastive Learning for Landslide Extraction Toward Power Transmission Corridor Safety Monitoring](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132216)
*Wei Song,S. Liu,S S Wu,Cheng Liao,Zongyuan Wu,Shiming Li,X B Zheng,Yanping Duan*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结构约束对比学习网络（SC-Net），用于从遥感影像中可靠提取滑坡信息。该方法通过多结构特征提取模块捕获滑坡几何特征，利用注意力自适应融合模块融合多尺度语义特征，并引入掩码约束的实例级对比学习策略增强滑坡与非滑坡区域的判别性。在CAS滑坡数据集上，SC-Net在CAS-UAV和CAS-SAT数据集上分别达到89.89%和79.76%的IoU，优于现有最佳方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 滑坡是常见且破坏性极强的地质灾害，严重威胁基础设施系统的长期稳定性。远距离输电走廊常穿越山区和森林区域，滑坡会危及塔基和输电线路安全。这些滑坡主要发生在植被茂密的斜坡区域，密集植被造成严重遮挡，模糊了滑坡边界，并与周围地物产生强烈的视觉相似性，导致从遥感影像中准确高效地识别滑坡仍是一个重大挑战。

Method: 1) 多结构特征提取模块：捕获滑坡特有的几何结构特征；2) 注意力自适应特征融合模块：融合从预训练骨干网络提取的多尺度语义表示；3) 掩码约束的实例级对比学习策略：在滑坡实例层面强制全局结构一致性，提高滑坡与非滑坡区域的可判别性。

Result: 在公开CAS滑坡数据集上，SC-Net在CAS-UAV和CAS-SAT数据集上分别达到89.89%和79.76%的IoU，分别比最佳基线方法高出2.09%和0.46%。

Conclusion: 所提方法为大规模滑坡监测提供了有效解决方案，并在输电走廊巡检和基础设施安全评估中展现出应用潜力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。改进方案：1) 可引入多时相遥感数据（如InSAR形变信息）作为额外输入模态，提升对早期滑坡的识别能力；2) 当前方法主要基于可见光影像，可扩展融合SAR或LiDAR数据以穿透植被遮挡；3) 对比学习策略可进一步引入域适应机制，增强模型在不同地理区域和传感器间的泛化能力；4) 可结合边缘检测分支细化滑坡边界，解决植被遮挡导致的边界模糊问题。

Abstract (英文): Landslides are among the most common and destructive geological hazards and pose a significant threat to the long-term stability of infrastructure systems. In particular, long-distance power transmission corridors often traverse mountainous and forested regions, where landslides can endanger tower foundations and transmission line safety. Such landslides predominantly occur in sloped forested areas, where dense vegetation causes severe occlusion that blurs landslide boundaries and creates strong visual similarity with surrounding land covers. Consequently, accurate and efficient landslide identification from remote sensing imagery remains a significant challenge. To address these challenges, we propose a structural constrained contrastive learning network (SC-Net) for reliable landslide extraction from remote sensing images. First, a multi-structural feature extraction module is designed to capture landslide-specific geometric characteristics. These features are further enhanced by fusing multi-scale semantic representations extracted from a pretrained backbone network through an attention-based adaptive feature fusion module. Additionally, a mask-constrained object-level contrastive learning strategy is introduced to enforce global structural consistency at the landslide object-level, thereby improving the discriminability between landslide and non-landslide regions. Extensive experiments conducted on the publicly available CAS landslide dataset demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed method. The proposed SC-Net achieves IoU scores of 89.89% and 79.76% on the CAS-UAV and CAS-SAT datasets, respectively, outperforming the best-performing baseline by 2.09% and 0.46%. The proposed method provides an effective solution for large-scale landslide monitoring and demonstrates potential for applications in power transmission corridor inspection and infrastructure safety assessment.

### [193] [Multi-Level Classification of Urban Green Space Using Multi-Source Remote Sensing and Geospatial Data](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132192)
*Aizhu Zhang,Jiahao Cheng,Xinyuan Su,Wenhai Zhu,Genyun Sun*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种融合多源遥感和地理空间大数据的多层次城市绿地分类方法，通过BERT微调实现社会功能语义重建，并设计MSSANet网络进行精细植被分类，最终建立“功能优先、植被其次”的耦合范式，在中国济南和青岛验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有城市绿地监测仅关注物理层植被提取，忽略了功能属性，导致监测结果无法客观反映绿地规划的合理性。为弥合物理层与功能层之间的语义鸿沟，本文提出多层次分类方法。

Method: 1) 构建社会功能底图：通过BERT微调与跨映射规则，结合POI、OSM和全球城市边界数据，将城市区域划分为24个功能类别；2) 物理层植被分类：设计多形状与光谱感知网络（MSSANet）进行精细植被分类；3) 耦合范式：建立“功能优先、植被其次”的耦合框架，依据中国城市绿地分类标准（CJJ/T 85-2017），构建3个功能属性层，形成5大类、11中类、24小类的多层次绿地分类体系。

Result: 在济南和青岛的实验表明，该方法能够有效实现精细的多层次城市绿地制图。

Conclusion: 所提出的多层次分类方法成功弥合了城市绿地监测中物理层与功能层之间的语义鸿沟，为城市绿地规划合理性评估提供了更客观的技术支持。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。作为遥感与自然语言处理/地理大数据交叉的典型工作，后续可从以下方面改进：1) 引入时间序列遥感数据（如Landsat/Sentinel时序）增强植被物候特征的区分能力；2) 将MSSANet扩展为多模态融合架构，直接整合POI语义特征与光谱-空间特征进行端到端学习；3) 探索自监督/弱监督学习范式降低对精细标注样本的依赖；4) 引入街景图像等视觉数据补充社会功能层的细粒度信息；5) 将该框架迁移至其他城市功能区分类任务（如不透水面功能识别）。

Abstract (英文): Urban Green Spaces (UGSs) monitoring usually focuses on the extraction of vegetation in the physical layer, while neglecting their functional attributes. This renders the monitoring results unable to objectively reflect the rationality of UGS planning. To address these issues, this study proposes a multi-level classification method integrating multi-source remote sensing and geospatial big data to bridge the semantic gap between the physical layer and the functional layer. In this method, a strategy of prior knowledge injection and semantic reconstruction was developed through the fine-tuning of a BERT model with cross-mapping rules. This strategy aims to classify the urban area into 24 functional categories, generating the social-functional basemap in a functional layer, based on Point of Interest (POI), OpenStreetMap (OSM), and Global Urban Boundary (GUB). Meanwhile, a novel deep learning architecture, namely the Multi-Shape and Spectral Aware Network (MSSANet), was designed for precise vegetation classification of UGSs in the physical layer. Finally, a “function-first, vegetation-second” coupling paradigm containing three functional attribute layers, referring to the Code for Classification of UGS in China (CJJ/T 85-2017), was established. This paradigm integrates the social-functional basemap with physical vegetation patches to build a multi-level UGS classification framework, i.e., the 5 major UGS categories, 11 intermediate UGS categories, and 24 fine-grained UGS sub-categories. Experiments conducted in Jinan and Qingdao, China, demonstrate the efficacy of the proposed method for refined multi-level UGS mapping.

### [194] [Impacts of Extreme Climate on NDVI in China—Response Patterns and Threshold Effects](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132180)
*Mengwei Li,Rong Li,Rui Zhu,Jianan Shan,Zh. Zhao,Fulong Chen,Zhenliang Yin*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 基于2001-2024年ERA5-Land气候数据和MODIS NDVI数据，采用Pearson相关、小波分析和XGBoost-SHAP模型，分析了中国NDVI对极端气候变化的响应。NDVI以0.021/10yr速率增长，R25（31.6%）和SDII（12.5%）是主要驱动因子，阈值分别为1.85天和4.35 mm/day。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究极端气候事件对植被动态的影响对于维持生态系统稳定性至关重要，因此需要量化中国NDVI对极端气候变化的响应机制。

Method: 使用ERA5-Land温度和降水数据及MOD13C2数据，结合Pearson相关分析、小波分析和XGBoost-SHAP模型进行分析。

Result: (1) NDVI以0.021/10yr速率增长，极端温度和降水指数在多数区域呈增加趋势；(2) NDVI与多数极端指数正相关，仅与FDO（霜冻日）和CDD（连续干日）显著负相关；(3) R25（31.6%）和SDII（12.5%）是全国NDVI变化的主要驱动因子，阈值分别为1.85天和4.35 mm/day。

Conclusion: 本研究为理解和应对植被对日益增加的气候极端事件的响应提供了科学依据。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。改进方向：(1) 可引入更高分辨率植被指数（如Landsat NDVI、Sentinel-2）以提升空间细节；(2) 可结合GPP/SIF等遥感参数验证植被动态的生理机制；(3) 可扩展至不同生态系统（如农田、森林、草原）进行分区建模；(4) 可融合多源遥感数据（如SMAP土壤湿度）增强对干旱胁迫的解释力；(5) XGBoost-SHAP模型可与其他集成学习方法（随机森林、LightGBM）进行对比验证鲁棒性。

Abstract (英文): Studying the impact of extreme climate events on vegetation dynamics is crucial for maintaining ecosystem stability. Based on ERA5-Land temperature and precipitation data, as well as MOD13C2 data, this study employs Pearson correlation analysis, wavelet analysis, and the XGBoost-SHAP model to analyze the response of the Normalized Difference Vegetation Index (NDVI) in China to extreme climate variations. The findings reveal the following. (1) NDVI increased steadily at a rate of 0.021/10 yr from 2001 to 2024. Extreme temperature and precipitation indices show an increasing trend in most regions. (2) NDVI was positively correlated with most extreme temperature and precipitation indices, and showed a significant negative correlation exclusively with Frost Days FDO (Frost Days) and CDD (Consecutive Dry Days). (3) R25 (Number of Heavy Precipitation Days) and SDII (Simple daily intensity index) are the primary drivers of nationwide NDVI changes, with contribution rates of 31.6% and 12.5%. Extreme climate indices can significantly affect vegetation growth when surpassing certain thresholds. For instance, the thresholds for R25 and SDII are 1.85 days and 4.35 mm/day. This study provides a scientific basis for understanding and managing vegetation responses to increasing climate extremes.

### [195] [RepLite-YOLO: A Parameter-Efficient Residual-Enhanced Detector for Ship Recognition in Remote Sensing Imagery](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132238)
*Ruijia Fu,Zuomin Wang,Zijun Lin,Ying Li,Bingxin Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 针对遥感舰船检测中背景噪声、尺度变化和硬件限制问题，提出基于YOLOv11n的轻量化检测框架RepLite-YOLO，通过ADown模块、C3k2_OREPA_RS模块、ELANFusion_Block和Detect_DWLite检测头，在Vessel和Ship Detection数据集上参数量减少57.4%、GFLOPs减少49.2%，mAP@50分别提升1.2和1.3个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有遥感舰船检测方法在复杂海面背景噪声、大范围目标尺度变化和边缘硬件限制下表现不佳，亟需一种兼顾检测精度与计算效率的轻量化检测框架。

Method: 1) 采用ADown模块（来自YOLOv9）的双分支下采样机制，保留船体边缘响应并抑制海面干扰；2) 设计C3k2_OREPA_RS模块，利用在线重参数化（OREPA）重构深层结构，不引入额外推理开销；3) 构建ELANFusion_Block，将深度可分离卷积（DSC）集成到ELAN范式中缓解多尺度聚合瓶颈；4) 设计Detect_DWLite检测头实现高度压缩的解耦预测。

Result: 相比YOLOv11n，参数量减少57.4%，GFLOPs减少49.2%；在Vessel数据集上mAP@50提升1.2个百分点，在Ship Detection数据集上mAP@50提升1.3个百分点，检测精度保持竞争力。

Conclusion: RepLite-YOLO在检测精度与计算效率之间取得了良好平衡，验证了所提轻量化设计的有效性，适用于资源受限场景下的遥感舰船检测任务。
