Abstract (英文): Changes in urban form strongly affect surface thermal conditions, yet long-term quantitative assessments of this relationship, particularly the role of ventilation resistance, remain limited. To address this gap, this study integrates XGBoost, SHapley Additive explanations (SHAP), and multi-scale geographically weighted regression (MGWR) to examine how six morphological, ecological, and human-activity factors influence land surface temperature (LST) in Kaifeng City. The results indicate three main findings. First, LST increased significantly from 1986 to 2024, while interannual variability declined, indicating a gradual reduction in regional thermal fluctuations. Second, NTL was consistently the dominant indicator across the five representative years, while BF and NTL together captured the effects of urban expansion and intensified human activity. Third, FAD coefficients were more spatially heterogeneous in urban fringe areas than in the urban core. In 2020, the dispersion of FAD coefficients in fringe areas was 2.74 times greater than that in the central area, indicating stronger spatial differentiation in ventilation-related morphological constraints during urban expansion. Although FAD made only a modest contribution to overall predictive accuracy, it provided supplementary diagnostic information not captured by conventional density indicators and showed nonlinear, directional, and spatially heterogeneous responses. Compared with previous studies that mainly examined short-term or single-dimensional relationships between urban morphology and LST, this study integrates building densification, ventilation-related morphological resistance, ecological conditions, and human activity intensity into a long-term LST-driver framework, providing evidence to support heat-risk management during urban regeneration and outward expansion.

### [224] [Lagged Response of Groundwater Storage to Extreme Precipitation Using Machine-Learning-Downscaled GRACE Data at the Watershed Scale](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132217)
*Xiaoling Zheng,Yilei Yu,Jiyi Jiang,Lihu Yang,Shiqin Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究利用LightGBM模型降尺度GRACE数据，生成了2002-2024年白洋淀流域1km分辨率的地下水储量异常数据集，分析了地下水对极端降水事件的响应，发现地下水储量呈现先快速下降后回升的趋势，极端降水对地下水补给存在约两个月的延迟响应，且月尺度有效降水比日尺度极端降水对地下水恢复影响更大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解地下水储量如何响应极端降水对于评估气候变率下含水层的恢复力至关重要，但现有研究缺乏高分辨率地下水储量数据和对极端降水事件响应的定量分析。

Method: 利用LightGBM模型将GRACE卫星观测的粗分辨率地下水储量异常数据降尺度至1km分辨率，生成2002-2024年白洋淀流域的GWSA数据集；通过与GLDAS和地下水位异常等独立水文数据集验证；采用复合分析方法对11次极端降水事件进行统计分析。

Result: 降尺度GWSA与独立数据集一致性良好；地下水储量呈现三个阶段：2014年前快速枯竭（-1.35 cm/yr）、2014-2019年缓慢下降（-1.04 cm/yr）、2020年后显著恢复（+3.45 cm/yr）；GWSA从西南向东北递增；极端降水后约两个月出现最强响应信号；月有效降水比短期日极端降水与GWSA恢复更相关，平原地区响应强于山区。

Conclusion: 极端降水提供间歇性补给脉冲，但地下水持续恢复依赖于累积气候输入和人类水管理的影响。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该研究的遥感核心是基于GRACE重力卫星数据的降尺度处理。对于其他遥感研究而言：1）可将LightGBM降尺度框架迁移至其他粗分辨率遥感产品（如SMAP土壤水分、MODIS ET等）的空间精细化；2）极端降水事件复合分析方法可应用于评估其他水文变量（如地表水储量、土壤湿度）对极端气候的响应；3）该研究的1km GWSA数据集可与Sentinel-1 InSAR地表形变、Landsat植被指数等多源遥感数据联合分析，深入理解地下水-地表水-植被的耦合机制。

Abstract (英文): Understanding how groundwater storage responds to extreme precipitation is essential for assessing aquifer resilience under climate variability. In this study, we developed a 1 km groundwater storage anomaly (GWSA) dataset for the Baiyangdian Watershed from 2002 to 2024 by downscaling GRACE observations with a Light Gradient Boosting Machine (LightGBM) model. The downscaled GWSA showed good consistency with independent hydrological datasets, including GLDAS and groundwater-level anomalies. Based on the downscaled product, we characterized long-term groundwater changes and quantified GWSA responses to extreme precipitation events (EPEs). Groundwater storage exhibited three distinct phases: rapid depletion before 2014 (−1.35 cm/yr), a slower decline during 2014–2019 (−1.04 cm/yr), and marked recovery after 2020 (+3.45 cm/yr). Spatially, GWSA generally increased from the southwest to the northeast of the watershed. Composite analysis of 11 EPEs revealed a delayed groundwater response, with the strongest signal occurring approximately two months after precipitation. Monthly effective precipitation was more closely associated with GWSA recovery than short-duration daily precipitation extremes, and the response was stronger in plains than in mountainous areas. These findings indicate that EPEs provide episodic recharge pulses, while sustained groundwater recovery depends on cumulative climatic inputs and human water-management influences.

### [225] [SAGE: Saliency and Geometry Enhanced Transferable Attacks for LiDAR Point Cloud Perception in Remote Sensing](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132209)
*Yuheng Wu,Shiwei Lin,Shibo Ping,Xingchao Zhai,Zhiyuan Fang,Meijuan Chen,Weiquan Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出SAGE框架，通过显著性图与几何约束增强LiDAR点云对抗样本的可迁移性，在保持几何质量的同时提升攻击成功率，用于评估遥感感知系统的迁移鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于迁移的点云对抗攻击方法生成的扰动区域对代理模型有区分性，但跨不同架构时稳定性不足，导致可迁移性有限且几何畸变明显。

Method: SAGE框架：1）将点坐标先验与源模型梯度信号融合生成显著性图，作为脆弱局部结构的可迁移指示器；2）通过显著性引导的扰动分配和显式几何约束，在增强可迁移性的同时保持点云几何质量。

Result: 在点云分类基准及KITTI、nuScenes上的LiDAR 3D目标检测任务中，SAGE在攻击成功率上持续优于现有方法，同时保持对抗点云的良好几何质量。

Conclusion: SAGE为评估基于LiDAR的遥感感知系统的迁移鲁棒性提供了一个有效且实用的框架。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。本文本身就是面向遥感感知（自动驾驶、LiDAR点云）的迁移攻击研究。改进方向：1）可引入多模态融合（如图像-点云联合）的显著性图生成策略，以进一步提升跨模态迁移性；2）可扩展到遥感中的其他3D任务（如语义分割、目标检测中的多类别场景）；3）可结合场景级几何先验（如道路结构、建筑物分布）优化几何约束，适应更复杂的遥感环境。

Abstract (英文): LiDAR point clouds are widely used in remote sensing perception scenarios, such as autonomous driving. However, LiDAR-based perception models remain vulnerable to adversarial perturbations, which may compromise the reliability of safety-critical 3D perception systems. Among different attack paradigms, transfer-based attacks are particularly practical because they generate adversarial examples on accessible surrogate models and apply the generated examples directly to unknown target models. Nevertheless, existing transferable attacks on point clouds often perturb regions that are discriminative for the surrogate model but insufficiently stable across different architectures, leading to limited transferability and noticeable geometric distortion. To address this problem, we propose SAGE, a Saliency And Geometry Enhanced transferable attack framework for LiDAR point cloud perception in remote sensing. Specifically, SAGE unifies point-coordinate priors with source-model gradient signals to generate a saliency map, which serves as a transferable indicator of vulnerable local structures. SAGE further leverages this map through saliency-guided perturbation allocation and explicit geometric constraints to enhance transferability while preserving point-cloud geometry. To demonstrate the effectiveness of SAGE, we evaluate SAGE on point-cloud classification benchmarks and further validate it on LiDAR-based 3D object detection using KITTI and nuScenes. Experimental results show that SAGE consistently outperforms existing transferable attack methods in attack success rate while preserving favorable geometric quality of adversarial point clouds. These findings demonstrate that SAGE offers an effective and practical framework for assessing the transfer robustness of LiDAR-based remote sensing perception systems.

### [226] [Finding the Features with LiDAR and SAR: Automated Detection of Archaeological Earthworks at Cahokia](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132229)
*Justin M. Vilbig,Vasit Sagan,Joseph A. Jilek,Cagri Gul*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种半自动化遥感流程，结合LiDAR（三种数据集，包括UAV和有人机）和SAR（PALSAR-3、Sentinel-1）数据，通过局部地形模型（LRM）、K-means聚类、轮廓提取和局部入射角（LIA）角度偏差映射，成功检测和勾勒了卡霍基亚土丘群（美国伊利诺伊州）的考古遗迹（土丘、取土坑、堤道）。结果表明LiDAR擅长高程定义特征，SAR的LIA擅长捕捉斜坡方向异常，两者互补。该方法可扩展、跨站点适用，且可使用开放获取数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂混合环境下的考古特征检测需要准确高效的方法来识别微弱的形态学信号，而传统方法在识别效率、主观性和可扩展性方面存在不足。

Method: (1) 使用三种LiDAR数据集（两种UAV-mounted传感器和一种有人机航空调查）生成数字地形模型并转换为局部地形模型（LRM）；(2) 应用K-means聚类对LRM进行特征类别分割，再利用OpenCV库进行轮廓边界提取以勾勒土丘和取土坑；(3) 处理PALSAR-3和Sentinel-1的SAR数据生成局部入射角（LIA）栅格，通过角度偏差映射识别与考古特征相关的坡度异常。

Result: 所有五个数据集的结果显示LiDAR和SAR具有互补优势：LiDAR在解析高程定义特征（如土丘足迹）方面表现优异，而LIA则能捕捉方向性坡度行为，突出显示土丘边缘、取土坑边缘和线性特征（如堤道）。LiDAR采集频率的对比分析表明，传感器平台选择比功率密度权衡对考古特征恢复的影响更大。

Conclusion: 尽管仍需人工审查以过滤现代干扰和自然假阳性，但该集成工作流显著加速了勘探过程并减少了解释主观性。方法具有可扩展性、站点不变性，且可使用开放获取数据，适用于全球范围内的考古景观。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。改进方案：(1) 引入多尺度形态学分割或深度学习语义分割（如U-Net、Mask R-CNN）替代K-means聚类，提升复杂地物识别精度；(2) 结合多时相InSAR相干性分析，检测微小的地表形变或隐藏遗迹；(3) 引入多光谱LiDAR或高光谱数据，增加对植被覆盖下遗迹的探测能力；(4) 将LIA角度偏差映射与光学影像（如WorldView、Planet）的纹理特征融合，构建多模态检测框架，减少人工审查负担。

Abstract (英文): Archaeological feature detection at complex, mixed-environment sites requires accurate, efficient methods for identifying subtle morphological signatures. This study presents a semi-automated remote sensing pipeline for the detection and delineation of archaeological earthworks at Cahokia Mounds (Illinois, USA), a major Mississippian urban center and UNESCO World Heritage Site. Three LiDAR datasets, two collected via UAV-mounted sensors and one from a piloted aircraft survey, were processed into Digital Terrain Models and transformed into Local Relief Models (LRM). K-means clustering was applied to segment the LRMs into feature classes, followed by contour bounding using the OpenCV library to outline mounds and borrow pits. Additionally, SAR-derived Local Incidence Angle (LIA) rasters from PALSAR-3 and Sentinel-1 were processed through angular deviation mapping to identify slope anomalies associated with archaeological features. Results across all five datasets demonstrate the complementary strengths of LiDAR and SAR: LiDAR excels at resolving elevation-defined features such as mound footprints, while LIA captures directional slope behavior that highlights mound edges, borrow pit rims, and linear features such as causeways. Comparative analysis of LiDAR acquisition frequencies reveals minimal differences in archaeological feature recovery between pulse settings, suggesting that sensor platform choice matters more than power-density tradeoffs for this application. Despite the need for human review to filter modern disturbances and natural false positives, the integrated workflow meaningfully accelerates prospection and reduces interpretive subjectivity. The methods are scalable, site-invariant, and work with open-access data, making them applicable to archaeological landscapes worldwide.

Abstract (英文): Crop targets in UAV aerial images are typically characterized by small scale, dense distribution, severe mutual occlusion, and complex backgrounds, which often lead to low detection accuracy and large counting errors for existing deep learning models. To address these issues, this study proposes an improved YOLOv12-based crop detection and counting model, named YOLO-DC. By introducing an attention mechanism (LGCB-AM) and a multi-scale detection head (MS-DH), the proposed model effectively enhances local texture extraction, global modeling, foreground–background contrast, and boundary perception for dense small objects. Subsequently, a series of comparative experiments, ablation studies, and transfer experiments were conducted on the wheat and rice datasets. The results show that YOLO-DC achieves a favorable balance among detection accuracy, counting error, and model efficiency and overall outperforms the other comparison models. Ablation studies further verify the effectiveness of the proposed design, showing that LGCB-AM is the key contributor to the performance improvement, while the boundary branch and repulsion branch play critical roles in dense-target discrimination. In addition, an appropriate module insertion strategy can effectively balance high-level semantic enhancement and feature fusion stability. Transfer experiments demonstrate that pretraining on the wheat dataset and fine-tuning on the rice dataset significantly outperform training from scratch, indicating strong cross-crop transfer potential. Overall, the proposed YOLO-DC provides an effective solution for high-precision crop detection and counting in agricultural scenarios.

### [229] [A Hybrid VRT-S-BR Method for Composite Electromagnetic Scattering from Targets Above Vegetated Rough Surfaces](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132183)
*Yu-Feng Zou,Shui‐Rong Chai,Xiao-Jie Qu,Jiajun Li,Kun Chao,Lixin Guo,Wei Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种混合矢量辐射传输-弹跳射线法（VRT-S-BR），用于预测植被覆盖粗糙表面上目标的复合电磁散射。该方法将植被层建模为分层随机介质，通过VRT-S模型生成植被诱导的复反射系数离线数据库，替代传统菲涅尔反射项，并引入依赖于面元的相位补偿方案以描述传播路径变化。在天然草地场测量数据上验证，HH和VV极化的均方根误差分别为1.82 dB和3.10 dB。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有混合模型在处理植被覆盖粗糙表面与目标的复合电磁散射时，通常采用经验性随机相位扰动来近似植被效应，缺乏物理机制支撑，导致精度受限。亟需一种能准确描述植被诱导的衰减和相干散射效应的物理驱动方法。

Method: 将植被层建模为分层随机介质，通过VRT-S模型预先计算不同入射角下的植被复反射系数，建立离线数据库；在BR射线追踪过程中，用该系数逐次替代传统菲涅尔反射项；引入依赖于面元的相位补偿方案替代经验随机相位扰动，描述不同射线穿过植被冠层的传播路径变化。

Result: 在天然草地的场测量数据上验证，HH和VV极化的均方根误差分别为1.82 dB和3.10 dB。数值实验表明，该方法能够有效表征不同植被覆盖百分比、植被高度、地形背景及双站观测几何下的目标-植被耦合散射特性。

Conclusion: 提出的VRT-S-BR方法为植被覆盖环境下目标电磁散射预测提供了一种物理驱动的精确建模方案，相比传统经验方法具有更高的精度和物理可解释性，可广泛应用于遥感、雷达探测等领域。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：（1）将VRT-S-BR方法扩展至多频段遥感场景，建立频段依赖的植被复反射系数数据库，提升多光谱/雷达遥感数据融合的物理一致性；（2）针对不同植被类型（森林、农田、灌木等）建立分类别的高精度VRT-S模型参数库，提升通用性和跨区域迁移能力；（3）与全极化SAR成像模拟结合，利用面元相位补偿机制改进极化散射矩阵的建模精度，提升地物分类和目标识别性能；（4）引入动态植被生长模型参数，实现时序遥感场景下植被-目标耦合散射特性的动态演化模拟。

Abstract (英文): This paper proposes a hybrid Vector Radiative Transfer Shooting (VRT-S)-Bouncing Ray (BR) method, referred to as the VRT-S-BR method, for predicting composite electromagnetic scattering from targets above vegetation-covered rough surfaces. In this proposed framework, the vegetation layer is modeled as a stratified random medium and incorporated into the BR solver through VRT-S-derived amplitude modulation and deterministic phase compensation. Specifically, an offline database of vegetation-induced complex reflection coefficients is first generated using the VRT-S model over a set of incidence angles. During the BR ray-tracing process, these coefficients are used to replace the conventional Fresnel reflection terms on a per-interaction basis, thereby accounting for vegetation-induced attenuation and coherent scattering effects. In addition, a facet-dependent phase compensation scheme is introduced to describe propagation-path variations of individual rays through the vegetation canopy, avoiding the empirical random phase perturbation used in previous hybrid models. The proposed method is validated against field-measured backscattering data over natural grassland, achieving root mean square height (RMSE) values of 1.82 dB and 3.10 dB for horizontal-horizontal (HH) and vertical-vertical (VV) polarizations, respectively. Numerical results further demonstrate the capability of the method to characterize target–vegetation coupled scattering under different percentages of vegetation cover, vegetation heights, terrain backgrounds, and bistatic observation geometries.

### [230] [Locally Adaptive Mamba and Multi-Scale Feature Enhancement for Optical Remote Sensing Image Change Detection](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132226)
*Mingxuan Ding,Qirong Zhou,Qiaolin Ye,Le Sun*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出LADENet，一种融合CNN、Transformer和Mamba范式的遥感变化检测网络，通过局部自适应Mamba模块、多尺度特征增强和双时相差异增强，在四个公开数据集上取得了领先性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有遥感变化检测方法存在三大问题：1）局部细节与全局特征的协同建模困难；2）双时相差表示单一；3）跨尺度特征交流不足，限制了模型在复杂环境下的精度和鲁棒性。

Method: 1) 权重共享的多级Transformer编码器+序列缩减机制生成多尺度全局特征；2) 双时空自适应局部特征标记模块，基于状态空间扫描(SSS)实现高显著变化区域定位；3) 双分支差异增强模块（注意力增强差分分支+多尺度卷积拼接分支）；4) 全局跨尺度空间特征融合解码器（空间注意力+二维选择性扫描）。

Result: LEVIR-CD: F1=91.06%, IoU=85.28%; WHU-CD: F1=90.51%, IoU=82.45%; CLCD-CD: F1=82.15%, IoU=72.83%; GVLM-CD: F1=89.12%, IoU=77.78%。在四个基准上均超越现有方法。

Conclusion: LADENet通过CNN-Transformer-Mamba三重范式融合，在双时相遥感变化检测中实现了高精度、清晰的边界刻画和良好的泛化性能。

Abstract (英文): Within the domain of Earth observation, tracking terrestrial transitions via high-resolution optical data plays a fundamental role. Nevertheless, current methods face critical challenges, including the difficulty in collaborative modeling of local details and global features and the singularity of bi-temporal difference representation, along with insufficient cross-scale feature communication, thereby constraining both the precision and resilience of models when applied to complicated environments. To solve these problems, we propose LADENet (Locally Adaptive Mamba and Multi-scale Feature Enhancement Network), an innovative framework that synergizes CNN, Transformer, and Mamba paradigms. By leveraging customized local contextual refinement alongside sophisticated hierarchical fusion, this integration delivers highly precise and resilient detection performance. LADENet adopts a weight-sharing multi-level Transformer encoder combined with a sequence reduction mechanism to generate multi-scale global features, achieving precise alignment of bi-temporal features and global context modeling while reducing computational complexity. To realize accurate localization and local enhancement of changed regions, we design a dual spatiotemporal adaptive local feature marking module based on State-Space Scanning (SSS). This module screens high-saliency changed regions through an adaptive scanning strategy, realizes pixel-aligned spatiotemporal feature fusion via cross-temporal state-space scanning, and introduces a sliding window boundary calibration mechanism to alleviate boundary information loss caused by window segmentation. To strengthen the feature representation of changed regions, a dual-branch difference enhancement module is constructed, which collaboratively captures global change trends and fine-grained local features through an attention-enhanced difference branch and a multi-scale convolution concatenation branch, effectively suppressing background interference. To address the semantic gap between cross-scale features, a global cross-scale spatial feature fusion decoder is proposed, which balances local detail preservation and global context perception through the synergy of spatial attention and two-dimensional selective scanning, completing refined multi-scale feature fusion and spatial resolution recovery. To rigorously validate the proposed LADENet, comprehensive experiments were conducted across four widely adopted bi-temporal benchmarks: LEVIR-CD, WHU-CD, CLCD-CD, and GVLM-CD. The presented architecture establishes substantial superiority over existing cutting-edge methodologies across primary evaluation criteria. Specifically, it yields an F1-measure of 91.06% alongside an IoU of 85.28% in the LEVIR-CD tests, while registering 90.51% (F1) and 82.45% (IoU) for WHU-CD. Similarly, robust outcomes are delivered on CLCD-CD (82.15% F1, 72.83% IoU) as well as GVLM-CD (89.12% F1, 77.78% IoU). These results demonstrate that LADENet possesses excellent detection accuracy, boundary delineation capability and generalization performance in diverse and intricate bi-temporal observation environments.

### [231] [Efficient Sea Clutter Suppression Algorithm Based on BCD-Accelerated Dictionary Learning and TQWT Denoising](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132201)
*Jin Wang,Yubing Han,Yancun Lyu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出一种将BCD加速字典学习与TQWT去噪级联的海杂波抑制方法，通过BCD替代全局SVD降低计算复杂度，结合自适应软阈值算子和批量自适应OMP实现高效重构与杂波对消，最后利用TQWT滤除残余非平稳杂波。在IPIX等实测数据上，平均SCNR提升17.48 dB，执行时间仅7.99秒，在抑制性能与计算效率间取得优异平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂海况下弱雷达目标检测面临非平稳海杂波和海尖峰的挑战，传统字典学习算法计算复杂度高，难以在性能与效率间取得平衡。

Method: 1) BCD加速字典学习：用分析优化替代全局SVD，结合自适应软阈值算子实现字典原子和稀疏系数的低复杂度联合优化；2) 批量自适应OMP：采用Gram矩阵预计算和双停止机制实现高效重构与杂波初步对消；3) TQWT去噪：利用窄带特征表示和平移不变性滤除残余非平稳杂波和噪声。

Result: 在IPIX数据库和《雷达学报》实测数据集上，相比传统K-SVD算法，平均SCNR提升17.48 dB，总执行时间仅7.99秒。

Conclusion: 所提方法在抑制性能与计算效率间实现了高度有利的折中，显著优于传统K-SVD算法。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该方法的低复杂度字典学习框架可直接迁移至SAR图像相干斑抑制、遥感图像去噪等任务。具体改进方案：1) BCD加速策略可替换遥感图像稀疏表示中的K-SVD步骤，大幅降低训练时间；2) 批量自适应OMP可用于高光谱图像解混中的端元提取；3) TQWT的小波变换特性可用于遥感影像中地物边缘保持与纹理增强，尤其适用于高分辨率遥感图像的多尺度细节提取。

Abstract (英文): Detecting weak radar targets in complex sea conditions is inherently challenging due to non-stationary sea clutter and sea spikes. Furthermore, traditional dictionary learning algorithms for clutter suppression suffer from high computational complexity. To address these issues, this paper proposes an efficient sea clutter suppression method cascading Block Coordinate Descent (BCD)-accelerated dictionary learning with Tunable Q-factor Wavelet Transform (TQWT) denoising. During dictionary learning, a BCD strategy replaces global Singular Value Decomposition (SVD) with analytical optimization. Combined with an adaptive soft-thresholding operator, this enables low-complexity joint optimization of dictionary atoms and sparse coefficients, drastically reducing training time. Subsequently, a batch-adaptive Orthogonal Matching Pursuit (OMP) algorithm featuring Gram matrix precomputation and a dual-stop mechanism achieves efficient reconstruction and preliminary cancellation of clutter components. Finally, TQWT is applied to filter out residual non-stationary clutter and noise by leveraging its narrowband feature representation and shift invariance. Experiments on measured radar data from the IPIX database and datasets published by the Journal of Radars demonstrate that the proposed method significantly outperforms traditional K-SVD-based algorithms. Specifically, it improves the average signal-to-clutter-plus-noise ratio (SCNR) by 17.48 dB and requires a total execution time of only 7.99 s, achieving a highly favorable trade-off between suppression performance and computational efficiency.

### [232] [MCPF-Net: Multi-Stage LiDAR-Image Collaborative Perception Fusion Network for Point Cloud Semantic Segmentation of Urban Scenes](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132218)
*Huchen Li,Wubiao Huang,Xiangda Lei,Bin Liu,Haibing Liu,Shihan Chen,Fei Deng*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出一种多阶段LiDAR-图像协同感知融合网络（MCPFNet），用于城市场景点云语义分割，包含中层融合（高程引导几何感知模块+语义感知交叉注意力模块）和晚期融合（双向自适应融合模块），在三个多模态数据集上超越现有方法，分别达到74.51%、95.15%和62.76%的mIoU。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有融合方法面临跨模态感知能力有限和信息互补性不足的问题，难以充分利用LiDAR精确的3D结构几何信息与光学图像丰富的语义纹理信息。

Method: MCPFNet包含三个关键模块：1) 中层融合阶段的高程引导几何感知融合模块，实现高程引导的几何特征提取；2) 中层融合阶段的语义感知交叉注意力融合模块，实现双向特征注入；3) 晚期融合阶段的双向自适应融合模块，通过门控加权和双向交叉注意力机制进一步优化语义表示。

Result: 在ISPRS Vaihingen、N3C-California和UAVScenes三个不同分辨率的多模态数据集上分别达到74.51%、95.15%和62.76%的mIoU，优于现有融合方法。

Conclusion: 多阶段融合和双向交互策略在多样且复杂的城市场景分割任务中比现有方法更可靠、更准确。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。改进方案：1) 可引入多尺度高程引导机制，结合DEM/DSM数据进一步提升几何感知能力；2) 可扩展为多模态遥感数据融合框架（如SAR+光学+LiDAR），用于更丰富的遥感场景解译；3) 双向自适应融合模块可迁移至遥感图像与点云联合的地物分类任务中；4) 可引入时序信息或跨模态对比学习策略，进一步提升遥感场景下的分割鲁棒性。

Abstract (英文): Multimodal fusion unlocks the potential of point cloud semantic segmentation, thereby driving advancements in surface observation and visual perception tasks. Although light detection and ranging (LiDAR) systems capture precise 3D structural geometry and optical images provide rich semantic and textural information, existing fusion methods struggle with limited cross-modal perception and insufficient information complementarity. To address these limitations, we propose a multi-stage LiDAR-image collaborative perception fusion network (MCPFNet) for point cloud semantic segmentation of urban scenes. At the middle fusion stage, the network incorporates an elevation-guided geometric-aware fusion module and a semantic-aware cross-attention fusion module to enable bidirectional feature injection between LiDAR and image modalities. In the late fusion stage, a bidirectional adaptive fusion module further refines semantic representations through gated weighting and bidirectional cross-attention mechanisms. Extensive experiments on three multimodal datasets with different resolutions, i.e., ISPRS Vaihingen, N3C-California, and UAVScenes, demonstrate that MCPFNet outperforms existing fusion methods, achieving mIoUs of 74.51%, 95.15%, and 62.76%, respectively. Hence, our multi-stage fusion and bidirectional interaction strategy is more reliable and accurate than existing methods in performing segmentation across diverse and complex urban scenes.

### [233] [Total Ozone Column Changes over Northeast China: Trends and Variability Analysis](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132189)
*Yu Shi,O. Evtushevsky,Gennadi Milinevsky*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 基于MSR-2和ERA5数据集，分析2015-2024年中国东北地区（40-53°N, 115-135°E）月平均总臭氧柱（TOC）的变化，结合龙凤山站地面观测数据，研究了TOC的季节性特征及其与臭氧浓度和气温的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究中国东北地区TOC的区域季节性格局及其与平流层和对流层臭氧浓度、气温的定量关系，填补该区域在臭氧气候学方面的研究空白。

Method: 利用MSR-2再分析和ERA5数据集，结合WMO/GAW龙凤山站地面观测数据，采用统计方法分析2015-2024年TOC的时空变化、季节周期、线性趋势及其与臭氧浓度和气温的相关性。

Result: TOC无显著线性趋势；区域年均TOC高于纬向均值25 DU（7.4%）；年最大值出现在2月、最小值在8月，分别比北半球中纬度早1和2个月；TOC从东北部（~415 DU）向西南部（~330 DU）气候性递减；TOC与地面臭氧浓度呈强正相关（|r|≈0.8-0.9），与地面气温呈强负相关；龙凤山站数据与MSR-2月均差异在±15 DU（±4.2%）内。

Conclusion: 龙凤山站数据可作为区域TOC变率的可靠代理，Brewer-Dobson环流、准定常波和中国东北冷涡在解释TOC格局和定量关联中起重要作用，研究成果可用于东亚臭氧观测和平流层-对流层耦合分析。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该研究已充分融合了多源遥感再分析数据（MSR-2、ERA5）与地面观测数据，属于遥感与大气科学的交叉应用。改进方向：（1）引入更高空间分辨率的卫星传感器数据（如TROPOMI、OMPS）以精细化TOC空间分布格局；（2）结合机器学习方法（如随机森林、LSTM）对TOC与气象要素的非线性关系进行建模预测；（3）将分析扩展至整个东亚区域，结合FY-4等国产卫星资料进行多源数据同化验证；（4）将TOC变化与植被指数（NDVI）等遥感产品关联，探究臭氧变化对地表生态的潜在影响。

Abstract (英文): Based on the Multi-Sensor Reanalysis Version 2 (MSR-2) and ERA5 datasets, variations in monthly mean total ozone column (TOC) over Northeast China (40–53°N, 115–135°E) from 2015 to 2024 are analyzed. Local ground-based observations at the regional WMO/GAW Longfengshan Station are also used. The aim is to investigate regional seasonality in TOC pattern and the relationship between TOC and ozone concentration and air temperature in the stratosphere and at the surface. No statistically significant linear trend was found for TOC; however, the annual mean TOC in the study region exceeds the zonal mean TOC by 25 DU (7.4%), and the annual maximum in February and minimum in August are observed one and two months earlier, respectively, than in the Northern Hemisphere mid-latitudes. A climatological decrease in TOC from the northeastern (~415 DU) to southwestern (~330 DU) parts of Northeast China was found. We also found a strong correlation, approaching |r| = 0.8–0.9, between TOC and ozone concentration (positive) and temperature (negative) at the surface. The time series from Longfengshan Station for 2015–2022 closely match the MSR-2 data averaged over Northeast China: the monthly mean difference varies within ±15 DU (±4.2%), validating the reliability of the station data as a representative proxy for regional TOC variability. The role of the Brewer–Dobson circulation, quasi-stationary waves, and the Northeast China cold vortex in the detected patterns and quantitative associations of TOC is discussed. The findings of this work can be applied to analyze the ozone observations, TOC variability, and stratosphere–troposphere coupling in East Asia.

### [234] [Impervious Surface Area Changes and Urban Expansion in China’s Three Major Urban Agglomerations over the Past 40 Years](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132236)
*Fei Wang,Yi Yang,Lei Yu,Fengyun Sang,Yaning Chen,Siquan Yang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文分析了1985-2024年中国三大城市群（珠三角、长三角、京津冀）的不透水面面积（ISA）时空动态，并利用位置中心性指数（LCI）研究了五个超大城市的扩张结构。结果显示，三大城市群的ISA从22,544.10 km²扩张至69,348.59 km²，但扩张速率和强度呈明显下降趋势；各城市群的峰值扩张阶段存在显著差异；邻接扩张已成为大多数超大城市的主导增长模式（超过50%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分析中国三大城市群的不透水面面积及代表性城市的扩张模式，对于制定因地制宜的城市规划政策、增强城市发展韧性具有重要意义。

Method: 采用不透水面扩张指标揭示ISA的时空动态，并应用位置中心性指数（LCI）探究五个超大城市的扩张结构和模式。

Result: 1985-2024年三大城市群ISA从22,544.10 km²扩张至69,348.59 km²；扩张速率和强度呈明显减速趋势；各城市群峰值扩张阶段存在显著区域差异；LCI分析显示邻接扩张已成为多数超大城市的主导增长模式（>50%）。

Conclusion: 这些发现增强了对城市群ISA演化轨迹和超大城市扩张模式的理解，为可持续城市规划和城市韧性提供了科学依据。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。改进方案：（1）可引入多源遥感数据（如Sentinel-1 SAR + Sentinel-2光学数据）进行不透水面提取，提高时序一致性；（2）可结合夜间灯光遥感（如NPP-VIIRS）验证城市扩张边界；（3）可引入高时间分辨率遥感数据（如MODIS/Landsat融合）实现更精细的逐月/逐年扩张动态监测；（4）可利用深度学习遥感分类方法（如U-Net、DeepLabV3+）提升不透水面提取精度，减少混合像元影响。

Abstract (英文): Analyzing the impervious surface area (ISA) of China’s three major urban agglomerations and expansion pattern of representative cities is of great significance for formulating context-specific urban planning policies and enhancing the resilience of urban development. This research employs impervious surface expansion indicators to reveal the spatiotemporal dynamics of impervious surface area, and further applies the location centrality index (LCI) to investigate the expansion structures and patterns of five megacities. The results indicate that the ISA of China’s three major urban agglomerations expanded from 22,544.10 km2 to 69,348.59 km2 from 1985 to 2024; both the expansion rate and intensity have exhibited a distinct decelerating trend. However, significant regional variation exists in the peak expansion phases: the Guangdong–Hong Kong–Macao Greater Bay Area Urban Agglomeration (GBA) peaked during the Initial Exploratory Phase (1985–1995), whereas the Yangtze River Delta Urban Agglomeration (YRD) and Beijing–Tianjin–Hebei Urban Agglomeration (BTH) reached their peaks during the High-speed Development Phase (2005–2015). At the urban scale, LCI-based analysis of urban expansion across five megacities reveals that adjacency expansion type has become the predominant form of growth, exceeding 50% in most cities. These findings enhance our understanding of evolutionary trajectories of ISA within urban agglomerations and the expansion patterns of five megacities, providing a scientific basis for sustainable urban planning and urban resilience.

### [235] [MSIA-YOLO: A Multi-Scale Semantic Interaction and Alignment Network for Small Object Detection in Low-Altitude UAV Remote Sensing Images](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132210)
*Wen Zhang,Xiaorong Xue,Bingyan Lu,Yishuo Tian,Jingtong Yang,Xin Zhao,W X Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: MSIA-YOLO是一种基于YOLOv11的小目标检测器，通过多尺度语义交互与对齐机制（包括RFAConv、CHSP-P2检测框架和DTIA-Head），分别在特征建模、高分辨率语义补偿和任务协同对齐三个层面优化，在VisDrone、TinyPerson和RSOD数据集上mAP50分别提升7.7%、10.3%和1.0%，有效解决了小目标检测中细粒度特征不足、背景噪声放大和检测头任务不对齐等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小目标检测受限于缺乏判别性细粒度特征；引入高分辨率检测尺度虽能提升性能但会放大背景噪声；传统检测头的独立解耦设计无法有效解决小目标的漏检和误检问题。

Method: 1）在骨干网络中集成感受野注意力卷积（RFAConv），通过感受野感知注意力增强边缘和纹理等关键局部细节；2）构建CHSP-P2小目标检测框架，增加P2分支并引入尺度序列融合机制，通过跨尺度混合输入实现高分辨率语义补偿；3）设计DTIA-Head（动态任务交互与对齐头），通过动态任务交互和空间对齐促进分类与定位的联合优化。

Result: 在VisDrone、TinyPerson和RSOD数据集上，相比YOLOv11n基线，MSIA-YOLO的mAP50分别提升7.7%、10.3%和1.0%，且优于多个先进检测器。

Conclusion: MSIA-YOLO在小目标、密集目标和复杂场景目标检测中展现出有效的性能和泛化能力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：100%。该论文已在RSOD遥感数据集上验证有效性，以下为改进方案：1）针对遥感图像特有的旋转目标问题，可在DTIA-Head中引入角度回归分支，扩展为旋转框检测；2）CHSP-P2的P2分支可结合遥感影像的多光谱/高光谱通道信息，利用通道注意力机制实现光谱-空间联合语义补偿；3）RFAConv的感受野设计可针对遥感图像中不同地物尺度差异大的特点，采用自适应感受野缩放策略；4）可进一步引入遥感场景下的数据增强策略（如马赛克、随机翻转结合地理先验）以提升泛化性。

Abstract (英文): Small object detection is fundamentally constrained by the lack of discriminative fine-grained features. Although introducing higher resolution detection scales can improve performance, it also amplifies background noise. In addition, the independently decoupled design of conventional detection heads is insufficient to address the persistent challenges of missed detections and false positives for small objects. To this end, we propose MSIA-YOLO, a YOLOv11-based detector with multi-scale semantic interaction and alignment, optimized from three complementary perspectives: feature modeling, high resolution semantic compensation, and task coordinated alignment. First, Receptive Field Attention Convolution (RFAConv) is integrated into the backbone to enhance critical local details, such as edge and texture cues, via receptive field aware attention. Second, to alleviate fine detail attenuation caused by repeated downsampling, we construct a CHSP-P2 small object detection framework with an additional P2 branch. A scale sequence fusion mechanism is further introduced to perform high resolution semantic compensation through cross scale hybrid inputs. Finally, we design a DTIA-Head (Dynamic Task Interaction and Alignment Head), which promotes joint optimization of classification and localization through dynamic task interaction and spatial alignment. Extensive experiments on the public datasets VisDrone, TinyPerson, and RSOD show that, compared with the YOLOv11n baseline, MSIA-YOLO improves mAP50 by 7.7%, 10.3%, and 1.0%, respectively, while also outperforming several advanced detectors. These results demonstrate the effectiveness and generalization capability of the proposed method in small object, dense object, and complex scene object detection scenarios.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文评估了BepiColombo水星探测任务中MORE无线电科学实验的预期性能，通过数值模拟分析了改进的Ka波段跟踪系统在确定水星重力场、Love数k2和自转状态方面的不确定性降低效果，并首次在协方差分析中引入动力学模型误差。

Abstract (英文): The BepiColombo spacecraft, designed by ESA and JAXA, is currently in its cruise phase toward Mercury. Among the scientific investigations is the Mercury Orbiter Radio-science Experiment (MORE), which will exploit a multi-frequency microwave tracking system with an advanced Ka-band transponder to achieve its objectives pertaining to Mercury’s geodesy and fundamental physics. Leveraging precise measurements from this state-of-the-art radio tracking system, MORE is expected to provide new insights into Mercury’s interior, refining and expanding upon the findings of the MESSENGER mission. This work evaluates the performance of MORE’s gravity and rotation experiment, specifically assessing how BepiColombo’s improved radio tracking data can reduce uncertainties in the determination of Mercury’s gravity field, Love number k2, and rotational state. Differently from previous covariance analyses, this work includes errors in the dynamical model to assess the experiment’s performance under controlled mismodeling conditions. We present the results of a numerical simulation covering BepiColombo’s extended two-year orbital phase, with scientific operations set to begin in 2027.

### [237] [Realistic Error Budget and Cross-Validation of Sentinel-1 3D Displacement for the 2025 Dingri Earthquake](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132252)
*Zhangdi Xie*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究对2025年定日地震（Mw 7.1）的双轨InSAR三维形变场进行了系统的不确定性量化。利用Sentinel-1升降轨数据通过最小二乘反演构建三维同震位移场，发现该地震产生南北走向正断层破裂，垂直分量最大沉降-403.3 mm、最大抬升+621.1 mm，东西分量最大西向位移-592.3 mm、东向位移+332.1 mm。不确定性分析表明，形式误差传播给出的1σ不确定性仅为1.09 mm（垂直）和1.38 mm（东西），而基于蒙特卡洛模拟的实际误差约为13.8 mm（垂直）和17.2 mm（东西），系统误差贡献远超随机噪声。交叉验证的相关系数R在升轨LOS为0.88，降轨为0.62；三维分量中垂直为0.88，东西仅为0.59。研究证明形式误差传播严重低估了双轨InSAR反演的实际不确定性，系统误差来源远大于随机噪声。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双轨InSAR三维形变场反演中，形式误差传播方法常被用于不确定性评估，但其是否反映真实误差水平尚不明确。本研究旨在系统量化双轨InSAR三维形变场的实际不确定性，揭示形式误差与实际精度之间的差异，并识别主要误差来源。

Method: 利用Sentinel-1升降轨SAR数据，采用最小二乘反演构建2025年定日地震的三维同震位移场；通过形式误差传播计算理论1σ不确定性；采用蒙特卡洛模拟进行实际误差预算分析；并与独立Sentinel-1处理链进行交叉验证（计算LOS和三维分量的相关系数R）。

Result: 地震产生南北走向正断层破裂；垂直分量最大沉降-403.3 mm、最大抬升+621.1 mm；东西分量最大西向-592.3 mm、东向+332.1 mm。形式误差1σ：垂直1.09 mm、东西1.38 mm；蒙特卡洛实际误差：垂直~13.8 mm、东西~17.2 mm，系统误差主导。交叉验证R：升轨LOS=0.88，降轨LOS=0.62；垂直分量R=0.88，东西分量R=0.59。

Conclusion: 形式误差传播严重低估了双轨InSAR三维形变反演的实际不确定性；系统误差（如处理策略和观测几何）贡献远超随机噪声；东西分量对处理策略和观测几何更为敏感，不确定性更大。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：（1）引入系统误差建模方法（如协方差矩阵参数化或方差分量估计）替代传统形式误差传播，以更准确地量化InSAR反演不确定性；（2）将蒙特卡洛模拟作为InSAR三维形变反演的标配不确定性评估流程；（3）针对东西分量敏感性高的问题，可引入多轨道数据（如ALOS-2、高分三号）或联合GPS/北斗数据以增强观测几何约束，降低系统误差影响；（4）可尝试基于贝叶斯反演框架，将先验误差信息融入三维形变解算，提高估计可靠性。

Abstract (英文): This study presents a systematic uncertainty quantification of the two-track InSAR three-dimensional (3D) deformation field of the 2025 Dingri earthquake (Mw 7.1). Using Sentinel-1 ascending and descending track data, a 3D coseismic displacement field was constructed via least-squares inversion. The results revealed that the earthquake produced a north–south-striking normal fault rupture, with the vertical component reaching a maximum subsidence of −403.3 mm and a maximum uplift of +621.1 mm, and the east–west component reaching a maximum westward displacement of −592.3 mm and an eastward displacement of +332.1 mm. Uncertainty analysis reveals a divergence between formal errors and actual accuracy: formal error propagation yields 1σ uncertainties of 1.09 mm and 1.38 mm for the vertical and east–west components, respectively; a realistic error budget based on Monte Carlo simulations indicates that the actual errors are approximately 13.8 mm for the vertical component and 17.2 mm for the east–west component, with systematic error contributions far exceeding random noise. Cross-validation against an independent Sentinel-1 processing chain supports the above error assessment: the correlation coefficient R for ascending track line-of-sight (LOS) displacement is 0.88, whereas it is 0.62 for the descending track; for the three-dimensional components, R reaches 0.88 for the vertical component and 0.59 for the east–west component, with discrepancies arising primarily from the greater sensitivity of the east–west component to processing strategies and observation geometry. This study demonstrates that formal error propagation underestimates the actual uncertainty of two-track InSAR inversion and that systematic error sources contribute far more than random noise does.

</details>


### [238] [Physically Consistent SAR Image Generation for Unseen Aspect Angles via Attributed Scattering Center Evolution](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132247)
*Zihao Jiang,Chao Liu,Zhangzeyu Xing,Yamei Wang,Shuwen Xiao*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 针对SAR目标图像在未见方位角下的数据稀疏问题，本文提出了一种物理一致性框架，利用ASC启发的稀疏散射结构先验引导生成器合成结构合理的散射布局，并引入双一致性方案分别约束目标区域散射一致性和背景区域统计一致性，在未见角度插值和留出协议下显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SAR目标图像对方位角高度敏感，实际数据采集通常只能获得有限视角下的稀疏观测，导致在未见方位角下数据严重匮乏。现有方法要么仅关注分布匹配而未充分挖掘散射结构线索，要么强调角度条件化但未能联合保持物理合理的散射响应变化和真实的背景斑纹统计特性。

Method: 提出物理一致性SAR图像生成框架：(1) ASC启发的稀疏散射结构先验，近似SAR图像平面中的主要散射响应，作为可微分的角度感知结构代理引导生成器；(2) 双一致性方案，分别约束目标区域散射一致性和背景区域统计一致性，提升生成结果的物理真实性。

Result: 在严格的未见角度插值和留出协议下，该方法在图像保真度、目标区域散射一致性、背景统计一致性和角度条件一致性方面 consistently 优于代表性基线方法。

Conclusion: 所提ASC启发的稀疏散射结构先验在物理一致的SAR视角补全中起关键作用，验证了将散射物理先验引入生成模型的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该工作本身就是遥感SAR图像生成的核心问题。改进方向：(1) 将ASC稀疏先验扩展到极化SAR(PolSAR)或干涉SAR(InSAR)的多通道散射特征建模；(2) 引入物理信息神经网络(PINN)替代CNN生成器，更严格地满足电磁散射方程约束；(3) 结合地基SAR或GEO SAR的长时间序列观测，将方位角先验扩展为时空联合先验；(4) 将双一致性损失推广为自监督对比学习范式，减少对配对数据的依赖。

Abstract (英文): Synthetic aperture radar (SAR) target images are highly sensitive to aspect angle, while practical data acquisition usually provides only sparse observations over limited viewpoints. This leads to severe data scarcity at unseen aspect angles and makes cross-angle generation prone to scattering-structure distortion and background statistical mismatch. Existing SAR image generation methods either focus on distribution matching without sufficiently exploiting scattering-related structural cues, or emphasize angle conditioning while failing to jointly preserve physically plausible dominant scattering-response variations and realistic background speckle statistics at unseen aspect angles. To address this issue, we propose a physically consistent framework for SAR image generation at unseen aspect angles. The proposed method introduces an ASC-inspired sparse scattering-structure prior to approximate the dominant scattering responses in the SAR image plane. Rather than performing full parametric ASC inversion, this prior serves as a differentiable and angle-aware structural proxy that guides the generator toward synthesizing SAR images with structurally plausible scattering layouts. In addition, a dual-consistency scheme is introduced to jointly enforce target-region scattering consistency and background-region statistical consistency, thereby improving the physical realism of the generated results in both the target and background regions. Extensive experiments under strict unseen-angle interpolation and hold-out protocols demonstrate that the proposed method consistently outperforms representative baselines in image fidelity, target-region scattering consistency, background statistical consistency, and angle-conditioned consistency. Further visualization and ablation studies verify the critical role of the ASC-inspired sparse scattering-structure prior in physically consistent SAR view completion.

### [239] [Mapping Evapotranspiration Patterns in the Desert-Oasis Ecotone Using UAV-Based Thermal Infrared Imagery with a Three-Temperature Model](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132242)
*Siying Li,Yuhua Xing,Dapeng Zhang,Pei Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究通过将无人机热红外遥感与三温度(3T)模型相结合，在河西走廊荒漠-绿洲交错带实现了米级高分辨率蒸散发(ET)估算，有效捕捉了从农田到荒漠的ET空间梯度，空间验证R²达0.90-0.95，点尺度MAE为0.38 mm d⁻¹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 荒漠-绿洲交错带因气象观测稀疏和卫星遥感空间分辨率粗，难以解析高度异质的下垫面条件，导致ET估算面临挑战。

Method: 将无人机热红外遥感获取的米级地表温度(LST)与气象、植被数据输入三温度(3T)模型，生成高分辨率ET图，并分别用SEBAL模型(空间验证)和双源模型(点验证)进行精度评估。

Result: (1) 3T模型有效捕捉了从农田(3-10.69 mm d⁻¹)到防护林(3-6 mm d⁻¹)再到沙漠(<3 mm d⁻¹)的ET递减梯度。(2) 空间验证R²=0.90-0.95，RMSE=0.22-0.43 mm d⁻¹，农田精度最高(R²=0.92, RMSE=0.24 mm d⁻¹)。(3) 点验证MAE=0.38 mm d⁻¹。

Abstract (英文): Evapotranspiration (ET) estimation in desert-oasis ecotones remains challenging due to sparse meteorological observations and the coarse spatial resolution of satellite remote sensing, which limit the ability to resolve highly heterogeneous surface conditions. To address this issue, this study develops a high-resolution ET estimation framework by integrating unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV)-based thermal infrared remote sensing with a three-temperature (3T) model in the Hexi Corridor. UAV-derived land surface temperature (LST) at meter-scale resolution, together with meteorological and vegetation data, was used to drive the model and generate high-resolution ET maps. The model’s performance was validated spatially against the Surface Energy Balance Algorithm for Land (SEBAL) model and at the point-scale against a two-source model. The results show that: (1) The 3T model effectively captured the spatial gradient of decreasing ET from cropland (3–10.69 mm d−1), through shelterbelts (3–6 mm d−1), to desert areas (&lt;3 mm d−1). The model achieved highest accuracy in cropland (R2 = 0.92; RMSE = 0.24 mm d−1), with slight overestimation in shelterbelts. (3) Point-scale validation against the two-source model yielded an MAE of 0.38 mm d−1. This study demonstrates the effectiveness of combining UAV thermal infrared data with the 3T model for high-resolution ET simulation in complex ecological transition zones, offering a promising technical approach for ecohydrological monitoring and water resource assessment in arid regions.

### [240] [Multi-Scale Assessment of Nighttime Heat Health Risk and Dominant Factors Using MODIS and SDGSAT-1 Observations](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132243)
*Zhuang Tan,Qixia Man,Baolei Zhang,Pinliang Dong,Haiying Sun,Zhongchang Sun,Linlin Lu,Changyong Dou,Xiaomin Yang,Changyin Han,Cong Zhou,Xia Sun,Yi-Xiang Wang,Z G Li*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: (1) 宏观上，高风险区集中在鲁南和主要城市核心区；(2) 精细尺度上，内陆城市整体风险高于沿海城市，且内陆城市间空间格局相似；(3) 高风险单元（区级和街区级）的主导因子配置更复杂；(4) LCZ 1-2以多主导因子为主，LCZ 6/9以无主导因子为主。

Conclusion: 本研究为热风险治理提供了多层次视角，既支撑宏观政策制定，也指导精细干预，有助于建设更可持续和韧性的城市。

Abstract (英文): Climate change is amplifying heat-related health risks, making heat health risk assessment increasingly important for sustainable urban development. However, current studies still face three challenges: (1) macro-scale and fine-scale assessments remain weakly linked; (2) nighttime heat health risk has received limited attention; and (3) dominant factor identification remains insufficient, especially within the Local Climate Zone (LCZ) framework. To address these gaps, this study developed a hazard–exposure–vulnerability-based, multi-scale framework for assessing nighttime heat health risk in Shandong Province, China. At the macro scale, MODIS nighttime land surface temperature (1 km) was used to characterize heat hazard, and district-level risk was assessed by integrating socio-statistical data. Hotspot analysis was then applied to identify high-risk clusters and select cities for fine-scale assessment. At the fine scale, SDGSAT-1 thermal infrared data (30 m) were used to characterize intra-urban nighttime heat hazard, and block-level risk was assessed by integrating socioeconomic and urban infrastructure data. Dominant risk factors were further identified for each spatial unit. Results show that (1) at the macro scale, high nighttime heat health risk districts are concentrated mainly in southern Shandong and major urban cores; (2) at the fine scale, overall risk is higher in inland cities than in the coastal city, and the inland cities show similar spatial patterns; (3) at both district and block units, higher risk levels are associated with more complex dominant factor configurations; and (4) compact high- and mid-rise zones (LCZ 1–2) are mainly characterized by multiple dominant factors, whereas open low-rise/sparsely built zones (LCZ 6/9) are mainly characterized by no dominant factor. This study provides a multi-level perspective for heat-risk governance, offers a scientific basis for both macro-scale policy formulation and fine-scale intervention, and contributes to more sustainable and resilient cities.

### [241] [Estimation of High-Resolution Multi-Layer Soil Moisture Using Land Data Assimilation and the Three-Cornered Hat Method](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132248)
*Xinlei He,Wenbin Zhu,Shaomin Liu,Tongren Xu,Zhitao Wu,Sayed M. Bateni,Zhen Hao,Xiang Li,Dongxin Wu,Hanxue Liang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 同化HRSM（DA_HRSM）显著改善了Noah-MP模型对地表和根区土壤湿度的估计；DA_HRSM模拟的土壤湿度相对不确定性更低；与同化SMAP土壤湿度相比，DA_HRSM提供了更高分辨率的土壤湿度空间特征并增强了20个灌区的空间异质性；DA_HRSM有效捕捉了云南中部春旱，与PDSI一致性良好。

Conclusion: 将高分辨率土壤湿度数据纳入农业和干旱监测系统具有显著优势，DA_HRSM方法能够在不牺牲空间细节的前提下提升土壤湿度廓线估计精度，为精细尺度的干旱监测和农业管理提供有力支撑。

Abstract (英文): Soil moisture (SM) plays a pivotal role in regulating terrestrial energy-water exchanges and exerts substantial influence on agricultural productivity. In this study, a high-resolution soil moisture (HRSM) dataset (16 m) was generated by integrating multi-source remote sensing data from SMAP, HJ-2, Sentinel-2, and Gaofen-6, together with the Enhanced Spatial and Temporal Adaptive Reflectance Fusion Model. The data assimilation (DA) method was implemented for assimilating HRSM within the Ensemble Kalman Filter (EnKF) framework using the Noah-MP model at a spatial resolution of 1 km. To enhance the spatial detail of SM, HRSM and its relative uncertainties derived from the three-cornered hat (TCH) method were used to update the observation error and Kalman gain in the EnKF framework, thereby improving SM profile estimates at a 16 m resolution. The performance of the DA method was evaluated against in situ measurements during the spring drought period in central Yunnan Province, China. The results show that assimilating HRSM (DA_HRSM) significantly improves surface and root-zone SM estimates in the Noah-MP model. The simulated SM from the DA_HRSM method demonstrates lower relative uncertainty. Compared to the assimilation of SMAP SM, the DA_HRSM method provides higher-resolution spatial features of SM and enhances spatial heterogeneity across 20 irrigation districts. The DA_HRSM method effectively captured the spring drought in central Yunnan, demonstrating good agreement with the Palmer Drought Severity Index (PDSI). The result highlights the advantages of incorporating high-resolution SM data into agricultural and drought monitoring systems.

### [242] [Reconstruction of Land Surface Temperature Based on EATC Constraints and Spatially Adaptive Residual Correction: A Case Study of the Qinghai–Tibet Engineering Corridor](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132254)
*Minghan Xu,Qian Li,Shufang Tian,Shiqi Kuang,Tianqi Li*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出了一种物理约束的空间残差学习框架（PCSRL），结合增强年温度循环（EATC）模型和地理加权XGBoost（G-XGBoost）算法，用于重建青藏高原复杂地形下缺失的卫星地表温度数据。在2017年MODIS LST数据集上验证，R²=0.88，RMSE=1.92 K，平均偏差0.07 K，冬季表现最佳（RMSE=1.19 K）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 卫星LST产品受云覆盖和大气条件影响，在青藏高原等复杂地形下存在大范围数据缺失。现有时空插值方法在处理大面积空缺时精度有限，物理模型因气象输入不足而受限，传统数据驱动方法忽略局部空间变异导致平滑和系统性误差。

Method: 首先利用增强年温度循环（EATC）模型捕捉LST的时间基线，然后将多源辅助数据集成到地理加权XGBoost（G-XGBoost）算法中，对空间非线性残差进行建模，实现物理模型与数据驱动方法的混合框架。

Result: R²=0.88, RMSE=1.92 K, 平均偏差0.07 K；冬季RMSE=1.19 K表现最佳；有效减少了边界伪影，通过自适应局部带宽和权重调整准确再现了复杂地形的热空间模式。

Conclusion: 该物理约束的空间残差学习框架为异质高寒地表的高精度LST重建提供了一种可靠方法，优于单独的物理模型和全局机器学习模型。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本论文本身就是遥感领域论文。改进方案：（1）可将EATC模型替换为更精细的时序分解方法（如STL或BFAST）以适应非平稳气候信号；（2）G-XGBoost可进一步结合深度空间编码（如Spatial Transformer Networks）提升非线性残差捕捉能力；（3）引入多传感器融合（如Sentinel-3 SLSTR与MODIS）提高时间分辨率；（4）将框架扩展到全球尺度时，需考虑不同气候区的参数自适应策略。

Abstract (英文): Satellite-based land surface temperature (LST) products are frequently affected by cloud cover and atmospheric conditions, resulting in missing data that significantly limits the continuous monitoring of the thermal environment in complex terrains, such as the Tibetan Plateau. Existing spatiotemporal interpolation methods face clear accuracy limitations when addressing extensive data gaps, while physical models often struggle due to insufficient meteorological inputs in complex landscapes. Moreover, conventional data-driven approaches usually overlook local spatial variations, resulting in smoothed thermal patterns and systematic errors. To overcome these issues, we propose a Physically Constrained Spatial Residual Learning framework. In this framework, we use the Enhanced Annual Temperature Cycle (EATC) model to capture the temporal baseline of LST first. Then, we integrate multi-source auxiliary data into the Geographical-XGBoost (G-XGBoost) algorithm to model spatial nonlinear residuals. Using simulated cloud masks on the 2017 MODIS LST dataset from the Qinghai–Tibet Engineering Corridor, we show that the hybrid model outperforms both individual physical models and global machine learning models in accuracy and spatial detail recovery. Validation results yield an R2 of 0.88, an RMSE of 1.92 K, and a mean bias of 0.07 K. Seasonal evaluations indicate best performance in winter (RMSE = 1.19 K) with robust performance in summer. Furthermore, the framework reduces boundary artifacts and accurately reproduces thermal spatial patterns in complex terrain through adaptive local bandwidth and weight adjustments. This approach provides a reliable method for high-precision LST reconstruction over heterogeneous alpine surfaces.

### [243] [Filling Satellite Microwave Observation Gaps via Generative Synthesis](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132256)
*Han Du,Baoxiang Pan,Fan Ping,J Q Xu,Congyi Nai,Sencan Sun,Jie Chao,Jingnan Wang,Shangshang Yang,Xi Chen,Jingyuan Li,J. Mao,Lei Yin,Yupeng Li,Ziniu Xiao*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: MIDAS是一种概率框架，利用扩散模型从10分钟间隔的红外观测中估计地球静止卫星全圆盘区域的微波亮温场，在183 GHz湿度探测通道上实现优于1.15 K的精度，并通过融合采样机制实时融入极轨卫星观测约束，显著提升降水预报和热带气旋路径预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极轨微波辐射计提供全天候大气状态测量，但重访间隔长达数小时，在快速演变的天气事件中存在关键观测空白。解决这一时空分辨率不足的问题，实现高频次、全圆盘的微波亮温场估计。

Method: 基于扩散概率模型（diffusion probabilistic model）的MIDAS框架，从10分钟间隔的地球静止卫星红外观测中估计极轨微波亮温场；通过合并采样（merge-sampling）机制实时融入实际极轨观测作为物理约束；针对MWHS-2在183 GHz附近的五个湿度探测通道进行建模。

Result: 多数情况下相对误差低于0.5%，通道平均绝对误差1.15 K，优于U-Net基线（1.43 K）；合并采样使集成RMSE降低20%以上，概率校准提升超过30%；热带气旋路径误差从约110 km降至40 km，极端降水预报改善显著。

Conclusion: 生成模型有能力补充稀疏的观测覆盖，为下游应用提供物理合理的微波湿度场；MIDAS生成的场在数据同化实验中可取得与真实卫星观测相当的预报改进效果。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该框架可直接应用于遥感领域，改进方向包括：(1)扩展到其他微波频率通道（如低频温度探测通道）以提供更全面的热力学信息；(2)将输入从红外扩展至多光谱或高光谱数据，提升云区重建精度；(3)引入时间序列扩散模型或视频扩散架构，利用时序一致性进一步提升精度；(4)在缺乏地球静止红外数据的区域（如极地），探索利用极轨红外数据与时空插值的替代方案；(5)将该生成框架与物理约束数据同化系统更深度耦合，实现端到端的实时预报增强。

Abstract (英文): Polar-orbiting microwave radiometers provide indispensable all-weather measurements of the atmospheric state, yet revisit intervals of many hours leave critical gaps during rapidly evolving weather events. To address this limitation, we developed MIDAS (Microwave Inference via Diffusion Across Satellites), a probabilistic framework that estimates microwave brightness temperature (BT) fields across the geostationary full-disk domain from infrared observations at 10 min intervals. This study focuses on the five Microwave Humidity Sounder-2 (MWHS-2) humidity-sounding channels near 183 GHz, which provide vertically resolved water vapor information. MIDAS achieves relative errors below 0.5% for the majority of cases, with a channel-averaged mean absolute error of 1.15 K, outperforming a deterministic U-Net baseline (1.43 K). Beyond per-sample evaluation, MIDAS reproduces large-scale climatological patterns across the full-disk domain over a three-month summer period, consistent with Radiative Transfer for TOVS–Scattering (RTTOV-SCATT) simulations. In deep convective scenes where reconstruction is most difficult, the ensemble spread naturally tracks reconstruction difficulty, providing a built-in indicator of prediction confidence. Notably, MIDAS incorporates real-time polar-orbiting observations as physical constraints via a merge-sampling mechanism, reducing ensemble RMSE by over 20% and improving probabilistic calibration by more than 30%. Proof-of-concept assimilation experiments for two high-impact weather cases show that MIDAS-generated fields yield forecast improvements comparable to those from real satellite observations, reducing tropical cyclone track errors from approximately 110 km to 40 km and improving heavy precipitation forecasts at extreme rainfall thresholds where direct infrared assimilation shows no benefit. Overall, our framework demonstrates the potential of generative models to supplement sparse observational coverage and provide physically plausible microwave humidity fields for downstream applications.

</details>


### [244] [Spatial-Temporal Evolution of Proglacial Lake Volumes and Estimation Models in the Himalaya and Nyainqentanglha Ranges](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132249)

TL;DR: 本研究融合实地测深数据与区域数据集，优化了喜马拉雅和念青唐古拉山脉冰前湖的体积与最大深度经验模型，发现1990-2020年间湖体积显著扩张（西喜马拉雅+46.7%，中喜马拉雅+46.4%，东喜马拉雅+51.5%，念青唐古拉+92.9%），为GLOF灾害评估提供了关键参数约束。

Method: 整合10个冰前湖的实地测深数据与综合区域数据集，推导优化的湖泊体积和最大深度经验模型；利用统计误差指标和独立数据集进行鲁棒性验证；与14个已有公式对比评估性能；应用最优缩放关系重建1990-2020年研究区冰前湖的体积时空变化。

Result: 区域专属模型相比14个现有公式在捕捉局地地貌特征方面表现更优；1990-2020年间，西喜马拉雅湖体积增加46.7%，中喜马拉雅增加46.4%，东喜马拉雅增加51.5%，念青唐古拉山增加约92.9%。

Conclusion: 研究结果为基于卫星的水文监测提供了关键参数约束，显著提升了喜马拉雅和念青唐古拉山脉GLOF灾害评估的可靠性。

Abstract (英文): Volume quantification of proglacial lakes is a fundamental prerequisite for reliable hydrodynamic modeling and peak discharge estimation during glacial lake outburst floods (GLOFs). In this study, we integrated in situ bathymetric surveys of 10 proglacial lakes across the Himalaya and Nyainqentanglha ranges with a comprehensive regional dataset to derive optimized empirical models for lake volume and maximum depth. The predictive robustness of these models was rigorously validated using statistical error metrics and independent datasets. Comparative analysis with 14 established formulas demonstrates that our region-specific models yield superior performance in capturing local geomorphological characteristics. Leveraging these refined scaling relationships, we reconstructed the spatiotemporal volume changes in proglacial lakes across the study region from 1990 to 2020. Our analysis reveals significant lake expansion over the past three decades: lake volumes in the Western and Central Himalayas increased by 46.7% and 46.4%, respectively. Notably, the Eastern Himalayas exhibited a volume increase of 51.5%, while the Nyainqentanglha Mountains experienced a substantial expansion of approximately 92.9%. These findings provide critical parametric constraints for satellite-based hydrological monitoring and significantly enhance the reliability of GLOF hazard assessments in the Himalaya and Nyainqentanglha ranges.

### [245] [DEAF-Net: Dual-Domain Enhanced Adaptive Fusion Network for UAV Visible–Infrared Object Detection](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132241)
*Qian Weng,Yu Zhang,Xiansheng Huang,Liming Deng,Jiawen Lin*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出DEAF-Net，一种面向无人机多模态目标检测的双域增强自适应融合网络。其核心包括双域渐进细化模块（DDPR，通过频域可学习滤波+空间域尺度感知上下文精炼抑制噪声、增强纹理）和一致性-差异性引导融合策略（CDGF，利用VMamba选择性扫描机制建模模态间共性与差异模式，结合熵权全局先验动态生成局部模态贡献图进行自适应融合）。在DroneVehicle和VEDAI数据集上，mAP@0.5分别达到81.9%和76.2%，在低光照、浓雾和稀疏类别场景下表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无人机多模态（可见光+红外）目标检测方法采用静态融合策略，忽略了模态可靠性的空间异质性，且未充分探索空间-频域协同表征，导致在动态环境（复杂光照、天气变化）中鲁棒性受限。

Method: （1）双域渐进细化模块（DDPR）：频域可学习滤波抑制噪声 + 空间域尺度感知上下文精炼增强纹理，获得纯净融合特征基座；（2）一致性-差异性引导融合策略（CDGF）：基于VMamba选择性扫描机制建模模态间一致/差异模式，动态生成局部模态贡献图实现自适应融合，并利用熵权全局场景先验进行校准。

Result: 在DroneVehicle和VEDAI数据集上，mAP@0.5分别达到81.9%和76.2%，优于主流多模态检测方法；在低光照、浓雾和稀疏类别场景下鲁棒性显著提升。

Conclusion: DEAF-Net通过双域协同增强与自适应融合策略，有效解决了多模态无人机目标检测中模态可靠性空间异质性和频域-空间表征不足的问题，提升了复杂环境下的检测鲁棒性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。具体方案：（1）将该双域渐进细化思路迁移至遥感多传感器融合（如SAR+光学、多光谱+高光谱），通过频域滤波抑制相干斑噪声或云雾干扰；（2）CDGF的VMamba交叉模态建模可直接用于遥感多源数据融合（如DEM+光谱），动态评估各源在当前空间位置的可信度；（3）可进一步引入遥感特有的地形/地物先验（如NDVI、建筑物高度）作为全局熵权先验的补充；（4）轻量化适配机载或星载边缘计算平台。

Abstract (英文): In Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV) object detection tasks, complex lighting conditions and variable weather render robust all-weather perception challenging when relying solely on the visible modality. Although infrared modalities can provide complementary information, the reliability of individual modalities is highly scene-dependent. Existing multimodal detection methods typically adopt static fusion strategies, which ignore spatial heterogeneity of modal reliability and under-explore spatial-frequency collaborative representation, thus limiting detection robustness in dynamic environments. To address these issues, this paper proposes a Dual-domain Enhanced Adaptive Fusion Network (DEAF-Net), with two core innovative modules to tackle the above challenges. First, the Dual Domain Progressive Refinement (DDPR) module mitigates feature degradation caused by poor imaging conditions via the joint design of frequency-domain learnable filtering and scale-aware contextual refinement in the spatial domain, effectively suppressing noise, enhancing textures, and yielding a purified feature basis for fusion. Second, the Consistency–Discrepancy Guided Fusion (CDGF) strategy leverages the selective scanning mechanism of VMamba to model consistent and differential patterns across modalities, dynamically generates local modal contribution maps for adaptive fusion, and integrates global scene prior via entropy weights for calibration. Extensive experiments on the DroneVehicle and VEDAI datasets show that DEAF-Net outperforms mainstream multimodal detection methods, achieving mAP@0.5 scores of 81.9% and 76.2%, respectively, while delivering improved robustness in low-light, dense fog, and sparse-category scenarios.

### [246] [Stereo Matching in Satellite Imagery: A Depth Estimation Foundation Model-Assisted Iterative Approach](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132245)
*Kunpeng Hu,Wei Zhao*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出IFMA-Stereo，一种结合单目深度基础模型与多尺度空间信息金字塔的双目视差估计方法，通过注意力交互机制和循环迭代优化模块，在光学遥感立体匹配任务中解决了极端成像几何、无纹理区域、重复图案及时空异质性等挑战，在US3D和高分七号数据集上达到了SOTA精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光学遥感三维重建中的高分辨率卫星立体匹配面临极端成像几何、无纹理/重复图案、遮挡以及时空异质性导致的场景变化等挑战，现有方法难以有效应对这些复杂情况。

Method: 1) 构建多尺度空间信息金字塔，联合集成单目深度基础模型与视差提取网络；2) 在特征层面设计注意力交互机制，捕获多维上下文依赖关系，将通用场景理解先验转化为适合立体代价体构建的长程关联特征；3) 在像素层面设计循环迭代细化模块，在迭代过程中嵌入基础模型的深度信息并进行联合优化，提升模型在几何复杂区域的适应性。

Result: 在US3D数据集上EPE为1.347、D1误差为7.26%；在高分七号数据集上EPE为1.585、D1误差为13.41%；在未见过的城区也能给出精确预测，表现出强泛化能力；但推理时间比基线方法增加。

Conclusion: IFMA-Stereo在遥感视差估计任务中达到了SOTA精度，有效缓解了无纹理区域、视差不连续、重复图案以及时空异质性导致的预测误差，验证了单目深度基础模型与立体匹配网络联合优化的可行性与优越性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：1) 可引入多视角时序数据（如不同时相的高分影像）进一步增强时空异质性鲁棒性；2) 针对推理速度瓶颈，可设计轻量化注意力模块或知识蒸馏策略降低计算开销；3) 可将该框架扩展至多视图立体匹配（MVS）任务，结合多基线立体影像提升重建完整性；4) 可引入SAR与光学影像的跨模态联合优化，利用SAR对纹理不敏感的特性补偿光学影像在无纹理区域的不足。

Abstract (英文): In optical remote sensing 3D reconstruction, high-resolution satellite stereo matching is a critical task, yet it is challenged by extreme imaging geometries, texture-less and repetitive patterns, occlusions, and scene variations caused by spatio-temporal heterogeneity. To address these issues, we propose IFMA-Stereo, an innovative binocular disparity estimation method that leverages a monocular depth foundation model. Our approach constructs a multi-scale spatial information pyramid to jointly integrate the foundation model with a disparity extraction network. At the feature level, an attention interaction mechanism captures multi-dimensional contextual dependencies and transforms general scene understanding priors into long-range associative features suitable for stereo cost volume construction. At the pixel level, a cyclic iterative refinement module embeds depth information from the foundation model throughout the iteration process and performs joint optimization, enhancing the model’s adaptability in geometrically complex regions. Experiments on the US3D and GaoFen-7 datasets demonstrate that IFMA-Stereo achieves superior performance in challenging areas (texture-less regions, disparity discontinuities, repetitive patterns) and effectively mitigates prediction errors caused by spatio-temporal heterogeneity, albeit at the cost of increased inference time compared to baseline methods. Quantitatively, the method achieves an end-point error (EPE) of 1.347 and a D1 error of 7.26% on the US3D dataset, and an EPE of 1.585 and a D1 error of 13.41% on the GaoFen-7 dataset. Notably, the method also yields precise predictions for unseen urban areas, indicating strong generalization. These results confirm that IFMA-Stereo achieves state-of-the-art accuracy in remote sensing disparity estimation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract (英文): High-precision WTC is essential for satellite altimetry and ocean dynamic environment monitoring. Existing WTC approaches often rely on globally unified statistical frameworks, which inadequately represent wind-speed-dependent nonlinear sea-surface microwave radiative responses and are prone to systematic bias under uneven observation distributions. To address these limitations, this study proposes an adaptive WTC method integrating overlapping wind-regime modeling, multi-scale collaborative sample balancing, and a model soft-fusion strategy. Firstly, a modeling framework with overlapping transition zones for low-, moderate-, and high-wind-speed regimes is established according to wind-speed-driven variations in sea-surface radiative responses, and sub-models are trained independently. Subsequently, a multi-scale sample balancing, combining global and local weights, is designed to enhance learning from sparse samples. Finally, a soft-fusion strategy based on a trapezoidal membership function is applied to dynamically weight sub-model outputs, ensuring retrieval continuity across transition zones. Using HY-2C Calibration Microwave Radiometer (CMR) observations, the proposed method is developed, trained, and evaluated against model-derived WTC and collocated Jason-3 AMR-2 measurements. Results show that the proposed method improves overall WTC retrieval accuracy and stability while effectively reducing systematic biases under wind-speed regimes with sparse observations, providing an effective and robust approach for high-accuracy WTC retrieval under various wind-speed conditions.

### [248] [On the Spectral–Phenological Features for Crop Mapping Under Complex Planting Patterns: A Case Study in Jiangsu Province, China](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132244)
*Ziyin You,Jiajun Wu,X F Wang,Bo Wang,Xuan Xu,Pei Zhan,N LI,Chitfai Yan*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 针对碎片化农业景观中作物制图面临的物候重叠和多源变量冗余问题，本研究利用Sentinel-1/2影像构建275个季节特异性光谱-物候特征变量，提出先验引导遗传算法（GA）进行特征选择，最终GA选取的9-39个变量子集在五类作物制图中达到91.77%的总体精度和93.95%的目标作物F1分数，证实了随机森林工作流中作物特异性、可解释的降维策略的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 碎片化农业景观中，作物物候期重叠以及多源时间序列变量之间的冗余性导致作物制图精度受限，亟需有效的特征选择方法来提升分类性能和模型可解释性。

Method: 基于Sentinel-1/2影像（2022.12-2023.12）构建275个季节特异性光谱-物候特征月变量；利用辅助二值随机森林估算OOB置换重要性构建搜索先验；采用先验引导遗传算法进行紧凑特征子集筛选；使用作物特异性五类随机森林模型评估候选子集并生成最终分类。

Result: GA选取的9-39变量子集在独立验证集上达到五类总体精度91.77%，目标作物F1分数93.95%；光学/植被指数方案、仅SAR方案和完整特征库的目标作物F1分别为78.42%、83.74%和86.96%；VH后向散射和SWIR相关指数（STI、NDTI）具有重复预测贡献。

Conclusion: 研究支持在随机森林工作流中进行作物特异性、可解释的降维，但更广泛的迁移性需要多年份和多区域的进一步评估。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：（1）可将先验引导GA特征选择框架引入高光谱遥感作物分类，解决波段冗余问题；（2）该方法可迁移至城市不透水面制图或湿地分类等具有时间序列特征的遥感任务；（3）可结合深度学习（如1D-CNN或Transformer）替代RF作为子集评估器，探索非线性特征交互；（4）STI和NDTI等SWIR指数在作物分类中的强贡献提示可进一步挖掘SWIR波段在植被胁迫监测中的潜力。

Abstract (英文): Accurate crop mapping in fragmented agricultural landscapes is challenged by overlapping crop calendars and redundancy among multi-source time-series variables. Using Sentinel-1/2 imagery from December 2022 to December 2023, we constructed 275 season-specific spectral–phenological feature–month variables (125 for summer crops and 150 for winter crops) for rice, maize, soybean, winter wheat, and winter rapeseed in Jiangsu Province, China. An auxiliary binary Random Forest (RF) was used to estimate out-of-bag (OOB) permutation-based predictive contributions and construct search priors. A prior-guided genetic algorithm (GA) then identified compact subsets, with crop-specific five-class RF models used both to evaluate candidate subsets and to produce the final classifications. A fixed stratified 80/20 development–validation split was maintained throughout the analysis, with the validation subset reserved for final assessment. August and April were the principal discriminative periods for summer and winter crops, respectively, while VH backscatter and SWIR-related indices, particularly STI and NDTI, showed recurrent predictive contributions across crops. On the independent validation subset, the optical/vegetation-index scheme, SAR-only scheme, and the complete feature library achieved mean target-crop F1-scores of 78.42%, 83.74%, and 86.96%, respectively. The GA-selected subsets retained 9–39 variables and achieved a mean five-class overall accuracy of 91.77% and a mean target-crop F1-score of 93.95%. After non-target classes were merged into a single background class, the integrated seasonal maps achieved overall accuracies of 81.20–95.03% on the same validation subset. Supplementary classifier comparisons indicated that subset effects depended on the crop and learning algorithm. The findings support crop-specific, interpretable dimensionality reduction within the RF workflow, while broader transferability requires multi-year and multi-region evaluation.

</details>


### [249] [Deep Learning Enables the Automatic Mapping of Tell Sites on Satellite Synthetic Aperture Radar Products](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132255)
*Elena Chiricallo,Giulio Poggi,Sara Ferro,Sebastiano Vascon,Arianna Traviglia*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于YOLOv8-Seg的深度学习流水线，利用Sentinel-1 SAR影像和DEM数据自动检测和分割伊拉克中部的考古土丘(tell sites)，平均精度0.495，IoU 0.361，并验证了对伊朗地区的可迁移性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SAR技术虽已用于考古景观研究，但缺乏鲁棒的自动化分析方法，限制了其在大规模考古勘探中的应用。本文旨在解决这一自动化瓶颈。

Method: 构建深度学习流水线，采用YOLOv8-Seg实例分割模型，输入为Copernicus Sentinel-1 SAR影像（干涉宽幅模式）和Copernicus全球30米DEM数据，对伊拉克中部考古土丘进行自动检测与分割。

Result: 测试区平均精度(AP)为0.495±0.010，像素级IoU为0.361±0.048；模型检测到此前未绘制的潜在遗址；在伊朗邻近区域的迁移性测试表明需要区域微调。

Conclusion: 该工作为基于SAR的深度学习考古勘探建立了基线，证明了深度学习在SAR考古自动化分析中的可行性与迁移潜力，但需针对不同区域的地貌与环境差异进行微调。

Abstract (英文): Satellite Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR) is an established technology for studying and monitoring archaeological landscapes, providing insights into surface morphology and the presence of near subsurface features. However, its application in large-scale archaeological prospection is limited by the lack of robust, automated methods for SAR data analysis. This study introduces a novel Deep Learning pipeline to automatically detect and segment archaeological settlement mounds, known as tells, in central Iraq on satellite SAR data. The pipeline leverages a state-of-the-art supervised method for instance segmentation, YOLOv8-Seg, and medium-resolution satellite SAR products, specifically the Copernicus Sentinel-1 Interferometric Wide Swath Mode Ground Range Detected and Copernicus Global 30-m Digital Elevation Model products. The model identifies tell sites with an Average Precision of 0.495±0.010 and a pixel-wise Intersection over Union of 0.361±0.048 over the test areas. Archaeological interpretation of the model’s inferences confirms its reliability in locating and segmenting archaeological sites, leading also to the identification of previously unmapped potential sites. After a main test in central Iraq, the proposed workflow demonstrates promising transferability to a nearby test area in Iran, although with a need for regional fine-tuning to account for inherent variations in feature morphology and environmental context. This research establishes a baseline for future Deep Learning applications in Synthetic Aperture Radar-based archaeological prospection.

### [250] [Mapping Acid Mine Drainage Areas with Sentinel-2 and WorldView-3 VNIR Satellite Images: An Example in the SE of Spain](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132240)
*Inés Pereira,Eduardo García‐Meléndez,Montserrat Ferrer‐Julià,H.M.A. van der Werff*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文评估并比较了Sentinel-2和WorldView-3 VNIR波段在西班牙Cartagena–La Unión矿区识别和区分次生铁矿物（赤铁矿、针铁矿、黄钾铁矾）的能力。通过波段比和抛物线拟合方法分析数据，并以74个土壤样本的X射线衍射结果进行验证。结果表明，Sentinel-2在区分这三种矿物方面表现更优，这得益于其红边和近红外波段配置，且数据免费获取，适用于矿山环境氧化过程的系统监测与风险评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硫化矿开采导致硫化物氧化，产生酸性矿山排水（AMD）并形成次生铁矿物。这些矿物在VNIR区域具有诊断性光谱特征，因此多光谱卫星数据可作为一种经济有效的监测手段。本文旨在评估和比较两种多光谱传感器（Sentinel-2和WorldView-3）在制图和区分这些次生铁矿物方面的性能，为矿区环境监测提供技术参考。

Method: 研究采用两种遥感分析方法处理Sentinel-2和WorldView-3 VNIR数据：1）波段比（band ratio）技术，以宽光谱模式而非确定性矿物识别进行解译；2）抛物线拟合（parabola fitting）技术，聚焦于反射率最大值特征。通过74个地表土壤样本的X射线衍射（XRD）分析对矿物制图结果进行地面验证。

Result: 两种传感器均能再现铁矿物分布的主要空间格局。Sentinel-2数据在区分赤铁矿、针铁矿和黄钾铁矾方面表现更优，尤其是在抛物线拟合方法下；而WorldView-3 VNIR数据主要能区分赤铁矿与针铁矿-黄钾铁矾组合体。Sentinel-2的更好性能归因于其红边和近红外波段配置。

Conclusion: 免费可用的Sentinel-2影像能够支持矿山环境中氧化过程的系统监测，并有助于退化景观的环境风险评估。该研究证实了Sentinel-2在矿区次生铁矿物精细制图中的实用价值，为酸性矿山排水污染的遥感监测提供了低成本、高效率的技术方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感应用论文，可作为遥感与矿山环境交叉的典型案例。改进方向：1）方法上可引入机器学习分类器（如随机森林、支持向量机）结合光谱特征进行矿物分类，提升区分精度；2）可融合Sentinel-2的SWIR波段（本文未使用）以增强矿物识别能力；3）结合时序Sentinel-2数据分析矿物演变的动态过程；4）将抛物线拟合参数作为特征输入深度学习模型进行端到端矿物填图；5）可扩展到其他矿区验证方法的普适性，并建立区域尺度的AMD风险预警模型。

Abstract (英文): Mining of sulfide-rich deposits enhances the oxidation of sulfide minerals, generating acid mine drainage (AMD) characterized by high sulphate and dissolved metal concentrations and the formation of secondary iron minerals (hematite, goethite, and jarosite). As these minerals display diagnostic features in the visible–near-infrared (VNIR) region, multispectral satellite data provide a cost-effective means of monitoring. Here, the performances of Sentinel-2 and the VNIR bands from WorldView-3 are assessed and compared for the mapping and discrimination of secondary iron minerals in Sierra Minera de Cartagena–La Unión (SE Spain). Both datasets were analyzed using a band ratio and a parabola fitting technique focused on reflectance maxima. Band ratio results were interpreted as broad spectral patterns rather than definitive mineral identifications. Mineral maps were validated by applying X-ray diffraction on 74 surface soil samples. Although both sensors were able to reproduce the main spatial patterns of iron mineral distribution, Sentinel-2 data better discriminated hematite, goethite, and jarosite, especially when using the parabola fitting approach, whereas WorldView-3 VNIR data distinguished mainly hematite from the combined goethite–jarosite group. The better performance of Sentinel-2 is attributed to its red-edge and near-infrared band configuration. These findings indicate that freely available Sentinel-2 imagery can support systematic monitoring of oxidation processes in mining environments and contribute to environmental risk assessment in degraded landscapes.

### [251] [A Sentinel-2-Based Framework for Methane Point-Source Detection and Quantification Using Low-Reflectance Artifact Detection](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132251)
*Kun Cai,T -Y Chen,Liang Zheng,Shenshen Li,Xinhui Zhou,Ying Liu,X Chen*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为MBMC（多波段多约束）的综合甲烷监测框架，利用Sentinel-2 MSI影像，通过LRAD算法抑制低反射率伪影、MBMP差分吸收反演模型和IME排放量化方法，实现了对甲烷点源的高分辨率、高频率卫星监测与排放量化，在亚利桑那州对照实验中排放速率MAPE为21.6%，并在中国西北天然气田成功识别了多个甲烷点源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有卫星监测甲烷点源存在空间覆盖范围有限和地表信号干扰等技术瓶颈，亟需一种高分辨率、高频率且能有效抑制地表伪影的甲烷监测方法，以支持气候减缓策略和排放清单的精细化。

Method: 提出MBMC框架，包含三个核心模块：(1) LRAD算法用于抑制低反射率地表和异质背景产生的伪影；(2) MBMP差分吸收反演模型用于反演甲烷柱浓度增强；(3) IME方法用于排放量化。此外还开发了结合形态学操作与空间数据库的半自动羽流分割工作流程。

Result: 在亚利桑那州单盲对照实验中，对于0.5~3.0 t/h的排放速率，MAPE为21.6%；能够检测约0.5 t/h以上的排放。在中国西北天然气田的Sentinel-2观测中成功识别并量化了多个与集气站相关的甲烷点源。

Conclusion: MBMC框架为基于Sentinel-2的高分辨率、高频率卫星甲烷点源监测提供了一种实用方法，可支持油气行业甲烷排放清单的细化和减排策略的制定。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。改进方案：(1) 可引入多时相融合策略（如LSTM或时空融合模型）以缓解云覆盖导致的观测缺失问题；(2) 将LRAD算法扩展到其他痕量气体（如NO₂、CO）的遥感反演中，提升异质地表下的气体柱浓度反演精度；(3) 结合高光谱传感器（如PRISMA、EnMAP）的多波段信息进一步优化MBMP模型的分波段选择策略；(4) 将半自动羽流分割流程与深度学习分割网络（如U-Net）结合，提高复杂背景下的羽流自动化提取能力。

Abstract (英文): Methane (CH4) is the second most significant greenhouse gas after carbon dioxide (CO2). Due to its high short-term global warming potential and the feasibility of emission abatement, monitoring methane point-source emissions has become a critical strategy for mitigating climate change. To address existing technical bottlenecks associated with spatial coverage limitations and surface-induced signal interference in satellite-based monitoring, this study proposes an integrated methane monitoring framework termed Multi-Band Multi-Constraint (MBMC) using Sentinel-2 MSI imagery. The MBMC framework combines a Low-Reflectance Artifact Detection (LRAD) algorithm, a Multi-Band Multi-Pass (MBMP) differential absorption retrieval model, and Integrated Mass Enhancement (IME)-based emission quantification. The LRAD module effectively suppresses artifacts caused by low-reflectance surfaces and heterogeneous backgrounds, thereby improving the signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) and retrieval accuracy of methane column enhancements. In addition, a semi-automatic plume segmentation workflow integrating morphological operations with a spatial database is developed to improve methane plume extraction and source localization. The framework was validated using data from single-blind controlled methane release experiments conducted in Arizona, USA. Results show that the proposed method achieved a mean absolute percentage error (MAPE) of 21.6% for emission rates ranging from 0.5 to 3.0 t/h, demonstrating promising performance for Sentinel-2-based screening and quantification of methane point sources, particularly for emissions above approximately 0.5 t/h under favorable observation conditions. The framework was further applied to Sentinel-2 observations over a natural gas field in Northwest China, where multiple methane point sources associated with gas gathering stations were successfully identified and quantified. The proposed framework provides a practical approach for high-resolution and high-frequency satellite monitoring of methane point sources and supports the refinement of methane emission inventories and mitigation strategies in the oil and gas sector.

### [252] [The Impact of Dynamic Observation Error and Hydrometeor Control Variables on GK-2A AMI All-Sky Radiance Assimilation](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132246)
*Seo-Youn Jo,Ki‐Hong Min*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 动态观测误差在全天空辐射率同化中，尤其是结合固态水凝物控制变量时，能显著改善云分析、热力场和降水预报，优于传统常值误差方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全天空辐射率同化直接更新水凝物场会引入较大不确定性，而观测误差的合理设定对同化效果至关重要。本研究旨在探究动态观测误差在不同水凝物控制变量配置下对分析和降水预报的影响。

Method: 采用五次多项式模型，将观测误差表示为云影响参数的函数，实现时空变化的场景依赖误差；对比不同水凝物控制变量配置（含/不含固态水凝物）下动态误差与常值误差的同化效果。

Result: 动态观测误差整体上改善了云分析和相关热力场；常值误差在强云区会过度加权观测从而降低分析质量；当HCV包含固态水凝物时动态误差优势更明显；动态误差+固态水凝物直接更新组合产生最真实的亮温/反射率分析和最优降水预报改进。

Conclusion: 在全天空辐射率同化中，云依赖的观测误差建模至关重要，尤其是使用固态水凝物控制变量时，应采用动态误差策略以提升同化质量。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该研究的动态观测误差建模方法可直接迁移至遥感反演与数据同化领域。(1) 将云影响参数驱动的误差模型应用于卫星遥感云属性反演（如MODIS、VIIRS），替代传统固定误差假设；(2) 在遥感降水反演中引入场景依赖误差，改善强对流云降水估计；(3) 为国产卫星（FY-4A/B）全天空辐射率同化提供云依赖误差参数化方案；(4) 将动态误差思路扩展到气溶胶、海冰等其他遥感参数的同化中。

Abstract (英文): Assimilation of all-sky radiance (ASR) observations informs atmospheric states and cloud distributions; however, it does not always lead to improved analyses or forecasts. In particular, directly updating hydrometeor fields introduces substantial uncertainty into ASR assimilation. This study examines the impact of dynamic observation errors on analyses and precipitation forecasts under different hydrometeor control variable (HCV) configurations. Observation errors are prescribed using a fifth-order polynomial model as a function of a cloud impact parameter, allowing spatiotemporally varying (i.e., scene-dependent) errors that adapt to cloud conditions. Results indicate that dynamic observation errors generally improve cloud analyses and associated thermodynamic fields. By contrast, constant errors tend to overweight ASR observations in heavily cloud-affected regions, thereby degrading analysis quality. The advantages of dynamic errors are more pronounced when solid-phase hydrometeors are included in the HCV, as these strongly influence brightness temperature (BT) analysis and the representation of convective cloud tops. Among all experiments, those combining dynamic errors with direct updates of solid-phase hydrometeors produce the most realistic BT and reflectivity analyses, as well as the greatest improvements in precipitation forecasts. These results underscore the importance of cloud-dependent observation error modeling in ASR assimilation, particularly when solid-phase HCVs are employed.

### [253] [GHF-DETR: An Improved DETR Framework with a Multi-Path Backbone and Dual-Domain Downsampling for UAV Object Detection](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132239)
*Lei Hu,Qingming Huang,Zhixiang Liu,Hongwei Ye*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出GHF-DETR，一种基于Transformer的无人机小目标检测器，通过异构多路径卷积网络（HMC）骨干、动态多尺度聚焦（DMSF）模块和高频选择性保留（HSP）下采样模块协同设计，在VisDrone2019上以15.4 GFLOPs和7.59 M参数实现33.1% mAP@0.5，较DFINE-n提升5.4%，并在NWPU VHR-10上验证了泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无人机图像中小目标存在像素覆盖率低、背景复杂、下采样过程中信息丢失等问题，现有检测器缺乏增强弱目标信号的显式机制。

Method: 1) HMC骨干网络：采用部分卷积（partial convolution）和门控线性单元（GLU）减少计算冗余并保持小目标特征判别性；2) DMSF模块：结合学习偏移对齐（learned offset alignment）与多核深度可分离卷积实现跨尺度特征融合；3) HSP下采样模块：将空间到深度卷积（space-to-depth convolution）与二维离散小波变换（2D DWT）相结合，在空间域和频率域补偿信息损失。

Result: VisDrone2019上mAP@0.5达33.1%，mAP@0.5:0.95达18.6%，AP_S达10.1%；计算量15.4 GFLOPs，参数量7.59 M；较DFINE-n基线分别提升5.4%和3.1%。

Conclusion: GHF-DETR在无人机小目标检测任务上实现了良好的精度-效率平衡，且具有跨数据集泛化能力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：1) HMC骨干中的部分卷积与GLU组合可直接迁移至遥感卫星图像中的小目标（如车辆、船只）检测，减少遥感大场景下计算冗余；2) DMSF模块的跨尺度融合策略可扩展至遥感多分辨率数据（如多光谱与全色融合）的特征对齐与增强；3) HSP中2D DWT与空间到深度卷积的结合可推广至遥感图像超分辨率重建或去云去雾预处理，从频域保留高频边缘信息；4) 建议在遥感场景下引入地理先验或地物分类语义信息辅助DMSF的偏移对齐，进一步提升复杂地表背景下的小目标检测性能。

Abstract (英文): Detecting small targets in Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV) imagery is challenging due to low pixel coverage, complex backgrounds, and information loss during downsampling. Existing detectors lack explicit mechanisms for enhancing weak target signals. We propose GHF-DETR, a Transformer-based detector featuring three collaboratively designed modules. First, a Heterogeneous Multi-Path Convolutional Network (HMC) backbone uses partial convolution and gated linear units to reduce computational redundancy while maintaining discrimination of small-object features. Second, a Dynamic Multi-Scale Focusing (DMSF) module integrates learned offset alignment with multi-kernel depthwise convolutions for cross-scale feature fusion. Third, a High-Frequency Selective Preservation (HSP) downsampling module combines space-to-depth convolution with 2D Discrete Wavelet Transform (DWT) to compensate for information loss in both spatial and frequency domains. On VisDrone2019, GHF-DETR achieves 33.1% mAP@0.5 and 18.6% mAP@0.5:0.95 with 15.4 GFLOPs and 7.59 M parameters, improving over the DFINE-n baseline by 5.4% and 3.1%, respectively, with AP_S reaching 10.1%. Generalization is validated on NWPU VHR-10. These results demonstrate that GHF-DETR achieves a favorable accuracy–efficiency balance for efficient UAV small-object detection.

</details>
