### [254] [Live fuel moisture mapping in unburned chaparral areas of Southern California with MODIS and VIIRS](https://doi.org/10.1016/j.rse.2026.115546)
*Yanni Zhan,S. Peterson,Dar A. Roberts,Charles Jones,Alan T. Murray*

Main category: RSE

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个基于MODIS和VIIRS卫星数据的框架，用于南加州灌木丛活燃料湿度（LFM）监测。研究发现随机森林模型在全数据集上精度更高，但多元线性回归在空间迁移性上更稳定；MODIS总体优于VIIRS，而M波段配置的VIIRS表现最佳。研究还将框架扩展到近实时应用，并确定了85-90%为最佳火灾风险阈值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 野外实测LFM数据稀疏且难以获取空间连续信息，同时MODIS向VIIRS的传感器过渡需要评估长期LFM监测的连续性，现有模型存在空间迁移性差的问题。

Method: 利用2003-2022年Globe-LFMC 2.0数据集，对比MODIS多元线性回归与随机森林模型，进行偏差校正后迁移至VIIRS评估跨传感器连续性，并集成类比年份物候估计和基于生存分析的干枯时间估计实现近实时应用。

Result: MODIS随机森林全数据集精度高但空间交叉验证下性能显著下降；多元线性回归在全数据集（R²=0.63, RMSE=12.35%）与空间交叉验证（R²=0.58, RMSE=12.43%）间表现稳定，空间迁移性更强。MODIS整体优于VIIRS，VIIRS的M波段配置效果最佳。独立验证表明85-90% LFM阈值能最平衡地分类高风险条件。

Conclusion: 可解释的、物候信息引导的卫星框架能够支持空间可迁移且时间一致的灌木丛LFM监测，用于火灾风险评估。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。改进方案：（1）引入多源遥感数据（如Sentinel-1 SAR、Landsat热红外）增强对低LFM和火灾扰动区域的捕捉能力；（2）探索深度学习模型（如CNN-LSTM）结合空间注意力机制提升空间迁移性；（3）将框架迁移至国产卫星（如高分系列、风云系列）以构建自主火灾监测体系；（4）引入数字高程模型（DEM）和地形因子修正局地微气候对LFM的影响；（5）扩展至更多植被类型（如草原、针叶林）评估框架泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): Live fuel moisture (LFM) is a critical determinant of wildfire behavior, especially in Southern California chaparral, yet spatially continuous and near-real-time estimates remain limited by sparse field measurements, and spatial transferability challenges. In addition, the transition from MODIS to VIIRS requires evaluation of the continuity of long-term satellite-based LFM monitoring. This study developed a framework using 2003–2022 Globe-LFMC 2.0 dataset that first compared MODIS-based multiple linear regression and random forest models, then applied bias correction, and transferred the framework to VIIRS to assess cross-sensor continuity. This framework was further extended for near-real-time application by integrating analog-year phenology estimation and survival-based dry-down timing estimation. For MODIS, random forest achieved higher accuracy with the full dataset, but its performance declined substantially under leave-one-county-out spatial cross-validation and showed reduced ability to capture low and fire-disturbed LFM values. Multiple linear regression showed more stable performance between full-dataset evaluation (R 2 = 0.63, RMSE = 12.35%) and spatial cross-validation (R 2 = 0.58, RMSE = 12.43%), indicating greater spatial transferability. MODIS models provided higher predictive skill overall than VIIRS, whereas the M-band-only VIIRS configuration produced the highest VIIRS performance and reproduced major seasonal and spatial LFM patterns. Independent validation using 2023–2024 Fire Environment Mapping System (FEMS) dataset showed that LFM thresholds of 85–90% provided the most balanced classification of elevated-risk conditions for both MODIS and VIIRS. This study shows that an interpretable, phenology-informed satellite framework can support spatially transferable and temporally consistent LFM monitoring for chaparral fire risk assessment.

</details>

### [257] [A unified kernel-driven modeling framework adapted to continuous, discrete and row-planted canopies in the thermal infrared domain](https://doi.org/10.1016/j.rse.2026.115548)
*Biao Cao,Yingjie Wang,Jean‐Philippe Gastellu‐Etchegorry*

Main category: RSE

TL;DR: 本文针对行播作物和果园的热红外辐射角度效应，提出了一种统一的核驱动建模框架，包含各向同性核、基础形状核、热点核和热条带核，通过两个实例化模型（Kimes-RL-Ganis和Kimes-Chen-Ganis）实现了对行播冠层的角度归一化，在模拟和实测数据上均显著优于现有模型，RMSE降低最高达84.9%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 行播作物和果园的热辐射观测存在角度依赖性，现有核驱动模型均针对离散或连续冠层设计，未考虑行播结构的特殊构型，难以准确归一化地表温度，影响水分管理和产量预测。

Method: 提出统一核驱动建模框架，包含各向同性核、基础形状核（表征行结构基础角度效应）、热点核（表征热点效应）和热条带核（表征条带状行结构的额外角度效应）；基于该框架构建两个实例化模型（Kimes-RL-Ganis和Kimes-Chen-Ganis）；采用三个DART模拟数据集和三个机载实测多角度数据集，与六种现有模型（Vinnikov、RL、Vinnikov-RL、Vinnikov-Chen、LSF-RL、LSF-Chen）进行对比验证。

Result: 模拟场景中RMSE从1.105–2.047 K降至0.265–0.349 K，降幅71.0–84.9%；实测场景中RMSE从1.316–2.227 K降至0.614–0.909 K，降幅42.5–61.2%。新模型对连续和离散冠层均表现出良好适应性。

Conclusion: 所提核驱动框架有效扩展了行播冠层的热红外角度归一化能力，显著优于现有模型，同时适用于连续和离散冠层，为不同植被类型的地表温度角度归一化提供了新方案，并具备向光学波段BRDF模拟推广的潜力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是热红外遥感角度归一化的核心研究。改进方向：（1）将热条带核引入光学波段BRDF模型，实现对行播作物的双向反射率角度归一化；（2）结合无人机多角度热红外数据验证模型在实际农业管理场景的适用性；（3）进一步考虑行间距、行向与太阳主平面夹角等参数对核函数进行物理约束，减少过拟合风险；（4）将框架扩展至非直行排列的果园（如等高种植、梯田），构建更通用的行结构核驱动模型。

Abstract (英文): To make better use of solar energy, many crops and orchards are planted in rows around the world. Accurate monitoring of the heat radiation status of row-planted crops and orchards is important for water management and yield forecasting. However, the radiation observed by a sensor is generally angle-dependent due to the complex architecture of the canopy, which must be normalized with respect to a reference direction (e.g., the nadir direction). Compared to physical models with numerous input parameters about the canopy structure and thermal property (e.g. canopy height, leaf area index, leaf emissivity and leaf temperature), semi-empirical kernel-driven models are much easier to be calibrated using only multi-angle sensor observations. However, all existing kernel-driven models have been developed for discrete and continuous canopies, without considering the specific architecture of row structure. To extend the fitting ability to row-planted canopies, a unified kernel-driven modeling framework in the thermal infrared domain has been developed in this study. It includes an isotropic kernel, a base shape kernel, a hotspot kernel and a hot belt kernel. Both base shape and hot belt kernels can represent the angular effect of row structure. Two instantiated models (i.e., Kimes-RL-Ganis and Kimes-Chen-Ganis) are proposed within this unified framework. Then, three DART (Discrete Anisotropic Radiative Transfer)-simulated datasets and three airborne-measured multi-angle datasets have been adopted to evaluate our two new models against six existing models (i.e., Vinnikov, RL, Vinnikov-RL, Vinnikov-Chen, LSF-RL and LSF-Chen). Results show RMSE reduction percentages as large as 71.0–84.9% for the three simulated scenes (1.322–1.445 K to 0.300–0.349 K, 1.105–1.263 K to 0.265–0.321 K, and 1.926–2.047 K to 0.269–0.291 K) and 42.5–61.2% for the three measured scenes (2.043–2.227 K to 0.78–0.792 K, 1.316–1.426 K to 0.614–0.649 K, and 1.580–1.654 K to 0.882–0.909 K). Given the demonstrated adaptability of these new models to both continuous and discrete canopies, they offer significant potential for advancing angular normalization of land surface temperature across diverse vegetation types in applications. This framework is well suited for the bi-directional reflectance distribution function simulation over row-planted scenes in the optical domain.

</details>
